 tataḥ pāñcālarājasya sutā cāpi jagāma ha
a tataḥ sā nartanāgāre dhanaṃjayam apaśyata
c rājñaḥ kanyā virāṭasya nartayānaṃ mahābhujam
a tatas tā nartanāgārād viniṣkramya sahārjunāḥ
c kanyā dadṛśur āyāntīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kliṣṭām anāgasam
 kanyā ūcuḥ
a diṣṭyā sairandhri muktāsi diṣṭyāsi punarāgatā
c diṣṭyā vinihatāḥ sūtā ye tvāṃ kliśyanty anāgasam
 bṛhannaḍovāca
a kathaṃ sairandhri muktāsi kathaṃ pāpāś ca te hatāḥ
c icchāmi vai tava śrotuṃ sarvam eva yathātatham
 sairandhry uvāca
a bṛhannaḍe kiṃ nu tava sairandhryā kāryam adya vai
c yā tvaṃ vasasi kalyāṇi sadā kanyāpure sukham
a na hi duḥkhaṃ samāpnoṣi sairandhrī yad upāśnute
b sukhena vartase yeha na tad duḥkham avāpyate
c tena māṃ duḥkhitām evaṃ pṛcchase prahasann iva
 bṛhannaḍovāca
a bṛhannaḍāpi kalyāṇi duḥkham āpnoty anuttamam
c tiryagyonigatā bāle na cainām avabudhyase
d tvayā sahoṣitā cāsmi tvaṃ ca sarvaiḥ sahoṣitā
d kliśyantyāṃ tvayi suśroṇi ko nu duḥkhaṃ na cintayet
d na tu kena cid atyantaṃ kasya cid dhṛdayaṃ kva cit
d vedituṃ śakyate nūnaṃ tena māṃ nāvabudhyase
d tvattaḥ kṛcchrataraṃ vāsaṃ vaseyam aham aṅgane
d kasya vai hṛdayaṃ kena vedituṃ pariśakyate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ sahaiva kanyābhir draupadī rājaveśma tat
c praviveśa sudeṣṇāyāḥ samīpam apalāyinī
a tām abravīd rājaputrī virāṭavacanād idam
c sairandhri gamyatāṃ śīghraṃ yatra kāmayase gatim
a rājā bibheti bhadraṃ te gandharvebhyaḥ parābhavāt
c tvaṃ cāpi taruṇī subhru rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi
d puṃsām iṣṭaś ca viṣayo gandharvāś cātikopanāḥ
d cittāni ca nṛṇāṃ śubhre raktāni sparśaje sukhe
d tasmāt tvatto bhayaṃ mahyaṃ rāṣṭrasya nagarasya ca
d gacchādyaiva yatheṣṭaṃ tvaṃ nagarād yatra raṃsyase
d tvannimittaṃ śubhe mahyaṃ sarve bandhujanā hatāḥ
d nṛśaṃsā khalu te buddhir bhrātṝṇāṃ me kṛto vadhaḥ
d tasmād gandharvarājebhyo bhayam adya pravartate
d yatheṣṭaṃ gaccha sairandhri iha svasti yathā bhavet
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d sudeṣṇāvacanaṃ śrutvā sairandhrī cedam abravīt
 sairandhry uvāca
a trayodaśāhamātraṃ me rājā kṣamatu bhāmini
c kṛtakṛtyā bhaviṣyanti gandharvās te na saṃśayaḥ
a tato māṃ te 'paneṣyanti kariṣyanti ca te priyam
c dhruvaṃ ca śreyasā rājā yokṣyate saha bāndhavaiḥ
d evam uktātha kaikeyī nṛpāyoktvā parāmṛśat
d pūrṇakāmā kṛtā kṛṣṇā vāyuputreṇa cāvasat
d rājñā kṛtopakārāś ca kṛtajñāś ca sadā śubhe
d sādhavaś ca balotsiktāḥ kṛtapratikṛtepsavaḥ
d arthinī prabravīmy eṣā yadvā tadveti cintaya
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d bharasva tad aharmātraṃ tat te śreyo bhaviṣyati
d tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā kaikeyī duḥkhamohitā
d uvāca draupadīm ārtā bhrātṛvyasanakarśitā
d vasa bhadre yatheṣṭaṃ tvaṃ tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā
d trāyasva mama bhartāraṃ putrāṃś caiva viśeṣataḥ
 iti pāṇḍavanigūḍhavāsasaṃvatsaracaritam abhidhāya pārāśaryaḥ
 kīcakavadhāntaṃ yatra trayodaśāham ajñāna
taśeṣavāsanivṛttaye
 kurupatikāryānusaṃdhānāya dūrānveṣitaphalāvāptaye hi suyodhanādīnāṃ
 cārapratyācāram abhidhātum āha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 kīcake tu hate rājā virāṭaḥ paravīrahā
 śokam āhārayat tīvraṃ sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ
a kīcakasya tu ghātena sānujasya viśāṃ pate
c atyāhitaṃ cintayitvā vyasmayanta pṛthagjanāḥ
a tasmin pure janapade saṃjalpo 'bhūc ca sarvaśaḥ
c śauryād dhi vallabho rājño mahāsattvaś ca kīcakaḥ
d sāṃparāye parikruṣṭo balavān durjayo raṇe
a āsīt prahartā ca nṛṇāṃ dārāmarśī ca durmatiḥ
c sa hataḥ khalu pāpātmā gandharvair duṣṭapūruṣaḥ
a ity ajalpan mahārāja parānīkaviśātanam
c deśe deśe manuṣyāś ca kīcakaṃ duṣpradharṣaṇam
a atha vai dhārtarāṣṭreṇa prayuktā ye bahiścarāḥ
c mṛgayitvā bahūn grāmān rāṣṭrāṇi nagarāṇi ca
a saṃvidhāya yathādiṣṭaṃ yathādeśapradarśanam
c kṛtacintā nyavartanta te ca nāgapuraṃ prati
d āgamya hāstinapuraṃ dhārtarāṣṭram ariṃdamam
a tatra dṛṣṭvā tu rājānaṃ kauravyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrajam
b praṇamya śirasā bhūmau vardhayitvā jayāśiṣā
b āsīnaṃ sūryasaṃkāśe kāñcane paramāsane
b upāsyamānaṃ sacivair marudbhir iva vāsavam
c droṇakarṇakṛpaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhīṣmeṇa ca mahātmanā
d vidvadbhir gāyakaiḥ sārdhaṃ kavibhiḥ stutipāṭhakaiḥ
d anekair api rājanyaiḥ sevitaṃ saparicchadaiḥ
a saṃgataṃ bhrātṛbhiś cāpi trigartaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
c duryodhanaṃ sabhāmadhye āsīnam idam abruvan
a kṛto 'smābhiḥ paro yatnas teṣām anveṣaṇe sadā
c pāṇḍavānāṃ manuṣyendra tasmin mahati kānane
a nirjane mṛgasaṃkīrṇe nānādrumalatāvṛte
c latāpratānabahule nānāgulmasamāvṛte
a na ca vidmo gatā yena pārthāḥ syur dṛḍhavikramāḥ
c mārgamāṇāḥ padanyāsaṃ teṣu teṣu tathā tathā
a girikūṭeṣu tuṅgeṣu nānājanapadeṣu ca
c janākīrṇeṣu deśeṣu kharvaṭeṣu pureṣu ca
a narendra bahuśo 'nviṣṭā naiva vidmaś ca pāṇḍavān
c atyantabhāvaṃ naṣṭās te bhadraṃ tubhyaṃ nararṣabha
d girīṇāṃ kūṭakuñjeṣu kandarāntarasānuṣu
d nadīprasravaṇeṣv eva hradeṣu ca saraḥsu ca
d gahvareṣu ca durgeṣu grāmeṣūpavaneṣu ca
d durvijñeyā gatis teṣāṃ mṛgyante 'smābhir eva hi
d gajavyālasamīpeṣu siṃhānte śarabhāntare
a vartmāny anviṣyamāṇās tu rathānāṃ rathasattama
b na hi vidmo gatiṃ teṣāṃ vāsaṃ hi narasattama
c kaṃ cit kālaṃ manuṣyendra sūtānām anugā vayam
a mṛgayitvā yathānyāyaṃ viditārthāḥ sma tattvataḥ
c prāptā dvāravatīṃ sūtā ṛte pārthaiḥ paraṃtapa
d santītare janapadā ye pārthān veṣibhir nṛpa
d pravicitās te hy asmābhiḥ pṛthivīmaṇḍale 'khile
a na tatra pāṇḍavā rājan nāpi kṛṣṇā pativratā
b naradeva yathoddiṣṭaṃ naiva vidma ca pāṇḍavān
b nirvṛto bhava naṣṭās te svastho bhava paraṃtapa
c sarvathā vipranaṣṭās te namas te bharatarṣabha
a na hi vidmo gatiṃ teṣāṃ vāsaṃ vāpi mahātmanām
c pāṇḍavānāṃ pravṛttiṃ vā vidmaḥ karmāpi vā kṛtam
d sarvā ca pṛthivī kṛtsnā saśailavanakānanā
d sarāṣṭranagaragrāmā pattanaiś ca samanvitā
d anveṣitā ca tatsarvaṃ na ca paśyāma pāṇḍavān
e sa naḥ śādhi manuṣyendra ata ūrdhvaṃ viśāṃ pate
a anveṣaṇe pāṇḍavānāṃ bhūyaḥ kiṃ karavāmahe
c imāṃ ca naḥ priyām īkṣa vācaṃ bhadravatīṃ śubhām
a yena trigartā nikṛtā balena mahatā nṛpa
c sūtena rājño matsyasya kīcakena mahātmanā
a sa hataḥ patitaḥ śete gandharvair niśi bhārata
b syālo rājño virāṭasya senāpatir udāradhīḥ
b sudeṣṇāyā mahāñ jyeṣṭhaḥ śūro vīro gatavyathaḥ
b utsāhavān mahāvīryo nītimān balavān api
b yuddhajño ripuvīraghnaḥ siṃhatulyaparākramaḥ
b prajārakṣaṇadakṣaś ca śatrugrahaṇaśaktimān
b vijitārir mahāyuddhe pracaṇḍo mānatatparaḥ
b naranārīmanohlādī dhīro vāgmī raṇapriyaḥ
b puṇyadharmārthakāmānāṃ bhājanaṃ manujottamaḥ
b sa hato niśi gandharvaiḥ strīnimittaṃ narādhipa
b gandharvāṇāṃ ca mahiṣī kā cid asti nitambinī
b sairandhrī nāma tāṃ dṛpto duṣṭātmākāmayad balī
c adṛśyamānair duṣṭātmā saha bhrātṛbhir acyuta
d suhṛdāś cātra nihatā yodhāś ca pravarā hatāḥ
d ity evaṃ śrutam asmābhir gandharvair nihato niśi
d bāndhavair bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ kīcako nihato 'bhavat
d adya prabhṛti rājendra pāṇḍavānveṣaṇaṃ prati
d cārāṃs tān sarvataś cartuṃ preṣayeti matir hi naḥ
d nihato niśi gandharvair duṣṭātmā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a priyam etad upaśrutya śatrūṇāṃ tu parābhavam
b etāvac chrutam asmābhir bhadraṃ te 'stu narādhipa
c kṛtakṛtyaś ca kauravya vidhatsva yad anantaram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato duryodhano rājā śrutvā teṣāṃ vacas tadā
c ciram antarmanā bhūtvā pratyuvāca sabhāsadaḥ
d jānann api mahārāja saśalyenāntarātmanā
d kīcakasya vadhaṃ śrutvā na cākāram adarśayat
d kevalaṃ śauryam ālambya gatasattva iva śvasan
d bhūyaḥ pratyāgataprāṇo dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajo balī
d śrutvā teṣāṃ vacas tāvac cintayām āsa kauravaḥ
a suduḥkhā khalu kāryāṇāṃ gatir vijñātum antataḥ
c tasmāt sarve udīkṣadhvaṃ kva nu syuḥ pāṇḍavā gatāḥ
a alpāvaśiṣṭaṃ kālasya gatabhūyiṣṭham antataḥ
c teṣām ajñātacaryāyām asmin varṣe trayodaśe
a asya varṣasya śeṣaṃ ced vyatīyur iha pāṇḍavāḥ
c nivṛttasamayās te hi satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ
a kṣaranta iva nāgendrāḥ sarva āśīviṣopamāḥ
c duḥkhā bhaveyuḥ saṃrabdhāḥ kauravān prati te dhruvam
d vijñātavyā manuṣyendrās tarkayā supraṇītayā
d nipuṇaiś cārapuruṣaiḥ prājñair dakṣaiḥ susaṃvṛtaiḥ
a arvāk kālasya vijñātāḥ kṛcchrarūpadharāḥ punaḥ
c praviśeyur jitakrodhās tāvad eva punar vanam
a tasmāt kṣipraṃ bubhutsadhvaṃ yathā no 'tyantam avyayam
c rājyaṃ nirdvandvam avyagraṃ niḥsapatnaṃ ciraṃ bhavet
a athābravīt tataḥ karṇaḥ kṣipraṃ gacchantu bhārata
a satyadharmārthasaṃyutam
a karṇaḥ
a ete punar na gacchantu
c anye dhūrtatarā dakṣā nibhṛtāḥ sādhukāriṇaḥ
d duryodhanenaivam ukte vacane 'tīva duḥkhinā
a carantu deśān saṃvītāḥ sphītāñ janapadākulān
c tatra goṣṭhīṣv athānyāsu siddhapravrajiteṣu ca
d paricāreṣu tīrtheṣu grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca
a paricāreṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣv ākareṣu ca
c vijñātavyā manuṣyais tais tarkayā suvinītayā
a vividhais tatparaiḥ samyak tajjñair nipuṇasaṃvṛtaiḥ
c anveṣṭavyāś ca nipuṇaṃ pāṇḍavāś channavāsinaḥ
a nadīkuñjeṣu tīrtheṣu grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca
c āśrameṣu ca ramyeṣu parvateṣu guhāsu ca
a athāgrajānantarajaḥ pāpabhāvānurāgiṇam
c jyeṣṭhaṃ duḥśāsanas tatra bhrātā bhrātaram abravīt
d yeṣu naḥ pratyayo rājaṃś cāreṣu manujādhipa
d te yāntu dattadeyā vai bhūyas tān parimārgitum
d tān ahaṃ preṣayiṣyāmi yatanto dṛḍhabhaktayaḥ
d etan mataṃ mahārāja madīyaṃ priyadarśana
d apare tatra gacchantu carāḥ pracchannacāriṇaḥ
a etac ca karṇo yat prāha sarvam īkṣāmahe tathā
b ghrāṇaiḥ paśyanti paśavo vedaiḥ paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥ
b cāraiḥ paśyanti rājānaś cakṣurbhyām itare janāḥ
c yathoddiṣṭaṃ carāḥ sarve mṛgayantu tatas tataḥ
e ete cānye ca bhūyāṃso deśād deśaṃ yathāvidhi
a na tu teṣāṃ gatir vāsaḥ pravṛttiś copalabhyate
c atyāhitaṃ vā gūḍhās te pāraṃ vormimato gatāḥ
d pratyāhartuṃ ca mūḍhās te pathi nāśam ato gatāḥ
a vyālair vāpi mahāraṇye bhakṣitāḥ śūramāninaḥ
b dvīpaṃ vā paramaṃ prāptā giridurgaṃ vanāni vā
b hīnadarpā nirāśās te bhakṣitā vāpi rākṣasaiḥ
c atha vā viṣamaṃ prāpya vinaṣṭāḥ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
a tasmān mānasam avyagraṃ kṛtvā tvaṃ kurunandana
c kuru kāryaṃ yathotsāhaṃ manyase yan narādhipa
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a athābravīn mahāvīryo droṇas tattvārthadarśivān
c na tādṛśā vinaśyanti nāpi yānti parābhavam
a śūrāś ca kṛtavidyāś ca buddhimanto jitendriyāḥ
c dharmajñāś ca kṛtajñāś ca dharmarājam anuvratāḥ
a nītidharmārthatattvajñaṃ pitṛvac ca samāhitam
c dharme sthitaṃ satyadhṛtiṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ jyeṣṭhāpacāyinam
a anuvratā mahātmānaṃ bhrātaraṃ bhrātaro nṛpa
c ajātaśatruṃ hrīmantaṃ taṃ ca bhrātṝn anuvratam
a teṣāṃ tathā vidheyānāṃ nibhṛtānāṃ mahātmanām
c kimarthaṃ nītimān pārthaḥ śreyo naiṣāṃ kariṣyati
a tasmād yatnāt pratīkṣante kālasyodayam āgatam
c na hi te nāśam ṛccheyur iti paśyāmy ahaṃ dhiyā
a sāṃprataṃ caiva yat kāryaṃ tac ca kṣipram akālikam
c kriyatāṃ sādhu saṃcintya vāsaś caiṣāṃ pracintyatām
d tathābhivādinaṃ matsyaṃ kauraveyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak
d ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥ
d pratinandāma te vākyaṃ sarva eva viśāṃ pate
a yathāvat pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ sarvārtheṣu dhṛtātmanām
b pravṛttir upalabhyeta tathā nītir vidhīyatām
b sarvopāyair yatasva tvaṃ yathā paśyasi pāṇḍavān
c durjñeyāḥ khalu śūrās te apāpās tapasā vṛtāḥ
a śuddhātmā guṇavān pārthaḥ satyavān nītimāñ śuciḥ
c tejorāśir asaṃkhyeyo gṛhṇīyād api cakṣuṣī
a vijñāya kriyatāṃ tasmād bhūyaś ca mṛgayāmahe
c brāhmaṇaiś cārakaiḥ siddhair ye cānye tadvido janāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥ
c śrutavān deśakālajñas tattvajñaḥ sarvadharmavit
a ācāryavākyoparame tad vākyam abhisaṃdadhat
c hitārthaṃ sa uvācemāṃ bhāratīṃ bhāratān prati
a yudhiṣṭhire samāsaktāṃ dharmajñe dharmasaṃśritām
b pāṇḍave nityam avyagrāṃ giraṃ bhīṣmaḥ samādade
c asatsu durlabhāṃ nityaṃ satāṃ cābhimatāṃ sadā
e bhīṣmaḥ samavadat tatra giraṃ sādhubhir arcitām
a yathaiṣa brāhmaṇaḥ prāha droṇaḥ sarvārthatattvavit
b tad vākyam abhinandāmi na me 'sty atra vicāraṇā
b niḥsaṃśayaṃ tathaivaitad bhūyaś caināṃ vibodhata
c sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā nāśaṃ nārhanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a śrutavṛttopasaṃpannāḥ sādhuvratasamanvitāḥ
c vṛddhānuśāsane magnāḥ satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ
a samayaṃ samayajñās te pālayantaḥ śucivratāḥ
c nāvasīditum arhanti udvahantaḥ satāṃ dhuram
d kṣatradharmaratā nityaṃ keśavānugatāḥ sadā
d pravīrapuruṣās te vai mahātmāno mahābalāḥ
a dharmataś caiva guptās te svavīryeṇa ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c na nāśam adhigaccheyur iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a tatra buddhiṃ praṇeṣyāmi pāṇḍavān prati bhārata
c na tu nītiḥ sunītasya śakyate 'nveṣituṃ paraiḥ
a yat tu śakyam ihāsmābhis tān vai saṃcintya pāṇḍavān
c buddhyā pravaktuṃ na drohāt pravakṣyāmi nibodha tat
d na tv iyaṃ mādṛśair nītis tasya vācyā kathaṃ cana
a sā tv iyaṃ sādhu vaktavyā na tv anītiḥ kathaṃ cana
c vṛddhānuśāsane tāta tiṣṭhataḥ satyaśīlinaḥ
d ayuktaṃ tu mayā vaktuṃ tulyā me kurupāṇḍavāḥ
d nivāsaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ saṃcintya ca vadāmy aham
d bahunā kiṃ pralāpena yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a avaśyaṃ tv iha dhīreṇa satāṃ madhye vivakṣatā
c yathāmati vivaktavyaṃ sarvaśo dharmalipsayā
a tatra nāhaṃ tathā manye yathāyam itaro janaḥ
b nivāsaṃ dharmarājasya varṣe 'smin vai trayodaśe
b tatra tāta na teṣāṃ hi rājñāṃ bhāvyam asāṃpratam
b nivāsaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ śṛṇuṣva manujādhipa
b bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito vīraiḥ kṛṣṇayā ca mahāyaśāḥ
b kimarthaṃ sa mahārājo nātmaśreyo bhaviṣyati
b pāṇḍavo nikṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ yathāvad viditaṃ tava
b kleśitaś ca pure nityaṃ rājyakāmaiś ca sāṃpratam
b channaś carati tasmāt sa prakṛtyā nītimān nṛpaḥ
b varṣam ekaṃ susaṃchannam uṣya vāsam anuttamam
b āyāti codaye kāle kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi pāṇḍavam
b sodaraiḥ sahitaṃ vīraṃ draupadyā ca paraṃtapa
b saṃvidhatsva mahābāho yathā na syāt sukhodayaḥ
b yasmin sa rājā vasatiś channaḥ sattvabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
b bhaviṣyanti narās tatra rāgamohavivarjitāḥ
b nādhayo hi mahārāja na vyādhiḥ kṣatriyarṣabha
c pure janapade vāpi yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dānaśīlo vadānyaś ca nibhṛto hrīniṣedhakaḥ
d jano janapade bhāvyo yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d priyavādī sadā dānto bhavyaḥ satyaparo janaḥ
d hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ śucir dakṣo yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a nāsūyako na cāpīrṣur nātivādī na matsarī
c bhaviṣyati janas tatra svaṃ svaṃ dharmam anuvrataḥ
a brahmaghoṣāś ca bhūyāṃsaḥ pūrṇāhutyas tathaiva ca
c kratavaś ca bhaviṣyanti bhūyāṃso bhūridakṣiṇāḥ
a sadā ca tatra parjanyaḥ samyag varṣī na saṃśayaḥ
c saṃpannasasyā ca mahī nirītīkā bhaviṣyati
a rasavanti ca dhānyāni guṇavanti phalāni ca
c gandhavanti ca mālyāni śubhaśabdā ca bhāratī
a vāyuś ca sukhasaṃsparśo niṣpratīpaṃ ca darśanam
b na rogās tatra vidyante vadhabandhā na santi ca
b na corā na hi dambhāś ca na ca bādhā bhavanti ca
b nāśaktā na ca duṣṭāś ca yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhayaṃ nābhyāviśet tatra yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a gāvaś ca bahulās tatra na kṛśā na ca durduhāḥ
c payāṃsi dadhisarpīṃṣi rasavanti hitāni ca
d salilāni prasannāni sarve bhāvāś ca śobhanāḥ
a guṇavanti ca pānāni bhojyāni rasavanti ca
c tatra deśe bhaviṣyanti yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a rasāḥ sparśāś ca gandhāś ca śabdāś cāpi guṇānvitāḥ
c dṛśyāni ca prasannāni yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d dharmāś ca tatra dṛśyante sevitāś ca dvijātibhiḥ
a svaiḥ svair guṇaiḥ susaṃyuktās tasmin varṣe trayodaśe
c deśe tasmin bhaviṣyanti tāta pāṇḍavasaṃyute
a saṃprītimāñ janas tatra saṃtuṣṭaḥ śucir avyayaḥ
c devatātithipūjāsu sarvabhūtānurāgavān
a iṣṭadāno mahotsāhaḥ śaśvad dharmaparāyaṇaḥ
c aśubhadviṭ śubhaprepsur nityayajñaḥ śubhavrataḥ
e bhaviṣyati janas tatra yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
f nityotsavapramudito nityahṛṣṭaḥ śriyā vṛtaḥ
f bhaviṣyati nivāso 'yaṃ yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tyaktavākyānṛtas tāta śubhakalyāṇamaṅgalaḥ
c śubhārthepsuḥ śubhamatir yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d sarvabhūtadayāyuktaḥ sadā nirmalamānasaḥ
d anirdiśyaḥ sa dharmātmā dvijair api hi bhārata
e bhaviṣyati janas tatra nityaṃ ceṣṭapriyavrataḥ
a dharmātmā sa tadādṛśyaḥ so 'pi tāta dvijātibhiḥ
c kiṃ punaḥ prākṛtaiḥ pārthaḥ śakyo vijñātum antataḥ
a yasmin satyaṃ dhṛtir dānaṃ parā śāntir dhruvā kṣamā
c hrīḥ śrīḥ kīrtiḥ paraṃ teja ānṛśaṃsyam athārjavam
a tasmāt tatra nivāsaṃ tu channaṃ satreṇa dhīmataḥ
c gatiṃ vā paramāṃ tasya notsahe vaktum anyathā
a evam etat tu saṃcintya yatkṛtaṃ manyase hitam
c tat kṣipraṃ kuru kauravya yady evaṃ śraddadhāsi me
d kulasya hi kṣamaṃ tāta yad ahaṃ tad bravīmi te
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śāradvato vākyam ity uvāca kṛpas tadā
c yuktaṃ prāptaṃ ca vṛddhena pāṇḍavān prati bhāṣitam
a dharmārthasahitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ tattvataś ca sahetumat
c tatrānurūpaṃ bhīṣmeṇa mamāpy atra giraṃ śṛṇu
a teṣāṃ caiva gatis tīrthair vāsaś caiṣāṃ pracintyatām
c nītir vidhīyatāṃ cāpi sāṃprataṃ yā hitā bhavet
a nāvajñeyo ripus tāta prākṛto 'pi bubhūṣatā
c kiṃ punaḥ pāṇḍavās tāta sarvāstrakuśalā raṇe
a tasmāt satraṃ praviṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
c gūḍhabhāveṣu channeṣu kāle codayam āgate
a svarāṣṭrapararāṣṭreṣu jñātavyaṃ balam ātmanaḥ
c udaye pāṇḍavānāṃ ca prāpte kāle na saṃśayaḥ
d nivāsaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ darśane mṛgayāmahe
a nivṛttasamayāḥ pārthā mahātmāno mahābalāḥ
c mahotsāhā bhaviṣyanti pāṇḍavā hy atitejasaḥ
a tasmād balaṃ ca kośaṃ ca nītiś cāpi vidhīyatām
c yathā kālodaye prāpte samyak taiḥ saṃdadhāmahe
a tāta manyāmi tat sarvaṃ budhyasva balam ātmanaḥ
c niyataṃ sarvamitreṣu balavatsv abaleṣu ca
a uccāvacaṃ balaṃ jñātvā madhyasthaṃ cāpi bhārata
c prahṛṣṭam aprahṛṣṭaṃ ca saṃdadhāma tathā paraiḥ
a sāmnā bhedena dānena daṇḍena balikarmaṇā
c nyāyenānamya ca parān balāc cānamya durbalān
a sāntvayitvā ca mitrāṇi balaṃ cābhāṣyatāṃ sukham
c sakośabalasaṃvṛddhaḥ samyak siddhim avāpsyasi
a yotsyase cāpi balibhir aribhiḥ pratyupasthitaiḥ
c anyais tvaṃ pāṇḍavair vāpi hīnasvabalavāhanaiḥ
a evaṃ sarvaṃ viniścitya vyavasāyaṃ svadharmataḥ
c yathākālaṃ manuṣyendra ciraṃ sukham avāpsyasi
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tato duryodhano vākyaṃ śrutvā teṣāṃ mahātmanām
d muhūrtam iva saṃcintya sacivān idam abravīt
d śrutaṃ hy etan mayā pūrvaṃ kathāsu janasaṃsadi
d dhīrāṇāṃ śāstraviduṣāṃ prājñānāṃ matiniścaye
d kṛtīnāṃ sāraphalgutve jānāmi nayacakṣuṣā
d sattve bāhubale dhairye prāṇe śārīrasaṃbhave
d sāṃprataṃ mānuṣe loke sadaityanararākṣase
d catvāras tu naravyāghrā bale śakropamā bhuvi
d uttamāḥ prāṇināṃ teṣāṃ nāsti kaś cid bale samaḥ
d samaprāṇabalā nityaṃ saṃpūrṇabalapauruṣāḥ
d baladevaś ca bhīmaś ca madrarājaś ca vīryavān
d caturthaḥ kīcakas teṣāṃ pañcamaṃ nānuśuśrumaḥ
d anyonyānantarabalāḥ parasparajayaiṣiṇaḥ
d bāhuyuddham abhīpsanto nityaṃ saṃrabdhamānasāḥ
d tenāham avagacchāmi pratyayena vṛkodaram
d manasy abhiniviṣṭaṃ me vyaktaṃ jīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ
d tatrāhaṃ kīcakaṃ manye bhīmasenena māritam
d sairandhrīṃ draupadīṃ manye nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d śaṅke kṛṣṇānimittaṃ tu bhīmasenena kīcakaḥ
d gandharvavyapadeśena hato niśi mahābalaḥ
d ko hi śakto 'paro bhīmāt kīcakaṃ hantum ojasā
d śastraṃ vinā bāhuvīryāt tathā sarvāṅgacūrṇitam
d mardituṃ vā tathā śīghraṃ carmamāṃsāsthicūrṇitam
d rūpam anyat samāsthāya bhīmasyaitad viceṣṭitam
d dhruvaṃ kṛṣṇānimittaṃ tu bhīmasenena sūtajaḥ
d gandharvavyapadeśena hato niśi na saṃśayaḥ
d pitāmahena ye coktā deśasya ca janasya ca
d guṇās te matsyarāṣṭreṣu bahuśo 'pi mayā śrutāḥ
d virāṭanagare manye pāṇḍavāś channacāriṇaḥ
d nivasanti pure ramye tatra yātrā vidhīyatām
d matsyarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyāmo grahīṣyāmaś ca godhanam
d gṛhīte godhane nūnaṃ te 'pi yotsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
d apūrṇe samaye cāpi yadi paśyāma pāṇḍavān
d dvādaśānyāni varṣāṇi pravekṣyanti punar vanam
d tasmād anyatareṇāpi lābho 'smākaṃ bhaviṣyati
d kośavṛddhir ihāsmākaṃ śatrūṇāṃ nidhanaṃ bhavet
d kathaṃ suyodhanaṃ gacched yudhiṣṭhirabhṛtaḥ purā
d etac cāpi vadaty eṣa mātsyaḥ paribhavān mayi
d tasmāt kartavyam etad vai tasmin yātrā vidhīyatām
d etat sunītaṃ manye 'haṃ sarveṣāṃ yadi rocate
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a atha rājā trigartānāṃ suśarmā rathayūthapaḥ
b pūrvam ābhāṣya karṇena tathā duḥśāsanena ca
c prāptakālam idaṃ vākyam uvāca tvarito bhṛśam
a asakṛn nikṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ matsyaiḥ sālveyakaiḥ saha
c sūtena caiva matsyasya kīcakena punaḥ punaḥ
a bādhito bandhubhiḥ sārdhaṃ balād balavatā vibho
c sa karṇam abhyudīkṣyātha duryodhanam abhāṣata
a asakṛn matsyarājñā me rāṣṭraṃ bādhitam ojasā
c praṇetā kīcakaś cāsya balavān abhavat purā
a krūro 'marṣī sa duṣṭātmā bhuvi prakhyātavikramaḥ
c nihatas tatra gandharvaiḥ pāpakarmā nṛśaṃsavān
a tasmiṃś ca nihate rājan hīnadarpo nirāśrayaḥ
c bhaviṣyati nirutsāho virāṭa iti me matiḥ
a tatra yātrā mama matā yadi te rocate 'nagha
c kauravāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ karṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ
a etat prāptam ahaṃ manye kāryam ātyayikaṃ hitam
c rāṣṭraṃ tasyābhiyātv āśu bahudhānyasamākulam
a ādadāmo 'sya ratnāni vividhāni vasūni ca
c grāmān rāṣṭrāṇi vā tasya hariṣyāmo vibhāgaśaḥ
a atha vā gosahasrāṇi bahūni ca śubhāni ca
b vidhamitvā hariṣyāmaḥ praviśya ca purād balam
c vividhāni hariṣyāmaḥ pratipīḍya puraṃ balāt
a kauravaiḥ saha saṃgamya trigartaiś ca viśāṃ pate
c gās tasyāpaharāmāśu saha sarvaiḥ susaṃhatāḥ
a saṃdhiṃ vā tena kṛtvā tu nibadhnīmo 'sya pauruṣam
c hatvā cāsya camūṃ kṛtsnāṃ vaśam anvānayāmahe
a taṃ vaśe nyāyataḥ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vatsyāmahe vayam
c bhavato balavṛddhiś ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya karṇo rājānam abravīt
c sūktaṃ suśarmaṇā vākyaṃ prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ ca naḥ
a tasmāt kṣipraṃ viniryāmo yojayitvā varūthinīm
b yady etat te 'bhirucitaṃ mama caitad dhi rocate
c vibhajya cāpy anīkāni yathā vā manyase 'nagha
a prajñāvān kuruvṛddho 'yaṃ sarveṣāṃ naḥ pitāmahaḥ
c ācāryaś ca tathā droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tathā
a manyante te yathā sarve tathā yātrā vidhīyatām
c saṃmantrya cāśu gacchāmaḥ sādhanārthaṃ mahīpateḥ
a kiṃ ca naḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ kāryaṃ hīnārthabalapauruṣaiḥ
c atyarthaṃ vā pranaṣṭās te prāptā vāpi yamakṣayam
d tad bhavāṃś caturaṅgeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
a yāmo rājann anudvignā virāṭaviṣayaṃ vayam
c ādāsyāmo hi gās tasya vividhāni vasūni ca
d duryodhana uvāca
d uktam etad vidheyaṃ vā vākyam uktaṃ tvayānagha
d yadaiva cāraiḥ prahitair ihāgamya niveditam
d nidhanaṃ sūtaputrasya kīcakasya balīyasaḥ
d tadaiva hi mahācintā hṛdi pāṇḍusutān prati
d kīcakaṃ balasaṃpannaṃ nānyo hantā vṛkodarāt
d nityam eva hi pārthānāṃ virāṭaḥ priyam icchati
d tasmiṃs te cāpi viśvastā nivāsāya sthitā dhruvam
d pitāmahena yac coktaṃ cihnaṃ pārthābhivedane
d tad dhi rājño virāṭasya śrūyate viṣaye kila
d tat tatra gatvā karṇāśu virāṭaṃ godhanaṃ vayam
d gṛhṇīmas tasya rāṣṭraṃ ca pramathya svabalair yutāḥ
d anuyāsyanti te cāsmān virāṭasya hitaiṣiṇaḥ
d tatra vetsyāmahe tān vai buddhvā caiṣāṃ yathāgatim
d apūrṇasamayān bhūyo vanāya gamayāmahe
d hatvāpi caitāṃs tatraiva sukhaṃ bhokṣyāma medinīm
d alpāvaśiṣṭaḥ kālo 'yaṃ samayaś ca vibhāti me
d udyojayāma sainyāni śvobhūte gamanaṃ prati
d karṇa uvāca
d yadi tatra sma te pārthā bhaveyū rājasattama
d siddhiṃ cobhayakīṃ tat syāt tathāpi khalu yāsyatha
d nigrahād yā virāṭasya pāṇḍavānāṃ prabodhanam
d dīnās te kośahīnāś ca vanavāsena karśitāḥ
d sukhena hantum arhanti atha pravrājanāya vai
a tato duryodhano rājā vākyam ādāya tasya tat
c vaikartanasya karṇasya kṣipram ājñāpayat svayam
a śāsane nityasaṃyuktaṃ duḥśāsanam anantaram
c saha vṛddhais tu saṃmantrya kṣipraṃ yojaya vāhinīm
a yathoddeśaṃ ca gacchāmaḥ sahitāḥ sarvakauravaiḥ
c suśarmā tu yathoddiṣṭaṃ deśaṃ yātu mahārathaḥ
a trigartaiḥ sahito rājā samagrabalavāhanaḥ
c prāg eva hi susaṃvīto matsyasya viṣayaṃ prati
a jaghanyato vayaṃ tatra yāsyāmo divasāntaram
c viṣayaṃ matsyarājasya susamṛddhaṃ susaṃhatāḥ
d suśarmaṇā gṛhīte tu matsyarājasya godhane
d virāṭaḥ sainyam ādāya trigartaiḥ saha yotsyate
d aparaṃ divasaṃ gās tu tatra gṛhṇantu kauravāḥ
d gavārthe pāṇḍavās tatra yotsyanti kurubhiḥ saha
a te yātvā sahasā tatra virāṭanagaraṃ prati
c kṣipraṃ gopān samāsādya gṛhṇantu vipulaṃ dhanam
a gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi śrīmanti guṇavanti ca
c vayam api nigṛhṇīmo dvidhā kṛtvā varūthinīm
 asatāṃ saṅgadoṣeṇa sādhavo yānti vikriyām
 duryodhanaprasaṅgena bhīṣmo gograhaṇe gataḥ
 saṃnaddhā rathinaḥ sarve sapadātibalotkaṭāḥ
 prativairaṃ cikīrṣanto goṣu saṃnyapatan pare
a sa sma gatvā yathoddiṣṭāṃ diśaṃ vahner mahīpatiḥ
c ādatta gāḥ suśarmātha gharmapakṣasya saptamīm
a aparaṃ divasaṃ sarve rājan saṃbhūya kauravāḥ
c aṣṭamyāṃ tāny agṛhṇanta gokulāni sahasraśaḥ
d kauravās tu mahāvīryā matsyānāṃ viṣayāntare
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tatas teṣāṃ mahārāja tatraivāmitatejasām
c chadmaliṅgapraviṣṭānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
a vyatītaḥ samayaḥ samyag vasatāṃ vai purottame
c kurvatāṃ tasya karmāṇi virāṭasya mahīpateḥ
d kīcake tu hate rājā virāṭaḥ paravīrahā
d āsāṃ cakre sahāmātyaḥ kuntīputraś ca vīryavān
a tatas trayodaśasyānte tasya varṣasya bhārata
c suśarmaṇā gṛhītaṃ tu godhanaṃ tarasā bahu
d tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīd reṇuś ca divam aspṛśat
d śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣo bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaḥ
d gavāśvarathanāgānāṃ narāṇāṃ ca padātinām
d evaṃ tais tv abhiniryāya matsyarājasya godhane
d trigartair gṛhyamāṇe tu gopālāḥ pratyaṣedhayan
d atha trigartā bahavaḥ parigṛhya dhanaṃ bahu
d parikṣipya hayaiḥ śīghrai rathavrātaiś ca bhārata
d gopālān pratyayudhyanta raṇe kṛtvā jaye dhṛtim
d te hanyamānā bahubhiḥ prāsatomarapāṇibhiḥ
d gopālā gokule bhaktā vārayām āsur ojasā
d paraśvadhaiś ca musalair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca mudgaraiḥ
d gopālāḥ karpaṇaiś citrair jaghnur aśvān samantataḥ
d te hanyamānāḥ saṃkruddhās trigartā rathayodhinaḥ
d visṛjya śaravarṣāṇi gopān vyadrāvayan raṇe
d tato yuvānaḥ saṃbhītāḥ śvasanto reṇuguṇṭhitāḥ
a tato javena mahatā gopāḥ puram athāvrajat
c apaśyan matsyarājaṃ ca rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalī
d virāṭanagaraṃ prāpya narā rājānam abruvan
a śūraiḥ parivṛtaṃ yodhaiḥ kuṇḍalāṅgadadhāribhiḥ
c sadbhiś ca mantribhiḥ sārdhaṃ pāṇḍavaiś ca nararṣabhaiḥ
a taṃ sabhāyāṃ mahārājam āsīnaṃ rāṣṭravardhanam
c so 'bravīd upasaṃgamya virāṭaṃ praṇatas tadā
a asmān yudhi vinirjitya paribhūya sabāndhavān
c gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi trigartāḥ kālayanti te
e tān parīpsa manuṣyendra mā neśuḥ paśavas tava
f vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
f śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ gopālānām ariṃdamaḥ
a tac chrutvā nṛpatiḥ senāṃ matsyānāṃ samayojayat
c rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pattidhvajasamākulām
d samādiśya tadā rājā matsyānāṃ paravīrahā
a rājāno rājaputrāś ca tanutrāṇy atra bhejire
c bhānumanti vicitrāṇi sūpasevyāni bhāgaśaḥ
d pṛthak kāñcanasaṃnāhān ratheṣv aśvān ayojayan
d utkṛṣya pāśān maurvīṇāṃ vīrāś cāpeṣv ayojayan
a savajrāyasagarbhaṃ tu kavacaṃ taptakāñcanam
c virāṭasya priyo bhrātā śatānīko 'bhyahārayat
a sarvapārasavaṃ varma kalyāṇapaṭalaṃ dṛḍham
c śatānīkād avarajo madirāśvo 'bhyahārayat
a śatasūryaṃ śatāvartaṃ śatabindu śatākṣimat
c abhedyakalpaṃ matsyānāṃ rājā kavacam āharat
a utsedhe yasya padmāni śataṃ saugandhikāni ca
c suvarṇapṛṣṭhaṃ sūryābhaṃ sūryadatto 'bhyahārayat
a dṛḍham āyasagarbhaṃ tu śvetaṃ varma śatākṣimat
c virāṭasya suto jyeṣṭho vīraḥ śaṅkho 'bhyahārayat
a śataśaś ca tanutrāṇi yathāsvāni mahārathāḥ
c yotsyamānābhyanahyanta devarūpāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a sūpaskareṣu śubhreṣu mahatsu ca mahārathāḥ
c pṛthak kāñcanasaṃnāhān ratheṣv aśvān ayojayan
a sūryacandrapratīkāśo rathe divye hiraṇmayaḥ
c mahānubhāvo matsyasya dhvaja ucchiśriye tadā
a athānyān vividhākārān dhvajān hemavibhūṣitān
b vājino vividhāṃś caiva taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇān
c yathāsvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ śūrā ratheṣu samayojayan
d ratheṣu yujyamāneṣu kaṅko rājānam abravīt
d mayāpy astraṃ caturmārgam avāptam ṛṣisattamāt
d daṃśito ratham āsthāya padaṃ niryāmy ahaṃ gavām
d ayaṃ ca balavāñ chūro valalo dṛśyate 'nagha
d gosaṃkhyam aśvabandhaṃ ca ratheṣu samayojaya
d naite na jātu yudhyeyur gavārtham iti me matiḥ
a atha matsyo 'bravīd rājā śatānīkaṃ jaghanyajam
c kaṅkaballavagopālā dāmagranthiś ca vīryavān
d tantipālaś ca gosaṃkhyo ya etat puruṣarṣabhāḥ
e yudhyeyur iti me buddhir vartate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a eteṣām api dīyantāṃ rathā dhvajapatākinaḥ
c kavacāni vicitrāṇi dṛḍhāni ca mṛdūni ca
e pratimuñcantu gātreṣu dīyantām āyudhāni ca
a vīrāṅgarūpāḥ puruṣā nāgarājakaropamāḥ
c neme jātu na yudhyerann iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a etac chrutvā tu nṛpater vākyaṃ tvaritamānasaḥ
c śatānīkas tu pārthebhyo rathān rājan samādiśat
e sahadevāya rājñe ca bhīmāya nakulāya ca
a tān prahṛṣṭās tataḥ sūtā rājabhaktipuraskṛtāḥ
c nirdiṣṭān naradevena rathāñ śīghram ayojayan
a kavacāni vicitrāṇi dṛḍhāni ca mṛdūni ca
c virāṭaḥ prādiśad yāni teṣām akliṣṭakarmaṇām
d tāni te pratigṛhyāśu samanahyanta pāṇḍavāḥ
d vīrāś ca siṃhavikrāntā balavanto manasvinaḥ
e tāny āmucya śarīreṣu daṃśitās te paraṃtapāḥ
f rathān hayaiḥ susaṃpannān āsthāya ca narottamāḥ
f niryuyur muditāḥ pārthāḥ śatrusaṃghāvamardinaḥ
a tarasvinaś channarūpāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
b rathān hemaparicchinnān āsthāya ca mahārathāḥ
b pāṇḍavā niryayur hṛṣṭā daṃśitā rājasattamāḥ
c virāṭam anvayuḥ paścāt sahitāḥ kurupuṃgavāḥ
e catvāro bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ satyavikramāḥ
f dīrghāṇāṃ ca dṛḍhānāṃ ca dhanuṣāṃ te yathābalam
f utkṛṣya pāśān maurvīṇāṃ vīrāś cāpeṣv ayojayan
f tataḥ suvāsasaḥ sarve te vīrāś candanokṣitāḥ
f coditā naradevena kṣipram aśvān acodayan
f te hayā hemasaṃchannā bṛhantaḥ sādhuvāhinaḥ
f coditāḥ pratyadṛśyanta pakṣiṇām iva paṅktayaḥ
a bhīmāś ca mattamātaṅgāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
c kṣaranta iva jīmūtāḥ sudantāḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanāḥ
a svārūḍhā yuddhakuśalaiḥ śikṣitair hastisādibhiḥ
c rājānam anvayuḥ paścāc calanta iva parvatāḥ
a viśāradānāṃ vaśyānāṃ hṛṣṭānāṃ cānuyāyinām
b viṃśatis tu sahasrāṇi narāṇām anuyāyinām
c aṣṭau rathasahasrāṇi daśa nāgaśatāni ca
e ṣaṣṭiś cāśvasahasrāṇi matsyānām abhiniryayuḥ
f pūrṇe śatasahasre dve padātīnāṃ ca bhārata
f etad balam aparyantaṃ matsyānām abhiniryayau
a tad anīkaṃ virāṭasya śuśubhe bharatarṣabha
b vasante bahupuṣpāḍhyaṃ kānanaṃ citritaṃ yathā
c saṃprayātaṃ mahārāja ninīṣantaṃ gavāṃ padam
a tad balāgryaṃ virāṭasya saṃprasthitam aśobhata
c dṛḍhāyudhajanākīrṇaṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a niryāya nagarāc chūrā vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c trigartān aspṛśan matsyāḥ sūrye pariṇate sati
da trigartā aspṛśan mātsyān pūrvam eva mahārathāḥ
a te trigartāś ca matsyāś ca saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c anyonyam abhigarjanto goṣu gṛddhā mahābalāḥ
a bhīmāś ca mattamātaṅgās tomarāṅkuśacoditāḥ
c grāmaṇīyaiḥ samārūḍhāḥ kuśalair hastisādibhiḥ
a teṣāṃ samāgamo ghoras tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
b ghnatāṃ parasparaṃ ghoro yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥ
c devāsurasamo rājann āsīt sūrye vilambati
d padātirathanāgendrahayārohabalaughavān
d anyonyam abhyāpatatāṃ nighnatāṃ cetaretaram
a udatiṣṭhad rajo bhaumaṃ na prajñāyata kiṃ cana
c pakṣiṇaś cāpatan bhūmau sainyena rajasāvṛtāḥ
a iṣubhir vyatisaṃyadbhir ādityo 'ntaradhīyata
c khadyotair iva saṃyuktam antarikṣaṃ vyarājata
d rukmapuṅkhaiḥ sutīkṣṇāgrair vajrāgnisadṛśaprabhaiḥ
a rukmapṛṣṭhāni cāpāni vyatiṣaktāni dhanvinām
c patatāṃ lokavīrāṇāṃ savyadakṣiṇam asyatām
a rathā rathaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātaiś ca padātayaḥ
c sādibhiḥ sādinaś caiva gajaiś cāpi mahāgajāḥ
d rathinaḥ sādinaś cātra saṃprahāram akurvata
a asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsaiḥ śaktibhis tomarair api
c saṃrabdhāḥ samare rājan nijaghnur itaretaram
d antarikṣe gatir yeṣāṃ dadṛśuś cāpi vadhyatām
a nighnantaḥ samare 'nyonyaṃ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
c na śekur abhisaṃrabdhāḥ śūrān kartuṃ parāṅmukhān
a kḷptottaroṣṭhaṃ sunasaṃ kḷptakeśam alaṃkṛtam
c adṛśyata śiraś chinnaṃ rajodhvastaṃ sakuṇḍalam
a adṛśyaṃs tatra gātrāṇi śaraiś chinnāni bhāgaśaḥ
c śālaskandhanikāśāni kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahāmṛdhe
a nāgabhoganikāśaiś ca bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥ
c ākīrṇā vasudhā tatra śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
d rathināṃ rathibhiś cātra saṃprahāro 'bhyavartata
d sādibhiḥ sādināṃ cātra pādātānāṃ padātibhiḥ
d yathā vā vāsasī ślakṣṇe mahārajatarañjite
d bibhratī yuvatī śyāmā bhāti tadvad vasuṃdharā
a upaśāmyad rajo bhaumaṃ rudhireṇa prasarpatā
c kaśmalaṃ prāviśad ghoraṃ nirmaryādam avartata
d upākrośaṃs tadānyonyaṃ śarair gāḍhaṃ pravejitāḥ
d antarikṣe gatir yeṣāṃ darśanaṃ cāpy arudhyata
d upānighnaṃta subhṛśaṃ goṣu govṛṣabhā iva
d yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi dharmātmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitas tadā
d vyūhaṃ kṛtvā virāṭasya anvayudhyata pāṇḍavaḥ
d ātmānaṃ śyenavat kṛtvā tuṇḍam āsīd yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d pakṣau yamau ca bhavataḥ puccham āsīd vṛkodaraḥ
d sahasraṃ nyahanat tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d bhīmasenaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d dvisāhasraṃ rathān vīraḥ paralokaṃ praveśayat
d nakulas triśataṃ jaghne sahadevaś catuḥśatam
a śatānīkaḥ śataṃ hatvā viśālākṣaś catuḥśatam
c praviṣṭau mahatīṃ senāṃ trigartānāṃ mahārathau
d tau praviśya mahāsenāṃ balavantau yaśasvinau
e ārcchetāṃ bahusaṃrabdhau keśākeśi nakhānakhi
a lakṣayitvā trigartānāṃ tau praviṣṭau rathavrajam
c jagmatuḥ sūryadattaś ca madirāśvaś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
d śaṅkho virāṭaputras tu maheṣvāso mahābalaḥ
d vinighnan samare śatrūn praviveśa mahācamūm
a virāṭas tatra saṃgrāme hatvā pañcaśatān rathān
c hayānāṃ ca śatāny atra hatvā pañca mahārathān
a caran sa vividhān mārgān ratheṣu rathayūthapaḥ
c trigartānāṃ suśarmāṇam ārcchad rukmarathaṃ raṇe
a tau vyāvaharatāṃ tatra mahātmānau mahābalau
c anyonyam abhigarjantau goṣṭhe govṛṣabhāv iva
d tato rājā trigartānāṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥ
d matsyaṃ samīyād yattāśvaṃ dvairathena nararṣabhaḥ
d trigartānāṃ ca mukhyo 'sau matsyānāṃ ca mahābalaḥ
d abhīyatur athānyonyaṃ dvairathena nararṣabha
d rājasiṃhau susaṃrabdhau virejatur amarṣaṇau
d ayudhyanta raṇe vīrāḥ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥ
d kabandhāḥ samare hantuṃ mahāyodhāḥ pracakramuḥ
d hanyatāṃ hanyatām eva śirāṃsi patitāny api
d kabandhān prerayām āsur huṃkāroccāraṇādibhiḥ
d virāṭaś ca mahāścaryaṃ dṛṣṭvā kautukam āgatam
d harṣaṃ lebhe paraṃ rājā mamāpy evaṃvidhā narāḥ
d kabandhena śataṃ yodhāḥ pātitā raṇamūrdhani
d tataḥ kabandhaḥ patitaḥ puṣpavarṣaiḥ sahaiva tu
d vimānaṃ preritaṃ devair apsarobhiḥ samāvṛtam
d samakṣaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ tatrārūḍho divaṃ yayau
d na śekur iti saṃkruddhāḥ śūrāḥ kartuṃ parāṅmukhān
a tato rathābhyāṃ rathinau vyatiyāya samantataḥ
c śarān vyasṛjatāṃ śīghraṃ toyadhārā ghanāv iva
a anyonyaṃ cātisaṃrabdhau viceratur amarṣaṇau
c kṛtāstrau niśitair bāṇair asiśaktigadābhṛtau
a tato rājā suśarmāṇaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
c pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiś cāsya vivyādha caturo hayān
d dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ tu vivyādha ketuṃ ca tribhir āśugaiḥ
a tathaiva matsyarājānaṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥ
c pañcāśatā śitair bāṇair vivyādha paramāstravit
a tataḥ sainyaṃ samāvṛtya matsyarājasuśarmaṇoḥ
c nābhyajānaṃs tadānyonyaṃ pradoṣe rajasāvṛte
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tamasābhiplute loke rajasā caiva bhārata
c vyatiṣṭhan vai muhūrtaṃ tu vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a tato 'ndhakāraṃ praṇudann udatiṣṭhata candramāḥ
c kurvāṇo vimalāṃ rātriṃ nandayan kṣatriyān yudhi
a tataḥ prakāśam āsādya punar yuddham avartata
c ghorarūpaṃ tatas te sma nāvekṣanta parasparam
a tataḥ suśarmā traigartaḥ saha bhrātrā yavīyasā
c abhyadravan matsyarājaṃ rathavrātena sarvaśaḥ
a tato rathābhyāṃ praskandya bhrātarau kṣatriyarṣabhau
c gadāpāṇī susaṃrabdhau samabhyadravatāṃ hayān
a tathaiva teṣāṃ tu balāni tāni
kruddhāny athānyonyam abhidravanti
c gadāsikhaḍgaiś ca paraśvadhaiś ca
prāsaiś ca tīkṣṇāgrasupītadhāraiḥ
a balaṃ tu matsyasya balena rājā
sarvaṃ trigartādhipatiḥ suśarmā
c pramathya jitvā ca prasahya matsyaṃ
virāṭam ojasvinam abhyadhāvat
d mattāv iva vṛṣāv etau gajāv iva madoddhatau
d siṃhāv iva gajagrāhau śakravṛtrāv ivotthitau
d ubhau tulyabalotsāhāv ubhau tulyaparākramau
d ubhau tulyāstravikṣepāv ubhau yuddhaviśāradau
a tau nihatya pṛthag dhuryāv ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī
b āstāṃ tulyadhanurgrāhau viṣṇukaṃsāv ivoddhatau
b suśarmā paravīraghno balavān vīryavān gadī
c virathaṃ matsyarājānaṃ jīvagrāham agṛhṇatām
a tam unmathya suśarmā tu rudatīṃ vadhukām iva
c syandanaṃ svaṃ samāropya prayayau śīghravāhanaḥ
a tasmin gṛhīte virathe virāṭe balavattare
b balaṃ sarvaṃ vibhagnaṃ tan nirutsāhaṃ nirāśakam
c prādravanta bhayān matsyās trigartair arditā bhṛśam
d vidikṣu dikṣu sarvāsu palāyanti ca yānti ca
a teṣu saṃtrāsyamāneṣu kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c abhyabhāṣan mahābāhuṃ bhīmasenam ariṃdamam
a matsyarājaḥ parāmṛṣṭas trigartena suśarmaṇā
c taṃ mokṣaya mahābāho na gacched dviṣatāṃ vaśam
a uṣitāḥ smaḥ sukhaṃ sarve sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāḥ
b bhīmasena mahābāho gṛhītaṃ taṃ suśarmaṇā
b trāyasva mokṣaya kṣipram asmatprītikaraṃ nṛpam
c bhīmasena tvayā kāryā tasya vāsasya niṣkṛtiḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d taṃ tathāvādinaṃ tatra bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
d abhyabhāṣata durdharṣo raṇamadhye yudhiṣṭhiram
 bhīmasena uvāca
a aham enaṃ paritrāsye śāsanāt tava pārthiva
c paśya me sumahat karma yudhyataḥ saha śatrubhiḥ
a svabāhubalam āśritya tiṣṭha tvaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c ekāntam āśrito rājan paśya me 'dya parākramam
a suskandho 'yaṃ mahāvṛkṣo gadārūpa iva sthitaḥ
c enam eva samārujya drāvayiṣyāmi śātravān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a taṃ mattam iva mātaṅgaṃ vīkṣamāṇaṃ vanaspatim
c abravīd bhrātaraṃ vīraṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a mā bhīma sāhasaṃ kārṣīs tiṣṭhatv eṣa vanaspatiḥ
c mā tvā vṛkṣeṇa karmāṇi kurvāṇam atimānuṣam
e janāḥ samavabudhyeran bhīmo 'yam iti bhārata
f mā grahīs tvam imaṃ vṛkṣaṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca mā nada
f imaṃ vṛkṣaṃ gṛhītvā tvaṃ nemāṃ senām abhidrava
f vṛkṣaṃ cet tvaṃ nayer vīra vijñāsyati jano dhruvam
a anyad evāyudhaṃ kiṃ cit pratipadyasva mānuṣam
c cāpaṃ vā yadi vā śaktiṃ nistriṃśaṃ vā paraśvadham
a yad eva mānuṣaṃ bhīma bhaved anyair alakṣitam
c tad evāyudham ādāya mokṣayāśu mahīpatim
a yamau ca cakrarakṣau te bhavitārau mahābalau
c vyūhataḥ samare tāta matsyarājaṃ parīpsataḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d bhrātur vacanam ājñāya bhīmo vṛkṣaṃ visṛjya ca
d cāpam ādāya saṃprāpto ratham āruhya pāṇḍavaḥ
d ity uktvā bhīmasenaṃ taṃ svayam eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d anvayāj javanair aśvaiḥ parīpsan mātsyasattamam
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evam uktas tu vegena bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
d gṛhītvā tu dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ javena sumahājavaḥ
d vimuñcac charavarṣāṇi satoya iva toyadaḥ
d taṃ bhīmo bhīmakarmāṇaṃ suśarmāṇam athādravat
d virāṭaṃ samavīkṣyainaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cāvadat
d suśarmā cintayām āsa kālāntakayamopamam
d tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhāṣantaṃ pṛṣṭhato rathapuṃgavaḥ
d paśyatāṃ sumahat karma mahad yuddham upasthitam
d parāvṛtto dhanur gṛhya suśarmā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
d nimeṣāntaramātreṇa bhīmasenena te rathāḥ
d pātitā bhīmasenena virāṭasya samīpataḥ
d rathānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca vājināṃ ca sasādinām
d sahasraśatasaṃghātāḥ śūrāṇām ugradhanvinām
d pattayo nihatās teṣāṃ gadāṃ gṛhya mahātmanā
d tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ yuddhaṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥ
d cintayām āsa manasā kiṃśeṣaṃ hi balasya me
d aparo dṛśyate sainye purā magno mahābale
d ākarṇapūrṇena tadā dhanuṣā pratyadṛśyata
d suśarmā sāyakāṃs tīkṣṇān kṣipate ca punaḥ punaḥ
a tataḥ samastās te sarve turagān abhyacodayan
c divyam astraṃ vikurvāṇās trigartān pratyamarṣaṇāḥ
a tān nivṛttarathān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān sā mahācamūḥ
c vairāṭī paramakruddhā yuyudhe paramādbhutam
d trigartāḥ samatikramya vyayudhyanta jayaiṣiṇaḥ
d tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a sahasraṃ nyavadhīt tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmaḥ saptaśatān yodhān paralokam adarśayat
e nakulaś cāpi saptaiva śatāni prāhiṇoc charaiḥ
a śatāni trīṇi śūrāṇāṃ sahadevaḥ pratāpavān
c yudhiṣṭhirasamādiṣṭo nijaghne puruṣarṣabhaḥ
d tato 'bhyapatad atyugraḥ suśarmāṇam udāyudham
e bhittvā tāṃ mahatīṃ senāṃ trigartānāṃ nararṣabha
f kṣobhayan sarvasainyāni siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān iva
a tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥ
c abhidrutya suśarmāṇaṃ śarair abhyatudad bhṛśam
a suśarmāpi susaṃkruddhas tvaramāṇo yudhiṣṭhiram
c avidhyan navabhir bāṇaiś caturbhiś caturo hayān
a tato rājann āśukārī kuntīputro vṛkodaraḥ
c samāsādya suśarmāṇam aśvān asya vyapothayat
a pṛṣṭhagopau ca tasyātha hatvā paramasāyakaiḥ
c athāsya sārathiṃ kruddho rathopasthād apāharat
a cakrarakṣaś ca śūraś ca śoṇāśvo nāma viśrutaḥ
c sa bhayād dvairathaṃ dṛṣṭvā traigartaṃ prājahat tadā
a tato virāṭaḥ praskandya rathād atha suśarmaṇaḥ
c gadām asya parāmṛśya tam evājaghnivān balī
e sa cacāra gadāpāṇir vṛddho 'pi taruṇo yathā
f tayoḥ sa dṛṣṭvā tatkarma matsyapāṇḍavayor mṛdhe
f tvaramāṇo rathaṃ tyaktvā padātiḥ prādravad raṇāt
f palāyamānaṃ traigartaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmo 'bhyabhāṣata
f anena vīryeṇa kathaṃ gās tvaṃ prārthayase balāt
f rājaputra nivartasva na te yuktaṃ palāyanam
f kathaṃ cānucarāṃs tyaktvā śatrumadhye viṣīdasi
f ity uktaḥ sa tu pārthena suśarmā rathayūthapaḥ
f tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhīmaṃ sa sahasābhyadravad balī
f pañcabhis tvarito bhīmaṃ jaghāna samare balī
f tāṃ  bāṇān triṇīkṛtya jīvitepsus tato raṇāt
f prādravat tūrṇam avyagro jīvitepsuḥ suśarmaṇaḥ

d tvayājayat sahāyena pṛthivīṃ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
a sā sārathyaṃ mama bhrātuḥ kuru sādhu bṛhannaḍe
c purā dūrataraṃ gāvo hriyante kurubhir hi naḥ
a athaitad vacanaṃ me 'dya niyuktā na kariṣyasi
c praṇayād ucyamānā tvaṃ parityakṣyāmi jīvitam
a evam uktas tu suśroṇyā tayā sakhyā paraṃtapaḥ
c jagāma rājaputrasya sakāśam amitaujasaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d sā vajravaiḍūryavikārakuṇḍalā
d vinidrapadmotpalapatragandhinī
d prasannatārādhipasaṃnibhānanā
d pārthaṃ kumārī vacanaṃ babhāṣe
d haranti vittaṃ kuravaḥ pitur me
d śataṃ sahasrāṇi gavāṃ bṛhannale
d sā bhrātur aśvān mama saṃyamasva
d purā pare dūrataraṃ haranti gāḥ
d sairandhrir ākhyāti bṛhannale tvāṃ
d suśikṣitāṃ saṃgrahaṇe rathāśvayoḥ
d ahaṃ mariṣyāmi na me 'tra saṃśayo
d mayā vṛtā tatra na ced gamiṣyasi
d tathā niyukto naradevakanyayā
d narottamaḥ prītamanā dhanaṃjayaḥ
d uvāca pārthaḥ śubhamandayā girā
d śubhānanāṃ śukladatīṃ śucismitām
d gacchāmi yatrecchasi cāruhāsini
d hutāśanaṃ prajvalitaṃ vrajāmi vā
d icchāmi te 'haṃ varagātri jīvitaṃ
d karomi kiṃ te priyam adya sundari
d na matkṛte drakṣyasi tat puraṃ priye
d vaivasvataṃ pretapater mahābhayam
d sa evam uktvā kuruvīrapuṃgavo
d vilāsinīṃ śukladatīṃ śucismitām
d bṛhannalārūpavibhūṣitānano
d virāṭaputrasya samīpam āvrajat
d tam āvrajantaṃ varabhūṣaṇair vṛtaṃ
d mahāprabhaṃ vāraṇayūthapopamam
d gajendrabāhuṃ kamalāyatekṣaṇaṃ
d kavāṭavakṣaḥsthalam unnatāṃsam
d tam āgataṃ pārtham amitrakarśanaṃ
d mahābalaṃ nāgam iva pramāthinam
d vairāṭir āmantrya tato bṛhannalāṃ
d gavāṃ ninīṣan padam uttaro 'bravīt
a taṃ sā vrajantaṃ tvaritaṃ prabhinnam iva kuñjaram
c anvagacchad viśālākṣī śiśur gajavadhūr iva
a dūrād eva tu taṃ prekṣya rājaputro 'bhyabhāṣata
c tvayā sārathinā pārthaḥ khāṇḍave 'gnim atarpayat
a pṛthivīm ajayat kṛtsnāṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c sairandhrī tvāṃ samācaṣṭa sā hi jānāti pāṇḍavān
a saṃyaccha māmakān aśvāṃs tathaiva tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
c kurubhir yotsyamānasya godhanāni parīpsataḥ
a arjunasya kilāsīs tvaṃ sārathir dayitaḥ purā
c tvayājayat sahāyena pṛthivīṃ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥ
d devendrasārathir vīro mātaliḥ khyātavikramaḥ
d suhotro jāmadagnyasya viṣṇor yantā ca dārukaḥ
d aruṇaḥ sūryayantā ca sumantro daśarathasya ca
d sarve sārathayaḥ khyātā na bṛhannalayā samāḥ
d ity ukto 'haṃ ca sairandhryā tena tvām āhvayāmi vai
d āhūtā tvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ yoddhuṃ yāhi bṛhannale
d dūrād dūrataraṃ gāvo bhavanti kurubhir hṛtāḥ
a evam uktā pratyuvāca rājaputraṃ bṛhannaḍā
c kā śaktir mama sārathyaṃ kartuṃ saṃgrāmamūrdhani
a gītaṃ vā yadi vā nṛttaṃ vāditraṃ vā pṛthagvidham
c tat kariṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sārathyaṃ tu kuto mayi
 uttara uvāca
a bṛhannaḍe gāyano vā nartano vā punar bhava
c kṣipraṃ me ratham āsthāya nigṛhṇīṣva hayottamān
d tvaṃ nartako vā yadi vāpi gāyakaḥ
d kṣipraṃ tanutraṃ paridhatsva bhānumat
d abhīkṣṇam āhus tava karma pauruṣaṃ
d striyaḥ praśaṃsanti mamādya cāntike
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d ity evam uktvā nṛpasūnusattamas
d tadā smayitvārjunam abhyanandayat
d athottaraḥ pāraśavaṃ śatākṣimat
d suvarṇacitraṃ parigṛhya bhānumat
d bṛhannalāyai pradadau svayaṃ tadā
d virāṭaputraḥ paravīraghātine
d tadājñayā mātsyasutasya vīryavān
d akartukāmeva samādade tadā
d bṛhannalā
d yady asti ca raṇe śauryaṃ śaktiḥ syād dviṣatāṃ vadhe
d ahaṃ tvām abhigacchāmi yatra tvaṃ yāsi tatra bhoḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa tatra narmasaṃyuktam akarot pāṇḍavo bahu
c uttarāyāḥ pramukhataḥ sarvaṃ jānann ariṃdama
a ūrdhvam utkṣipya kavacaṃ śarīre pratyamuñcata
c kumāryas tatra taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāhasan pṛthulocanāḥ
d tam ādadānaṃ pramadā jahāsire
d hy adhomukhaṃ vīravaro 'bhyahārayat
d tatas tiraścīnakṛtaṃ sapatnahā
d hy adhomukhaṃ kavacam athābhyakarṣayat
d samyak prajānann api satyavikramo
d hy ajñātavat sarvakurupravīraḥ
d ūrdhvaṃ kṣipan vīravaro 'bhyahārayat
d punaś ca yatnāt kavacaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
d evaṃprakārāṇi bahūni kurvati
d tasmin kumāryaḥ pramadā jahāsire
a sa tu dṛṣṭvā vimuhyantaṃ svayam evottaras tataḥ
c kavacena mahārheṇa samanahyad bṛhannaḍām
d tathā vikurvantam amitrakarśanaṃ
d naivottaraḥ paryabhavad dhanaṃjayam
d taṃ rājaputraḥ samanāhayat svayaṃ
d jāmbūnadāntena śubhena varmaṇā
d kṛśānutaptapratimena bhāsvatā
d jājvalyamānena sahasraraśminā
a sa bibhrat kavacaṃ cāgryaṃ svayam apy aṃśumatprabham
c dhvajaṃ ca siṃham ucchritya sārathye samakalpayat
d athāsya śīghraṃ prasamīkṣya yojayad
d rathe hayān kāñcanajālasaṃvṛtān
d suvarṇajālāntarayoktṛbhūṣaṇān
d siṃhaṃ ca sauvarṇam upāśrayad rathe
a dhanūṃṣi ca mahārhāṇi bāṇāṃś ca rucirān bahūn
b āyudhāni ca vai tatra rathopasthe ca saṃnyasat
c ādāya prayayau vīraḥ sa bṛhannaḍasārathiḥ
a athottarā ca kanyāś ca sakhyas tām abruvaṃs tadā
c bṛhannaḍe ānayethā vāsāṃsi rucirāṇi naḥ
a pāñcālikārthaṃ sūkṣmāṇi citrāṇi vividhāni ca
c vijitya saṃgrāmagatān bhīṣmadroṇamukhān kurūn
a atha tā bruvatīḥ kanyāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c pratyuvāca hasan pārtho meghadundubhiniḥsvanaḥ
a yady uttaro 'yaṃ saṃgrāme vijeṣyati mahārathān
c athāhariṣye vāsāṃsi divyāni rucirāṇi ca
a evam uktvā tu bībhatsus tataḥ prācodayad dhayān
c kurūn abhimukhāñ śūro nānādhvajapatākinaḥ
d athottaro varma mahāprabhāvaṃ
d suvarṇavaiḍūryapariṣkṛtaṃ dṛḍham
d āmucya vīraḥ prayayau rathottamaṃ
d dhanaṃjayaṃ sārathinaṃ pragṛhya
d tam uttaraṃ vīkṣya rathottame sthitaṃ
d bṛhannaḍāyāḥ sahitaṃ mahābhujam
d striyaś ca kanyāś ca dvijāś ca suvratāḥ
d pradakṣiṇaṃ cakrur athocuraṅganāḥ
d yad arjunasyarṣabhatulyagāminaḥ
d purābhavat khāṇḍavadāhamaṅgalam
d kurūn samāsādya raṇe bṛhannaḍe
d sahottareṇāstu tad adya maṅgalam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa rājadhānyā niryāya vairāṭiḥ pṛthivīṃjayaḥ
c prayāhīty abravīt sūtaṃ yatra te kuravo gatāḥ
a samavetān kurūn yāvaj jigīṣūn avajitya vai
c gāś caiṣāṃ kṣipram ādāya punar āyāmi svaṃ puram
a tatas tāṃś codayām āsa sadaśvān pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c te hayā narasiṃhena coditā vātaraṃhasaḥ
e ālikhanta ivākāśam ūhuḥ kāñcanamālinaḥ
a nātidūram atho yātvā matsyaputradhanaṃjayau
c avekṣetām amitraghnau kurūṇāṃ balināṃ balam
e śmaśānam abhito gatvā āsasāda kurūn atha
f tāṃ śamīm anvavīkṣetāṃ vyūḍhānīkāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
a tad anīkaṃ mahat teṣāṃ vibabhau sāgarasvanam
c sarpamāṇam ivākāśe vanaṃ bahulapādapam
a dadṛśe pārthivo reṇur janitas tena sarpatā
c dṛṣṭipraṇāśo bhūtānāṃ divaspṛṅ narasattama
a tad anīkaṃ mahad dṛṣṭvā gajāśvarathasaṃkulam
c karṇaduryodhanakṛpair guptaṃ śāṃtanavena ca
a droṇena ca saputreṇa maheṣvāsena dhīmatā
b teṣāṃ tat sainyam atulaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayavivardhanam
c hṛṣṭaromā bhayodvignaḥ pārthaṃ vairāṭir abravīt
a notsahe kurubhir yoddhuṃ romaharṣaṃ hi paśya me
c bahupravīram atyugraṃ devair api durāsadam
e pratiyoddhuṃ na śakṣyāmi kurusainyam anantakam
a nāśaṃse bhāratīṃ senāṃ praveṣṭuṃ bhīmakārmukām
b devair api sahendreṇa na śakyaṃ kiṃ punar naraiḥ
c rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pattidhvajasamākulām
e dṛṣṭvaiva hi parān ājāv ātmā pravyathatīva me
a yatra droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca kṛpaḥ karṇo viviṃśatiḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadatto 'tha bāhlikaḥ
a duryodhanas tathā vīro rājā ca rathināṃ varaḥ
c dyutimanto maheṣvāsāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
d mattā iva mahānāgā yuktadhvajapatākinaḥ
d nītimanto maheṣvāsāḥ sarvāstrakṛtaniścayāḥ
d durjayāḥ sarvasainyānāṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
d patākinaś ca mātaṅgāḥ sadhvajāś ca mahārathāḥ
d viprakīrṇāḥ kṛtodyogā vājinaś citrabhūṣitāḥ
d tāñ jetuṃ samare śūrān durbuddhir aham āgataḥ
a dṛṣṭvaiva hi kurūn etān vyūḍhānīkān prahāriṇaḥ
c hṛṣitāni ca romāṇi kaśmalaṃ cāgataṃ mama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a aviyāto viyātasya maurkhyād dhūrtasya paśyataḥ
b dṛṣṭvā tu mahatīṃ senāṃ kurūṇāṃ dṛḍhadhanvinām
c paridevayate mandaḥ sakāśe savyasācinaḥ
a trigartān me pitā yātaḥ śūnye saṃpraṇidhāya mām
c sarvāṃ senām upādāya na me santīha sainikāḥ
a so 'ham eko bahūn bālaḥ kṛtāstrān akṛtaśramaḥ
c pratiyoddhuṃ na śakṣyāmi nivartasva bṛhannaḍe
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d taṃ tathāvādinaṃ tatra bībhatsuḥ pratyabhāṣata
d saṃprahasya punas taṃ vai sarvalokamahārathaḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a bhayena dīnarūpo 'si dviṣatāṃ harṣavardhanaḥ
c na ca tāvat kṛtaṃ kiṃ cit paraiḥ karma raṇājire
a svayam eva ca mām āttha vaha māṃ kauravān prati
c so 'haṃ tvāṃ tatra neṣyāmi yatraite bahulā dhvajāḥ
a madhyam āmiṣagṛdhrāṇāṃ kurūṇām ātatāyinām
c neṣyāmi tvāṃ mahābāho pṛthivyām api yudhyatām
d samudram iva gambhīraṃ kurusainyam ariṃdama
d strīsakāśe pratijñāya puruṣāṇāṃ hi śṛṇvatām
d vikatthamāno niryātvā brūhi kiṃ nātra budhyase
a tathā strīṣu pratiśrutya pauruṣaṃ puruṣeṣu ca
c katthamāno 'bhiniryāya kimarthaṃ na yuyutsase
a na ced vijitya gās tās tvaṃ gṛhān vai pratiyāsyasi
c prahasiṣyanti vīra tvāṃ narā nāryaś ca saṃgatāḥ
a aham apy atra sairandhryā stutaḥ sārathyakarmaṇi
c na hi śakṣyāmy anirjitya gāḥ prayātuṃ puraṃ prati
a stotreṇa caiva sairandhryās tava vākyena tena ca
c kathaṃ na yudhyeyam ahaṃ kurūn sarvān sthiro bhava
 uttara uvāca
a kāmaṃ harantu matsyānāṃ bhūyāṃsaṃ kuravo dhanam
b agnido garadaś caiva śastrapāṇir dhanāpahaḥ
b kṣetradāraharaś caiva ṣaḍete hy ātatāyinaḥ
b ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāṅgapāragam
b jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na naro brahmahā bhavet
b saṃgrāmeṇa na me kāryaṃ gāvo gacchantu cāpi me
b śūnyaṃ me nagaraṃ cāpi pituś caiva bibhemy aham
b kṣīraṃ vā dadhi vājyaṃ vā takraṃ vā na pibāmy aham
b āranālaṃ hi pāsyāmi na me gobhiḥ prayojanam
b nagaraṃ ca pravekṣyāmi paśyatas te bṛhannale
b nivartaya rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ me vidīryate
b varaṃ kālena jīvakṣabhun na me gobhiḥ prayojanam
b yady ahaṃ jīvamānas tu gacchāmi nagaraṃ prati 
c prahasantu ca māṃ nāryo narā vāpi bṛhannaḍe
d bhojanaṃ gorasair hīnaṃ kāñjikenāpy ataḥ param
d bhokṣye 'haṃ bahubhir vāpi yāsye bālo mṛter bhayāt
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktvā prādravad bhīto rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalī
c tyaktvā mānaṃ sa mandātmā visṛjya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
 bṛhannaḍovāca
a naiṣa pūrvaiḥ smṛto dharmaḥ kṣatriyasya palāyanam
c śreyas te maraṇaṃ yuddhe na bhītasya palāyanam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā tu kaunteyaḥ so 'vaplutya rathottamāt
c tam anvadhāvad dhāvantaṃ rājaputraṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
e dīrghāṃ veṇīṃ vidhunvānaḥ sādhu rakte ca vāsasī
f vikramantaṃ padanyāsair namayann iva bhūtalam
a vidhūya veṇīṃ dhāvantam ajānanto 'rjunaṃ tadā
c sainikāḥ prāhasan ke cit tathārūpam avekṣya tam
a taṃ śīghram abhidhāvantaṃ saṃprekṣya kuravo 'bruvan
b sainikāḥ
b ko 'yaṃ dhāvaty asaṃgena pūrvaṃ muktvā rathottamam
c ka eṣa veṣapracchanno bhasmaneva hutāśanaḥ
a kiṃ cid asya yathā puṃsaḥ kiṃ cid asya yathā striyaḥ
b ity evaṃ sainikāḥ prāhur droṇas tān idam abravīt
b ācāryaḥ kurupāṇḍūnāṃ matau śukrāṅgiropamaḥ
b kiṃ vicāreṇa vaḥ kāryam etenānusṛtena vai
b dhāvantam anudhāvaṃś ca nirbhayo bhayaviplutam
b veṇīkalāpaṃ nirdhūya pravibhāti nararṣabhaḥ
c sārūpyam arjunasyeva klībarūpaṃ bibharti ca
d rūpeṇa pārthasadṛśaḥ strīveṣasamalaṃkṛtaḥ
a tad evaitac chirogrīvaṃ tau bāhū parighopamau
c tadvad evāsya vikrāntaṃ nāyam anyo dhanaṃjayāt
a amareṣv iva devendro mānuṣeṣu dhanaṃjayaḥ
c ekaḥ ko 'smān upāyāyād anyo loke dhanaṃjayāt
d droṇena caivam ukte tu karṇaḥ provāca buddhimān
a ekaḥ putro virāṭasya śūnye saṃnihitaḥ pure
c sa eṣa kila niryāto bālabhāvān na pauruṣāt
d klībaṃ vai sārathiṃ kṛtvā niryāto nagarād bahiḥ
a satreṇa nūnaṃ channaṃ hi carantaṃ pārtham arjunam
b te hi naḥ pratisaṃyātuṃ saṃgrāme na hi śaknuyuḥ
b katham ekataras teṣāṃ samastān yodhayet kurūn
c uttaraḥ sārathiṃ kṛtvā niryāto nagarād bahiḥ
a sa no manye dhvajān dṛṣṭvā bhīta eṣa palāyati
c taṃ nūnam eṣa dhāvantaṃ jighṛkṣati dhanaṃjayaḥ
d eko 'smān anuyāty eṣa nānyo loke dhanaṃjayāt
d sārathiṃ hy uttaraṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ yoddhum ihecchati
a iti sma kuravaḥ sarve vimṛśantaḥ pṛthak pṛthak
c na ca vyavasituṃ kiṃ cid uttaraṃ śaknuvanti te
d duryodhana uvācedaṃ sainikān rathasattamān
d arjuno vāsudevo vā rāmaḥ pradyumna eva vā
d te hi naḥ pratisaṃyoddhuṃ saṃgrāme na hi śaknuyuḥ
d katham ekataras teṣāṃ samastān yodhayet kurūn
d anyo vai klībaveṣeṇa yady āgacched gavāṃ padam
d śarais tīkṣṇair arpayitvā pātayiṣyāmi bhūtale
e channaṃ tathā taṃ satreṇa pāṇḍavaṃ prekṣya bhārata
f arjunaṃ neti cety enaṃ na vyavasyanti te punaḥ
f iti sma kuravaḥ sarve mantrayanti mahārathāḥ
f dṛḍhavedhī mahāsattvaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ
f abhyāgacchati ced yoddhuṃ sarvaṃ saṃśayitaṃ balam
f na cāpy anyataraṃ tatra vyavasyanti dhanaṃjayāt
a uttaraṃ tu pradhāvantam anudrutya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c gatvā padaśataṃ tūrṇaṃ keśapakṣe parāmṛśat
d mā mā gṛhāṇa bhadraṃ te dāso 'haṃ te bṛhannale
d iti vādinam evāśu dhāvantaṃ tarasāgrahīt
d virāṭaputraṃ bībhatsur balavān arimardanaḥ
a so 'rjunena parāmṛṣṭaḥ paryadevayad ārtavat
b mā mā māraya bhadraṃ te muñca mām emi me gṛham
b muñca māṃ muñca muñceti tatpādāv agrahīd bruvan
b darśayitvā tataḥ sarvān adaśat so 'ṅguliṃ nṛpa
b mā bhais tvam iti pārthena prārthitaḥ paryadevayat
c bahulaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ caiva virāṭasya sutas tadā
d uttara uvāca
d śṛṇuyās tvaṃ hi kalyāṇi bṛhannaḍe sumadhyame
d nivartaya rathaṃ śīghraṃ jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyati
d grāmāś caturdaśa tathā pūrṇāś ca dhanagokulaiḥ
d dadāmy etad dhanaṃ tubhyaṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
d aśvānāṃ tu sahasre dve śubhrāṇāṃ hemamālinām
d sarvalakṣaṇayuktānāṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
d uttaraḥ
d suvarṇamaṇimuktānāṃ yad yad icchasi dadmi te
d hastino 'śvān rathān gāvaḥ striyaś ca samalaṃkṛtāḥ
a śātakumbhasya śuddhasya śataṃ niṣkān dadāmi te
a   śreṣṭhasya rajatasya ca
a dadāmi śataniṣkaṃ te muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannale
c maṇīn aṣṭau ca vaiḍūryān hemabaddhān mahāprabhān
a hemadaṇḍapraticchannaṃ rathaṃ yuktaṃ ca suvrajaiḥ
c mattāṃś ca daśa mātaṅgān muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
d ṣaṣṭiṃ svalaṃkṛtāḥ kanyā grāmam ekaṃ dadāmi te
d muñca māṃ tvaṃ bhṛśaṃ dīnaṃ vihvalaṃ bhayakampitam
d gamiṣyāmi puraṃ ṣaṇḍha draṣṭuṃ mātaram arditām
d mātsyasya putro bālo 'haṃ tena cāsmi sukhoṣitaḥ
d mātṛpārśvaśayāno 'ham aspṛṣṭātapavāyumān
d adṛṣṭabalayuddho 'haṃ kutas te kuravaḥ kutaḥ
d mātṛpārśvaṃ gamiṣyāmi muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannale
d pralayārṇavasaṃkāśaṃ dṛśyate kauravaṃ balam
d strīṇāṃ madhye 'ham ajñānād vīryaśauryāṅkitāṃ giram
d uktavān madagarveṇa ko jetuṃ śaknuyāt kurūn
d amuktvā vā yadi nayer mariṣyāmi tavāgrataḥ
d pragṛhyaitad dhanaṃ sarvaṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
d āranālena jīviṣye na me gobhiḥ prayojanam
d arjuna uvāca
d jīvan prāpsyāmi gā hy anyā nivartasva bṛhannaḍe
d yaśo hi kalpāntaśataikasākṣi
d na jīvitaṃ kuñjarakarṇalolam
d kṣitipālasūno bhava raṅgamadhye
d uttara uvāca
d lajjāmahe saṃgararaṅgabhaṅgāt
d yā kīrtir utsarpati dehanāśe
d dhig duḥkhadāṃ mūlavināśinīṃ tām
d vikrīya dehaṃ draviṇena ko nu
d yātrākṛtaṃ devakule karoti
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evamādīni vākyāni vilapantam acetasam
c prahasya puruṣavyāghro rathasyāntikam ānayat
a athainam abravīt pārtho bhayārtaṃ naṣṭacetasam
b arjunaḥ
b ahaṃ yotsyāmi kauravyair hayān saṃyaccha cottara
b ādadānaḥ kimarthaṃ tvaṃ palāyanaparobhavaḥ
b yudhyasva kauravaiḥ sārdhaṃ vijayas te bhaviṣyati
b yasya yantāsmy ahaṃ yuddhe saṃyacchāmi hayottamān
b rājño vā rājaputrasya tasya nityaṃ jayo dhruvaḥ
b sarvathottara yudhyasva yantrā sākaṃ mayā kurūn
b jitvā mahīṃ yaśaḥ prāpya bhokṣyase sakalām imām
b hato 'pi prāpsyase svargaṃ na śreyas te palāyanam
b adya sarvān kurūñ jitvā yathā jayam avāpsyasi
b tathāhaṃ prayatiṣye 'tra sahāyo 'tra mato hy aham
b saṃyacchāmi hayān yasya na sa bhītaḥ palāyati
c yadi notsahase yoddhuṃ śatrubhiḥ śatrukarśana
e ehi me tvaṃ hayān yaccha yudhyamānasya śatrubhiḥ
a prayāhy etad rathānīkaṃ madbāhubalarakṣitaḥ
c apradhṛṣyatamaṃ ghoraṃ guptaṃ vīrair mahārathaiḥ
a mā bhais tvaṃ rājaputrāgrya kṣatriyo 'si paraṃtapa
b kathaṃ puruṣaśārdūla śatrumadhye viṣīdasi
c ahaṃ vai kurubhir yotsyāmy avajeṣyāmi te paśūn
a praviśyaitad rathānīkam apradhṛṣyaṃ durāsadam
c yantā bhūs tvaṃ naraśreṣṭha yotsye 'haṃ kurubhiḥ saha
d śūrān samaracaṇḍāṃś ca nayiṣye yamasādanam
a evaṃ bruvāṇo bībhatsur vairāṭim aparājitaḥ
c samāśvāsya muhūrtaṃ tam uttaraṃ bharatarṣabha
a tata enaṃ viceṣṭantam akāmaṃ bhayapīḍitam
c ratham āropayām āsa pārthaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
d kurūn abhimukhaṃ pārthaḥ prayayau śīghravāhanaḥ
d yathendro dānavān hantuṃ prayāti ca samātaliḥ
d tam āropya rathopasthe vilapantaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
d gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanur ādātum upāyāt tāṃ śamīṃ prati
d uttaraṃ sa samāśvāsya kṛtvā yantāram arjunaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā klībaveṣeṇa rathasthaṃ narapuṃgavam
c śamīm abhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ ratham āropya cottaram
a bhīṣmadroṇamukhās tatra kurūṇāṃ rathasattamāḥ
c vitrastamanasaḥ sarve dhanaṃjayakṛtād bhayāt
a tān avekṣya hatotsāhān utpātān api cādbhutān
c guruḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho bhāradvājo 'bhyabhāṣata
a calāś ca vātāḥ saṃvānti rūkṣāḥ paruṣaniḥsvanāḥ
c bhasmavarṇaprakāśena tamasā saṃvṛtaṃ nabhaḥ
a rūkṣavarṇāś ca jaladā dṛśyante 'dbhutadarśanāḥ
c niḥsaranti ca kośebhyaḥ śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
a śivāś ca vinadanty etā dīptāyāṃ diśi dāruṇāḥ
c hayāś cāśrūṇi muñcanti dhvajāḥ kampanty akampitāḥ
a yādṛśāny atra rūpāṇi saṃdṛśyante bahūny api
c yattā bhavantas tiṣṭhantu syād yuddhaṃ samupasthitam
a rakṣadhvam api cātmānaṃ vyūhadhvaṃ vāhinīm api
c vaiśasaṃ ca pratīkṣadhvaṃ rakṣadhvaṃ cāpi godhanam
d etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ bhīṣmam ālokya cābravīt
d nadīja laṅkeśavanāriketur
d nagāhvayo nāma nagārisūnuḥ
d gatyā sureśaḥ kva cid aṅganeva
d gurur babhāṣe vacanaṃ tad eva
d ity uktvā saṃjñayā droṇas tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ pate
d bhāradvājavacaḥ śrutvā gāṅgeyaḥ saṃjñayābravīt
d atītaṃ cakram asmākaṃ viṣayāntaram āgatāḥ
d atītaḥ samayaś cokto hy asmābhir yaḥ sabhātale
d na bhayaṃ śatrutaḥ kāryaṃ śaṅkāṃ tyaja nararṣabha
d duryodhanam athālokya saṃjñayā droṇa abravīt
d devavratenaivam ukte vacane hitakāriṇā
a eṣa vīro maheṣvāsaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
b gavām arthe hi vikrāntaḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
b nadīja laṅkeśavanāriketur
b nagāhvayo nāma nagārisūnuḥ
b eṣo 'ṅganāveṣadharaḥ kirīṭī
b jitvāva yaṃ neṣyati cādya gā vaḥ
c āgataḥ klībaveṣeṇa pārtho nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ
a sa eṣa pārtho vikrāntaḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c nāyuddhena nivarteta sarvair api marudgaṇaiḥ
d ye jetāro mahīpānām amunā bahavo hatāḥ
d yasmiṃs tejo mahat kṛtsnaṃ nirbharocchvasitaṃ bhavet
d yena me dakṣiṇā dattā baddhvā drupadam ojasā
d viddhvā viyadgataṃ lakṣyaṃ vinirjitya ca pārthivān
d nirjitānena pāñcālī purānena svayaṃvare
d khāṇḍave yena saṃtṛpto vahnir jitvā surāsurān
d pariṇītā subhadrā ca yena nirjitya yādavān
d nirjito yena yuddhena tripurāriḥ smarārdanaḥ
d gatvā triviṣṭapaṃ yena jitendrā dānavā yudhi
d nivātakavacā rājan dānavānāṃ trikoṭayaḥ
d nirjitāḥ kālakeyāś ca hiraṇyapuravāsinaḥ
d yena tvaṃ mocito baddhaś citrasenena tadvane
d yena gatvottaraṃ meror ānināya mahad dhanam
d yājito dharmasūnuś ca nṛpān sarvān vijitya ca
d yasmiñ śauryaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca tejo dhairyaṃ parākramaḥ
d audāryaṃ caiva gāmbhīryaṃ hrīḥ śrīr dharmo dayārjavam
d evamādiguṇopetaḥ so 'yaṃ pārtho na saṃśayaḥ
a kleśitaś ca vane śūro vāsavena ca śikṣitaḥ
c amarṣavaśam āpanno yotsyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a nehāsya pratiyoddhāram ahaṃ paśyāmi kauravāḥ
c mahādevo 'pi pārthena śrūyate yudhi toṣitaḥ
d kirātaveṣapracchanno girau himavati prabhuḥ
d ity evaṃ vādinaṃ droṇaṃ karṇaḥ kruddho 'bravīd vacaḥ
 karṇa uvāca
a sadā bhavān phalgunasya guṇair asmān vikatthase
c na cārjunaḥ kalā pūrṇā mama duryodhanasya vā
 duryodhana uvāca
a yady eṣa pārtho rādheya kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ bhaven mama
c jñātāḥ punaś cariṣyanti dvādaśānyān hi vatsarān
a athaiṣa kaś cid evānyaḥ klībaveṣeṇa mānavaḥ
c śarair enaṃ suniśitaiḥ pātayiṣyāmi bhūtale
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasmin bruvati tad vākyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭre paraṃtape
c bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpo drauṇiḥ pauruṣaṃ tad apūjayan
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tāṃ śamīm upasaṃgamya pārtho vairāṭim abravīt
c sukumāraṃ samājñātaṃ saṃgrāme nātikovidam
d ehi bhūmiṃjayāruhya vairāṭe mahatīṃ śamīm
a samādiṣṭo mayā kṣipraṃ dhanūṃṣy avaharottara
c nemāni hi tvadīyāni soḍhuṃ śakṣyanti me balam
a bhāraṃ vāpi guruṃ hartuṃ kuñjaraṃ vā pramarditum
c mama vā bāhuvikṣepaṃ śatrūn iha vijeṣyataḥ
d naibhiḥ kāmam ahaṃ kartuṃ karma vaijayikaṃ tv iha
d atisūkṣmāṇi hrasvāni sarvāṇi ca mṛdūni ca
d āyudhāni mahābāho tavaitāni paraṃtapa
a tasmād bhūmiṃjayāroha śamīm etāṃ palāśinīm
c asyāṃ hi pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ dhanūṃṣi nihitāny uta
a yudhiṣṭhirasya bhīmasya bībhatsor yamayos tathā
c dhvajāḥ śarāś ca śūrāṇāṃ divyāni kavacāni ca
a atra caitan mahāvīryaṃ dhanuḥ pārthasya gāṇḍivam
c ekaṃ śatasahasreṇa saṃmitaṃ rāṣṭravardhanam
a vyāyāmasaham atyarthaṃ tṛṇarājasamaṃ mahat
c sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ śatrusaṃbādhakārakam
a suvarṇavikṛtaṃ divyaṃ ślakṣṇam āyatam avraṇam
c alaṃ bhāraṃ guruṃ voḍhuṃ dāruṇaṃ cārudarśanam
e tādṛśāny eva sarvāṇi balavanti dṛḍhāni ca
f pradhānāni viśiṣṭāni durdarśāni bhavanty uta
f arjunenaivam uktas tu vairāṭiḥ pratyabhāṣata
 uttara uvāca
a asmin vṛkṣe kilodbaddhaṃ śarīram iti naḥ śrutam
c tad ahaṃ rājaputraḥ san spṛśeyaṃ pāṇinā katham
a naivaṃvidhaṃ mayā yuktam ālabdhuṃ kṣatrayoninā
c mahatā rājaputreṇa mantrayajñavidā satā
d spṛśāmīha śarīraṃ ced apy asyāṃ śokavarjitaḥ
a spṛṣṭavantaṃ śarīraṃ māṃ śavavāham ivāśucim
c kathaṃ vā vyavahāryaṃ vai kurvīthās tvaṃ bṛhannaḍe
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tam uvāca tataḥ śūraḥ pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
d dāyādaṃ sarvamatsyānāṃ kule jātaṃ viśāradam
d jānāmi tvāṃ mahāprājña śubhaṃ jātyā kulena ca
d kathaṃ nu pāpakaṃ karma brūyāṃ tvāhaṃ paraṃtapa
 bṛhannaḍovāca
a vyavahāryaś ca rājendra śuciś caiva bhaviṣyasi
c dhanūṃṣy etāni mā bhais tvaṃ śarīraṃ nātra vidyate
a dāyādaṃ matsyarājasya kule jātaṃ manasvinam
c kathaṃ tvā ninditaṃ karma kārayeyaṃ nṛpātmaja
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ sa pārthena rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalī
c āruroha śamīvṛkṣaṃ vairāṭir avaśas tadā
a tam anvaśāsac chatrughno rathe tiṣṭhan dhanaṃjayaḥ
b avāropaya vṛkṣāgrād dhanūṃṣy etāni mā bibhaḥ
c pariveṣṭanam eteṣāṃ kṣipraṃ caiva vyapānuda
d so 'pahṛtya mahārhāṇi dhanūṃṣi pṛthuvakṣasām
d pariveṣṭanapatrāṇi vimucya samupānayat
a tathā saṃnahanāny eṣāṃ parimucya samantataḥ
c apaśyad gāṇḍivaṃ tatra caturbhir aparaiḥ saha
a teṣāṃ vimucyamānānāṃ dhanuṣām arkavarcasām
c viniśceruḥ prabhā divyā grahāṇām udayeṣv iva
a sa teṣāṃ rūpam ālokya bhoginām iva jṛmbhatām
c hṛṣṭaromā bhayodvignaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata
c   pravepitatanus tadā
c arjunena samāśvastaḥ
c   kiṃ cid dhṛṣṭo nṛpātmajaḥ
c teṣāṃ saṃdarśanābhyāsaṃ sparśābhyāsaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c āmīlya punar unmīlya spṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā cakāra saḥ
c samyag dṛṣṭvā tadāśvastaḥ
d tad upaśrutya śatrughnaḥ sa tadārjunam abravīt
d sārathe kim idaṃ śete nāgendro vāpi vā dhanuḥ
a saṃspṛśya tāni cāpāni bhānumanti bṛhanti ca
c vairāṭir arjunaṃ rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt
 uttara uvāca
 na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ citraṃ dhanuṣo rūpam īdṛśam
a bindavo jātarūpasya śataṃ yasmin nipātitāḥ
c sahasrakoṭi sauvarṇāḥ kasyaitad dhanur uttamam
a vāraṇā yasya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe bhāsanti daṃśitāḥ
c supārśvaṃ sugrahaṃ caiva kasyaitad dhanuruttamam
a tapanīyasya śuddhasya ṣaṣṭir yasyendragopakāḥ
c pṛṣṭhe vibhaktāḥ śobhante kasyaitad dhanur uttamam
a sūryā yatra ca sauvarṇās trayo bhāsanti daṃśitāḥ
c tejasā prajvalanto hi kasyaitad dhanur uttamam
a śālabhā yatra sauvarṇās tapanīyavicitritāḥ
c suvarṇamaṇicitraṃ ca kasyaitad dhanur uttamam
a ime ca kasya nārācāḥ sahasrā lomavāhinaḥ
c samantāt kaladhautāgrā upāsaṅge hiraṇmaye
a vipāṭhāḥ pṛthavaḥ kasya gārdhrapatrāḥ śilāśitāḥ
c hāridravarṇāḥ sunasāḥ pītāḥ sarvāyasāḥ śarāḥ
a kasyāyam asitāvāpaḥ pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥ
c varāhakarṇavyāmiśraḥ śarān dhārayate daśa
a kasyeme pṛthavo dīrghāḥ sarvapāraśavāḥ śarāḥ
c śatāni sapta tiṣṭhanti nārācā rudhirāśanāḥ
a kasyeme śukapatrābhaiḥ pūrvair ardhaiḥ suvāsasaḥ
c uttarair āyasaiḥ pītair hemapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
d gurubhārasaho divyaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥ
d hemapuṅkho gārdhapatraḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥ
a kasyāyaṃ sāyako dīrghaḥ śilīpṛṣṭhaḥ śilīmukhaḥ
c vaiyāghrakośe nihito hemacitratsarur mahān
a suphalaś citrakośaś ca kiṅkiṇīsāyako mahān
c kasya hematsarur divyaḥ khaḍgaḥ paramanirvraṇaḥ
a kasyāyaṃ vimalaḥ khaḍgo gavye kośe samarpitaḥ
c hematsarur anādhṛṣyo naiṣadhyo bhārasādhanaḥ
a kasya pāñcanakhe kośe sāyako hemavigrahaḥ
c pramāṇarūpasaṃpannaḥ pīta ākāśasaṃnibhaḥ
a kasya hemamaye kośe sutapte pāvakaprabhe
c nistriṃśo 'yaṃ guruḥ pītaḥ saikyaḥ paramanirvraṇaḥ
d kasyāyam asitaḥ khaḍgo hemabindubhir āvṛtaḥ
d āśīviṣasamasparśaḥ parakāyaprabhedanaḥ
d gurubhārasaho divyaḥ sapatnānāṃ bhayapradaḥ
d uttaraḥ
d sārathe kim idaṃ divyaṃ nāgo vā yadi vā dhanuḥ
d sauvarṇāny atra padmāni śatapatrāṇi bhāgaśaḥ
d kuśāgnipratitaptāni bhānumanti bṛhanti ca
d a bindavaś cātra sauvarṇā maṇiprotāḥ samantataḥ
d śaśisūryaprabhāḥ pṛṣṭhe bhānti rukmapariṣkṛtāḥ
d pughpāṇy atra suvarṇāni śatapatrāṇi bhāgaśaḥ
d vismāpanīyarūpaṃ ca bhīmaṃ bhīmapradarśanam
d nīlotpalanibhaṃ kasya śātakumbhapariṣkṛtam
d ab ṛṣabhā yasya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti śṛṅgiṇaḥ
d tālapramāṇaṃ kasyedaṃ maṇirukmavibhūṣitam
d hāṭakasya suvarṇasya yasmiñ śākhāmṛgā daśa
d durānamaṃ mahad dīrghaṃ surūpaṃ duṣpradharṣaṇam
d kasyedam īdṛśaṃ citraṃ dhanuḥ sarve ca daṃsitāḥ
d candrārkavimalā bhāsaḥ surūpāḥ supradarśanāḥ
d haṃsāḥ pṛṣṭhe śritā yasya kuśāgnipratimārciṣaḥ
d śārṅgagāṇḍīvasadṛśaṃ kasyedaṃ sārathe dhanuḥ
d caturthaṃ kāñcanavapur bhāti vidyudgaṇopamam
d nīlotpalitam acchidraṃ jātarūpaprabhaṃ dhanuḥ
d matsyā yasya hiraṇyasya pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti saṃcitāḥ
d śakracāpopamaṃ divyaṃ kasyedaṃ sārathe dhanuḥ
d ucchritaṃ phaṇivad dīrghaṃ sāravattvād durānamam
d c sahasragodhāḥ sauvarṇā dvīpinaś ca caturdaśa
d barhiṇaś cātra sauvarṇāḥ śatacandrārkabhūṣaṇāḥ
d jāmbūnadavicitrāṅgaṃ kasyedaṃ pañcamaṃ dhanuḥ
d ab kasyeme kṣuranārācāḥ sahasraṃ lomavāpinaḥ
d pakṣiṇas tīkṣṇatuṇḍāgrāḥ kasyeme niśitāḥ śarāḥ
d ab vipāṭāḥ pṛthavaḥ kasya gṛdhrapatrārdhavājitāḥ
d cab varāhakarṇās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ kasyeme rucirāḥ śarāḥ
d vajrāśanisamasparśā vaiśvānarasamārciṣaḥ
d suvarṇapuṅkhās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ kasya saptaśataṃ śarāḥ
d a kasyāyaṃ sāyako dīrgho gavye kośe ca daṃsitaḥ
d kasya daṇḍo dṛḍhaḥ ślakṣṇo ruciro 'yaṃ prakāśate
d c vaiyāghrakośaḥ kasyāyaṃ divyaḥ khaḍgo mahāprabhaḥ
d ab kasyāyam asir āvāpe pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥ
d ab kasyāyaṃ nirmalaḥ khaḍgo dvīpicarmādhivāsitaḥ
d nīlotpalasavarṇo 'yaṃ kasya khaḍgaḥ pṛthur mahān
d mṛgendracarmāvasitas tīkṣṇadhāraḥ sunirmalaḥ
d ṛṣabhājinakośas tu kasya khaḍgo mahān ayam
d yasyāpidhāne dṛśyante sūryāḥ pañca pariṣkṛtāḥ
d a kasyāyaṃ vipulaḥ khaḍgaḥ śṛṅgatsarumanoharaḥ
d nihitaḥ pārṣate kośe tailadhautaḥ samāhitaḥ
d c pramāṇavarṇayuktaś ca kasya khaḍgo mahān ayam
d naitena pratividdhaḥ sañ jīvet kaś cana kuñjaraḥ
d viprakṣiptās tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrā upāsaṅge hiraṇmaye
d hāridravarṇāḥ kasyeme śitāḥ pañcaśataṃ śarāḥ
d āśīviṣasamasparśā gatau cājihmagā dṛḍhāḥ
d yasyāpidhāne dṛśyante śārdūlāḥ kāñcanāḥ śubhāḥ
a nirdiśasva yathātattvaṃ mayā pṛṣṭā bṛhannaḍe
c vismayo me paro jāto dṛṣṭvā sarvam idaṃ mahat
 bṛhannaḍovāca
 vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
 uttareṇaivam uktas tu pārtho vairāṭim abravīt
 mṛdvyā pratyāyayan vācā bhītaṃ śaṅkāvaśaṃ gatam
a yan māṃ pūrvam ihāpṛcchaḥ śatrusenānibarhaṇam
c gāṇḍīvam etat pārthasya lokeṣu viditaṃ dhanuḥ
d abhedyam ajaraṃ śrīmad divyam acchedyam avraṇam
a sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ śātakumbhapariṣkṛtam

a yat tac chatasahasreṇa saṃmitaṃ rāṣṭravardhanam
c yena devān manuṣyāṃś ca pārtho viṣahate mṛdhe
d citram uccāvacair varṇaiḥ ślakṣṇam āyatam avraṇam
a devadānavagandharvaiḥ pūjitaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c etad varṣasahasraṃ tu brahmā pūrvam adhārayat
a tato 'nantaram evātha prajāpatir adhārayat
c trīṇi pañcaśataṃ caiva śakro 'śīti ca pañca ca
a somaḥ pañcaśataṃ rājā tathaiva varuṇaḥ śatam
b tasmāc ca varuṇād agniḥ premṇā prāhṛtya tac chubham
b agninā pratibhāvyena dattaṃ pārthāya gāṇḍivam
c pārthaḥ pañca ca ṣaṣṭiṃ ca varṣāṇi śvetavāhanaḥ
a mahāvīryaṃ mahad divyam etat tad dhanur uttamam
b etan mām anusaṃprāptaṃ varuṇāc cārudarśanam
b nīlotpalanibhaṃ rājñaḥ kauravyasya mahātmanaḥ
b bindavaś cāsya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe sādhu niyojitāḥ
c pūjitaṃ suramartyeṣu bibharti paramaṃ vapuḥ
d tālapramāṇaṃ bhīmasya maṇirukmavibhūṣitam
d durānamaṃ mahad dīrghaṃ surūpaṃ duṣpradharṣaṇam
a supārśvaṃ bhīmasenasya jātarūpagrahaṃ dhanuḥ
b sahasragodhā hairaṇyā dvīpinaś ca caturdaśa
b ṛṣabhāś cāpi sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti śṛṅgiṇaḥ
c yena pārtho 'jayat kṛtsnāṃ diśaṃ prācīṃ paraṃtapaḥ
d pṛṣṭhe vibhaktāḥ śobhante kuśāgnipratibhāvitāḥ
a indragopakacitraṃ ca yad etac cāruvigraham
c rājño yudhiṣṭhirasyaitad vairāṭe dhanur uttamam
a sūryā yasmiṃs tu sauvarṇāḥ prabhāsante prabhāsinaḥ
c tejasā prajvalanto vai nakulasyaitad āyudham
a śalabhā yatra sauvarṇās tapanīyavicitritāḥ
c etan mādrīsutasyāpi sahadevasya kārmukam
d tapanīyavicitraṃ ca vairāṭe nākulaṃ dhanuḥ
a ye tv ime kṣurasaṃkāśāḥ sahasrā lomavāhinaḥ
c ete 'rjunasya vairāṭe śarāḥ sarpaviṣopamāḥ
a ete jvalantaḥ saṃgrāme tejasā śīghragāminaḥ
c bhavanti vīrasyākṣayyā vyūhataḥ samare ripūn
d ghorāgrā dīrgharūpāś ca girīṇām api dāraṇāḥ
a ye ceme pṛthavo dīrghāś candrabimbārdhadarśanāḥ
c ete bhīmasya niśitā ripukṣayakarāḥ śarāḥ
a hāridravarṇā ye tv ete hemapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥ
c nakulasya kalāpo 'yaṃ pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥ
a yenāsau vyajayat kṛtsnāṃ pratīcīṃ diśam āhave
c kalāpo hy eṣa tasyāsīn mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥ
a ye tv ime bhāskarākārāḥ sarvapāraśavāḥ śarāḥ
c ete citrāḥ kriyopetāḥ sahadevasya dhīmataḥ
a ye tv ime niśitāḥ pītāḥ pṛthavo dīrghavāsasaḥ
c hemapuṅkhās triparvāṇo rājña ete mahāśarāḥ
a yas tv ayaṃ sāyako dīrghaḥ śilīpṛṣṭhaḥ śilīmukhaḥ
c arjunasyaiṣa saṃgrāme gurubhārasaho dṛḍhaḥ
a vaiyāghrakośas tu mahān bhīmasenasya sāyakaḥ
c gurubhārasaho divyaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥ
a suphalaś citrakośaś ca hematsarur anuttamaḥ
c nistriṃśaḥ kauravasyaiṣa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
a yas tu pāñcanakhe kośe nihitaś citrasevane
c nakulasyaiṣa nistriṃśo gurubhārasaho dṛḍhaḥ
a yas tv ayaṃ vimalaḥ khaḍgo gavye kośe samarpitaḥ
c sahadevasya viddhy enaṃ sarvabhārasahaṃ dṛḍham
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d evam ākhyātavāṃs tatra svāyudhāni paraṃtapaḥ
d virāṭaputrāya tadā pārthaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
d a barhiṇaś cātra sauvarṇāḥ śatacandrārkabhūṣaṇāḥ
d nakulasya dhanus tv etan mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥ
d etena sadṛśaṃ citraṃ dhanuś caitad yavīyasaḥ
d a hāridravarṇaṃ rājñaś ca kauravyasya mahātmanaḥ
d vipāṭā bhīmasenasya girīṇām api dāraṇāḥ
d suprabhāḥ sumahākāyās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ sukṛtā dṛḍhāḥ
d bhīmena prahitā hy ete vāraṇānāṃ nivāraṇāḥ
d suvarṇavarṇā rucirāḥ kāladaṇḍopamāḥ śubhāḥ
d c nakulasya śarā hy ete vajrāśanisamaprabhāḥ
d yāṃś ca tvaṃ pṛcchase dīrghān samadhārān samāhitān
d d varāhakarṇās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ sahadevasya te śarāḥ
d a yas tv ayaṃ sāyako divyo gavye kośe ca daṃsitaḥ
d d pārthasyāstram idaṃ ghoraṃ sarvabhārasahaṃ mahat
d yas tv ayaṃ nirmalaḥ khaḍgo dvīpicarmaṇi daṃsitaḥ
d rājño yudhiṣṭhirasyāyaṃ kuntīputrasya dhīmataḥ
d ad vaiyāghrakośo bhīmasya pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥ
d vāraṇānāṃ sudṛptānāṃ śikṣitaḥ skandhaśātane
d nīlotpalasavarṇābhaḥ khaḍgaḥ pārthasya dhīmataḥ
d mṛgendracarmapihitas tīkṣṇadhāraḥ samāhitaḥ
d darśanīyaḥ sutīkṣṇāgraḥ kuntīputrasya dhīmataḥ
d c arjunasyaiṣa nistriṃśaḥ parasainyāgradūṣaṇaḥ
d a yas tv ayaṃ pārṣate kośe prakṣipto ruciratsaruḥ
d c nakulasyaiṣa nistriṃśo vaiśvānarasamaprabhaḥ
d a yas tv ayaṃ piṅgalaḥ khaḍgaś citro maṇimayatsaruḥ
d cd sahadevasya khaḍgo 'yaṃ bhārasāho 'tidaṃsitaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d bhīmasyāyaṃ mahādaṇḍaḥ sarvāmitravināśanaḥ
d bhedato hy arjunas tūrṇaṃ kathayām āsa tattvataḥ
d āyudhāni kalāpāṃś ca nistriṃśāṃś cātulaprabhān
d anyat tu sahadevasya dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ mahaujasaḥ
d kvāsau pracchannavāsānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
d nyastāny atra mahārhāṇi vratasiddhim upeyuṣām
d ity uttaraṃ tu tat sarvam arjunas tattvato 'bravīt
 uttara uvāca
a suvarṇavikṛtānīmāny āyudhāni mahātmanām
c rucirāṇi prakāśante pārthānām āśukāriṇām
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d etasminn antare pārthaṃ mūḍhātmā na vyajānata
d virāṭaputraḥ pramukhe papraccha punar eva tu
a kva nu svid arjunaḥ pārthaḥ kauravyo vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d kva nu te pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ saṃgrāmeṣv aparājitāḥ
d eṣām imāni divyāni śriyā dīvyanti bhānti ca
d kasmin vasanti te deśe dharmajñā bandhuvatsalāḥ
d kva dharmarājaḥ kauravyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d bhīmasenārjunau cāpi sarve te mātulā mama
d nakulaḥ sahadevo vā sarvāstrakuśalo raṇe
d dharmaśīlaś ca dharmātmā dharmavān dharmavit sudhīḥ
d dharmādhyakṣo dharmavrato dharmajño dharmamūrtimān
d dharmaniṣṭho dharmakartā dharmagoptā sudharmakṛt
d satyārjavakṣamādhāro ghṛṇī dharmaparāyaṇaḥ
a sarva eva mahātmānaḥ sarvāmitravināśanāḥ
c rājyam akṣaiḥ parākīrya na śrūyante kadā cana
a draupadī kva ca pāñcālī strīratnam iti viśrutā
c jitān akṣais tadā kṛṣṇā tān evānvagamad vanam
d utsṛjya dharmarājyaṃ te na śrūyante vanaṃ gatāḥ
d pāṇḍavān yadi jānīṣe kva nu te dharmacāriṇaḥ
d kva cādya nivasantīti satyaṃ brūhi bṛhannale
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tataḥ prahasya bībhatsuḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
d uvāca rājaputraṃ tam uttaraṃ śṛṇu me vacaḥ
d kimartham āgatāny atra śastrāstrāṇi mahātmanām
d kathaṃ jñātāni bhavatā tathā me brūhi śobhane
d tataḥ prahasya kaunteyo rājaputram uvāca ha
d mā bhais tvaṃ rājaśārdūla sarvaṃ te varṇayāmy aham
d nātra bhetavyam adyāpi rājaputra yathā tathā
d vayaṃ te pāṇḍavā nāma vanavāsasya pāragāḥ
d atīte dvādaśe varṣe channavāsam ihoṣitāḥ
d tasmād aśaṅkitamanāḥ śṛṇuṣva mahitottara
 arjuna uvāca
a aham asmy arjunaḥ pārthaḥ sabhāstāro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c ballavo bhīmasenas tu pitus te rasapācakaḥ
a aśvabandho 'tha nakulaḥ sahadevas tu gokule
c sairandhrīṃ draupadīṃ viddhi yatkṛte kīcakā hatāḥ
d bhīmasenena durvṛttaḥ saha bhrātṛbhir āhave
d śrutvaitad vacanaṃ jiṣṇor vismayasphāritekṣaṇaḥ
d paśyann animiṣaḥ pārthaṃ śanair vācam uvāca ha
 uttara uvāca
a daśa pārthasya nāmāni yāni pūrvaṃ śrutāni me
c prabrūyās tāni yadi me śraddadhyāṃ sarvam eva te
 arjuna uvāca
a hanta te 'haṃ samācakṣe daśa nāmāni yāni me
b vairāṭe śṛṇu tāni tvaṃ yāni pūrvaṃ śrutāni te
b ekāgramānaso bhūtvā śṛṇu sarvaṃ samāhitaḥ
b īśāno vidadhe devas tridivasyeśvaro divi
b tāni loke pravṛttāni vairāṭe śṛṇu tattvataḥ
c arjunaḥ phalguno jiṣṇuḥ kirīṭī śvetavāhanaḥ
e bībhatsur vijayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ
f etāni mama nāmāni sthāpitāni surottamaiḥ
 uttara uvāca
 guṇato daśa nāmāni samavetāni pāṇḍave
 caranti loke khyātāni viditāni mamānagha
a kenāsi vijayo nāma kenāsi śvetavāhanaḥ
c kirīṭī nāma kenāsi savyasācī kathaṃ bhavān
a arjunaḥ phalguno jiṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇo bībhatsur eva ca
c dhanaṃjayaś ca kenāsi prabrūhi mama tattvataḥ
e śrutā me tasya vīrasya kevalā nāmahetavaḥ
f tatsarvaṃ yadi me brūyāḥ śraddadhyāṃ sarvam eva te
f itas tataś calaty etan mano me cañcalaṃ tvayi
f arjuno vā bhavān neti vada śīghraṃ bṛhannale
 arjuna uvāca
a sarvāñ janapadāñ jitvā vittam ācchidya kevalam
c madhye dhanasya tiṣṭhāmi tenāhur māṃ dhanaṃjayam
a abhiprayāmi saṃgrāme yad ahaṃ yuddhadurmadān
c nājitvā vinivartāmi tena māṃ vijayaṃ viduḥ
a śvetāḥ kāñcanasaṃnāhā rathe yujyanti me hayāḥ
c saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya tenāhaṃ śvetavāhanaḥ
d kirīṭaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ bhrājate me śirogatam
d raṇamadhye rathasthasya sūryapāvakasaṃnibham
a uttarābhyāṃ ca pūrvābhyāṃ phalgunībhyām ahaṃ divā
c jāto himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe tena māṃ phalgunaṃ viduḥ
d yo mamāṅge vraṇaṃ kuryān mama jyeṣṭhasya paśyataḥ
d yudhiṣṭhirasya rudhiraṃ darśayed vā kadā cana
d parābhavam ahaṃ tasya kule kuryāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
a purā śakreṇa me dattaṃ yudhyato dānavarṣabhaiḥ
c kirīṭaṃ mūrdhni sūryābhaṃ tena māhuḥ kirīṭinam
d acchedyaṃ ruciraṃ citraṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
d indradattam anāhāryaṃ
a na kuryāṃ karma bībhatsaṃ yudhyamānaḥ kathaṃ cana
c tena devamanuṣyeṣu bībhatsur iti māṃ viduḥ
a ubhau me dakṣiṇau pāṇī gāṇḍīvasya vikarṣaṇe
b dhanuṣāhaṃ samāyuktaḥ śaravarṣaṃ sṛjāmi ca
b bhujau me bhavataḥ saṃkhye parasainyavināśane
c tena devamanuṣyeṣu savyasācīti māṃ viduḥ
a pṛthivyāṃ caturantāyāṃ varṇo me durlabhaḥ samaḥ
c karomi karma śuklaṃ ca tena mām arjunaṃ viduḥ
a ahaṃ durāpo durdharṣo damanaḥ pākaśāsaniḥ
c tena devamanuṣyeṣu jiṣṇunāmāsmi viśrutaḥ
d mātā mama pṛthā nāma tena māṃ pārtham abruvan
d devadānavagandharvān piśācoragarākṣasān
d ahaṃ purā raṇe jitvā khāṇḍave 'gnim atarpayam
d hutāśanaṃ tarpayitvā sahitaḥ śārṅgadhanvanā
d triviṣṭapagatau dṛṣṭvā pitāmahamaheśvarau
d mūrcchayā patitaṃ bhūmāv āgatau devasattamau
d dṛṣṭvā tau varadau devau saṃjñāṃ labdhvotthitaṃ purā
d mūrdhnābhipraṇataṃ bhūmau tau tadā varadau varau
d kṛṣṇety ekādaśaṃ nāma prītyā me tatra cakratuḥ
d tuṣṭau ca mama vīryeṇa karmaṇā cābhirādhitau
d sarvadevaiḥ parivṛtau bhūyo māṃ svayam ūcatuḥ
d varaṃ tāta vṛṇīṣveti yat prārthayasi pāṇḍava
d tato 'ham astrāṇy alabhaṃ divyāni ca dṛḍhāni ca
d brāhmaṃ pāśupataṃ caiva sthūṇākarṇaṃ ca durjayam
d aindraṃ vāruṇam āgneyaṃ vāyavyam atha vaiṣṇavam
d tato 'ham ajayaṃ bhūyo rathenaindreṇa durjayān
d mātaliṃ sārathiṃ kṛtvā nivātakavacān raṇe
d avadhyakavacān devair varadattān mahāsurān
d tisraḥ koṭīr dānavānāṃ saṃyugeṣv anivartinām
d eko nirjitya saṃgrāme bhūyo devān atoṣayam
d tato me bhagavān indraḥ kirīṭam adadāt svayam
d devāś ca śaṅkham adaduḥ śatrusainyanivāraṇam
d ahaṃ pāre samudrasya hiraṇyapuravāsinām
d hatvā ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi jayaṃ saṃprāptavān aham
d asaṃbhrānto rathe tiṣṭhan sahasreṣu śateṣu ca
d śatrumadhye durādharṣo na muhyanti ca me diśaḥ
d ahaṃ gandharvarājena hriyamāṇaṃ suyodhanam
d bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ tāta gandharvaiḥ samare jitam
d caturdaśa sahasrāṇi hatvā cainam amocayam
d mā bhair vigatasaṃtrāsaḥ kurūn etān samāgatān
d suyodhanasya miṣataḥ karṇasya ca kṛpasya ca
d pitāmahasya bhīṣmasya drauṇer droṇasya ca svayam
d sarvān eva kurūñ jitvā pratyāneṣyāmi te paśūn
a kṛṣṇa ity eva daśamaṃ nāma cakre pitā mama
c kṛṣṇāvadātasya sataḥ priyatvād bālakasya vai
d sthito 'smi yattaḥ saṃgrāme vairāṭe vyetu te bhayam
d etac chrutvā prahṛṣṭātmā vismayotphullalocanaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ pārthaṃ sa vairāṭir abhyavādayad antikāt
b tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vairāṭiḥ pārṣatottama
b prahṛṣṭaromā hṛṣṭo 'bhūd vismayotphullalocanaḥ
b taṃ prekṣya vai mahātmānam arjunaṃ matsyanandanaḥ
b prāñjaliś cābhivādyātha idaṃ vacanam abravīt
c ahaṃ bhūmiṃjayo nāma nāmnāham api cottaraḥ
a diṣṭyā tvāṃ pārtha paśyāmi svāgataṃ te dhanaṃjaya
c lohitākṣa mahābāho nāgarājakaropama
e yad ajñānād avocaṃ tvāṃ kṣantum arhasi tan mama
e   pramādena narottama
e akṛtvā hṛdaye sarvaṃ
a yatas tvayā kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ vicitraṃ karma duṣkaram
c ato bhayaṃ vyatītaṃ me prītiś ca paramā tvayi
d dāso 'haṃ te bhaviṣyāmi paśya mām anukampayā
d yā pratijñā kṛtā pūrvaṃ tava sārathyakāraṇāt
d manaḥsvāsthyaṃ ca me jātaṃ jātaṃ bhāgyaṃ ca me mahat
d yad ajñānād avocaṃ tvāṃ vismartavyaṃ dhanaṃjaya
d yāvad arvāg ahaṃ vidyāṃ tvāṃ na tattvena bhārata
d tāvan me 'bhūd bhayaṃ tāta kurubhyo nātra saṃśayaḥ
d yadā tv ajñāsiṣam ahaṃ channaṃ tattvena bhārata
d vismito 'smi mahāsattva sarvaśatrūn vināśaya
d tvadvākyajalasaṃsiktam utpalaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama
d gharmābhitaptaṃ vijale mlānapadmam iva hrade
d neyaṃ pratijñā pūrṇā me harṣaś cārjuna jāyate
d devendratanayasyeha sārathiḥ syāṃ mahāmṛdhe
d iti pūrvaṃ kṛtāsmābhiḥ pratijñā yuddhadurmada
d pratijñā mama saṃpūrṇā tava sārathyakāraṇāt
d na smartavyaṃ tvayā vīra lokapālasamo hy asi
d prasādaye mahābāho pūrvaṃ yat skhalitaṃ mama
d tāvan me 'bhūd bhayaṃ pārtha yāvat tvāṃ nāvalokaye
d vibhayo darśanāt tubhyaṃ kas tvāṃ yotsyej jijīviṣuḥ
d evaṃ prahṛṣṭaromāsau brūte matsyasuto 'rjunam
d prāñjaliḥ samupātiṣṭhad vāsavo druhiṇaṃ yathā
d tato 'rjunaḥ samāśvāsya matsyaṃ vairāṭim abravīt
d uvāca muditaḥ kāle tamo hatvā yathā raviḥ
d āśvāsya putraṃ matsyasya dhanur visphārya gāṇḍivam
d prekṣaṇīyatamo bhūtvā tasthau dīpto ravir yathā
 uttara uvāca
a āsthāya vipulaṃ vīra rathaṃ sārathinā mayā
c katamaṃ yāsyase 'nīkam ukto yāsyāmy ahaṃ tvayā
 arjuna uvāca
a prīto 'smi puruṣavyāghra na bhayaṃ vidyate tava

 uttara uvāca
a bibhemi nāham eteṣāṃ jānāmi tvāṃ sthiraṃ yudhi

d yamapāśikuberebhyo droṇabhīṣmaśatād api
a idaṃ tu cintayann eva parimuhyāmi kevalam

 arjuna uvāca
a bhrātur niyogāj jyeṣṭhasya saṃvatsaram idaṃ vratam
c carāmi brahmacaryaṃ vai satyam etad bravīmi te
a nāsmi klībo mahābāho paravān dharmasaṃyutaḥ
b purāham ājñayā bhrātur jyeṣṭhasyāhaṃ surālayam
b prāptavān urvaśīṃ dṛṣṭvā sudharmāyām ahaṃ tadā
b nṛtyantīṃ paramaṃ rūpaṃ bibhratīṃ vajrisaṃnidhau

b urvaśīśāpasaṃbhūtaṃ klaibyaṃ māṃ samupasthitam
c samāptavratam uttīrṇaṃ viddhi māṃ tvaṃ nṛpātmaja
 uttara uvāca
a paramo 'nugraho me 'dya yat pratarko na me vṛthā

a sahāyavān asmi raṇe yudhyeyam amarair api

a yasya yāte na paśyanti bhūmau prāptaṃ padaṃ padam

c vāmaṃ sainyasya manye taṃ javena balavattaram

 tato rathād avaskandya vīryavān arimardanaḥ

c citre dundubhisaṃnāde pratyamuñcat tale śubhe
d indradatte ca te divye uddhṛtyāmucya kuṇḍale
a kṛṣṇān bhaṅgīmataḥ keśāñ śvetenodgrathya vāsasā

b abhyupeyur mahābhāgaṃ mahāstrāṇi tadārjunam

d uttara uvāca
d ekas tvaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha bahūn etān mahārathān
d kathaṃ jeṣyasi saṃgrāme sarvaśastrāstrapāragān
d asahāyo 'si kaunteya sasahāyāś ca kauravāḥ

d ata eva mahābāho bhītas tiṣṭhāmi te 'grataḥ

d yudhyamānasya me vīra gandharvaiḥ sumahābalaiḥ
d sahāyo ghoṣayātrāyāṃ kas tadāsīt sakhā mama
d tathā pratibhaye tasmin devadānavasaṃkule
d khāṇḍave yudhyamānasya kas tadāsīt sakhā mama
d nivātakavacaiḥ sārdhaṃ paulomaiś ca mahābalaiḥ

d upajīvya guruṃ droṇaṃ śakraṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ yamam

d pinākapāṇinaṃ caiva katham etān na yodhaye

 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uttaraṃ sārathiṃ kṛtvā śamīṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam
c āyudhaṃ sarvam ādāya tataḥ prāyād dhanaṃjayaḥ
a dhvajaṃ siṃhaṃ rathāt tasmād apanīya mahārathaḥ
c praṇidhāya śamīmūle prāyād uttarasārathiḥ
a daivīṃ māyāṃ rathe yuktvā vihitāṃ viśvakarmaṇā
c kāñcanaṃ siṃhalāṅgūlaṃ dhvajaṃ vānaralakṣaṇam
a manasā cintayām āsa prasādaṃ pāvakasya ca
c sa ca tac cintitaṃ jñātvā dhvaje bhūtāny acodayat
d dhvaje vānaram ucchritya gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥ
d uttasthau cottaras tāta smṛtvā punar ihāgataḥ
d taṃ samāśvāsya bībhatsur abhiyātuṃ pratatvare
a sapatākaṃ vicitrāṅgaṃ sopāsaṅgaṃ mahārathaḥ
b khāt papāta rathe tūrṇaṃ divyarūpaṃ manoramam
b rathaṃ tam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā dakṣiṇaṃ prākarot tadā
c ratham āsthāya bībhatsuḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
a baddhāsiḥ satanutrāṇaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ
c tataḥ prāyād udīcīṃ sa kapipravaraketanaḥ
d sainyābhyāśam anuprāpya gṛhītvā bhīmam uttamam
a svanavantaṃ mahāśaṅkhaṃ balavān arimardanaḥ
c prādhamad balam āsthāya dviṣatāṃ lomaharṣaṇam
d śaśāṅkakundadhavalaṃ mukhe nikṣipya vāsaviḥ
d ucchvasad gaṇḍayugulaṃ sirāḷyācitaphālakam
d āyattanimnanayanaṃ hrasvasthūlaśirodharam
