d yāvat svaśaktisāmagryaṃ trailokyaṃ kṣobhayann iva
d marudbhir daśabhiś caiva prādhmāpayad ariṃdamaḥ
d śaṅkhaśabdo 'sya so 'tyarthaṃ śrūyate kālameghavat
d tasya śaṅkhasya śabdena dhanuṣo nisvanena ca
d vānarasya ca nādena rathanemisvanena ca
d jaṅgamasya bhayaṃ ghoram akarot pākaśāsaniḥ
a tatas te javanā dhuryā jānubhyām agaman mahīm
c uttaraś cāpi saṃtrasto rathopastha upāviśat
a saṃsthāpya cāśvān kaunteyaḥ samudyamya ca raśmibhiḥ
b vyabhrājata rathopasthe bhānur merāv ivottare
b śaṅkhaśabdena vitrastaṃ jyāghātena ca mūrchitam
c uttaraṃ ca pariṣvajya samāśvāsayad arjunaḥ
a mā bhais tvaṃ rājaputrāgrya kṣatriyo 'si paraṃtapa
c kathaṃ puruṣaśārdūla śatrumadhye viṣīdasi
a śrutās te śaṅkhaśabdāś ca bherīśabdāś ca puṣkalāḥ
c kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nadatāṃ vyūḍhānīkeṣu tiṣṭhatām
a sa tvaṃ katham ihānena śaṅkhaśabdena bhīṣitaḥ
c viṣaṇṇarūpo vitrastaḥ puruṣaḥ prākṛto yathā
 uttara uvāca
a śrutā me śaṅkhaśabdāś ca bherīśabdāś ca puṣkalāḥ
c kuñjarāṇāṃ ca ninadā vyūḍhānīkeṣu tiṣṭhatām
a naivaṃvidhaḥ śaṅkhaśabdaḥ purā jātu mayā śrutaḥ
c dhvajasya cāpi rūpaṃ me dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ na hīdṛśam
e dhanuṣaś caiva nirghoṣaḥ śrutapūrvo na me kva cit
a asya śaṅkhasya śabdena dhanuṣo nisvanena ca
b amānuṣāṇāṃ śabdena bhūtānāṃ dhvajavāsinām
c rathasya ca ninādena mano muhyati me bhṛśam
a vyākulāś ca diśaḥ sarvā hṛdayaṃ vyathatīva me
c dhvajena pihitāḥ sarvā diśo na pratibhānti me
e gāṇḍīvasya ca śabdena karṇau me badhirīkṛtau
f tān   paribhāṣantam uttaraṃ yuddhadurmadaḥ
f sa muhūrtaṃ prayātaṃ tu pārtho vairāṭim abravīt
f vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
f punar dhvajaṃ punaḥ śaṅkhaṃ dhanuś caiva punaḥ punaḥ
f saṃmūḍhacetā vairāṭir arjunaṃ samudaikṣata
f arjunaḥ
f sthiro bhava mahābāho saṃjñāṃ cātmānam ānaya
 arjuna uvāca
a ekānte ratham āsthāya padbhyāṃ tvam avapīḍaya
c dṛḍhaṃ ca raśmīn saṃyaccha śaṅkhaṃ dhmāsyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ
d na bhayaṃ vidyate cānyan mayi tiṣṭhati saṃyuge
d paśya bāhubalaṃ vīra yudhyataḥ śatrubhiḥ saha
d sthirīkuruṣva hṛdayaṃ yathā śabdo mahān bhavet
d evam uktvā mahābāhuḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
d pradadhmau ca mahāśaṅkhaṃ devadattam anuttamam
d jyāghoṣaṃ talaghoṣaṃ ca kṛtvā bhūtāny amohayat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 tataḥ sa punar evātha taṃ śaṅkhaṃ prādhamad balī
 dviṣatāṃ duḥkhajananaṃ suhṛdāṃ prītivardhanam
 tataḥ śaṅkham upādhmāsīd dārayann iva parvatān
 guhā girīṇāṃ ca tadā diśaḥ śailāṃs tathaiva ca
 uttaraś cāpi saṃlīno rathopastha upāviśat
 tato 'rjunaḥ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ cakārātīva duḥsaham
a tasya śaṅkhasya śabdena rathanemisvanena ca
c gāṇḍīvasya ca ghoṣeṇa pṛthivī samakampata
d śrutvā śabdaṃ tadā droṇo gāṅgeyaṃ vākyam abravīt
d uttaraṃ tu rathe dṛṣṭvā śaṅkhaśabdena mohitam
d sa rathaḥ saṃsmṛtas tena upāyād vānaradhvajaḥ
d taṃ samāśvāsayām āsa punar eva dhanaṃjayaḥ
d tato droṇo mahābuddhiḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d uvāca ha kuror madhye sarvaṃ saṃbodhayann iva
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d śaṅkhaśabdaṃ ca taṃ śrutvā meghasya ninadaṃ yathā
d gāṇḍīvajyāsvanenaiva vismayotphullalocanaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d bhāradvājas tato droṇaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d rājānaṃ cāha saṃprekṣya duryodhanam ariṃdamam
 droṇa uvāca
 nadīja laṅkeśavanāriketur
 nagāhvayo nāma nagārisūnuḥ
 eṣo 'ṅganāveṣadharas tarasvī
 vijeṣyate sarvakurupravīrān
 eṣā na yoṣā yadi yoṣid eṣā
 tat saiva yā śumbhaniśumbhahantrī
 māyāmayastrīvapur ātanoti
 līlāyitaṃ vā puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ
 yathendrajit kṣatriyāṇy aṅganeyaṃ
 gurur babhāṣe vacanaṃ kilaitat
a yathā rathasya nirghoṣo yathā śaṅkha udīryate
c kampate ca yathā bhūmir naiṣo 'nyaḥ savyasācinaḥ
d autpātikam idaṃ rājan nimittaṃ bhavatīha naḥ
d na hi paśyāmi vijayaṃ sainye 'smākaṃ paraṃtapa
a śastrāṇi na prakāśante na prahṛṣyanti vājinaḥ
c agnayaś ca na bhāsante samiddhās tan na śobhanam
a praty ādityaṃ ca naḥ sarve mṛgā ghorapravādinaḥ
c dhvajeṣu ca nilīyante vāyasās tan na śobhanam
e śakunāś cāpasavyā no vedayanti mahad bhayam
a gomāyur eṣa senāyā ruvan madhye 'nudhāvati
c anāhataś ca niṣkrānto mahad vedayate bhayam
e bhavatāṃ romakūpāṇi prahṛṣṭāny upalakṣaye
f dhruvaṃ vināśo yuddhena kṣatriyāṇāṃ pradṛśyate
f jyotīṃṣi na prakāśante dāruṇā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
f utpātā vividhā ghorā dṛśyante kṣatranāśanāḥ
f viśeṣata ihāsmākaṃ nimittāni vināśane
f ulkābhiś ca pradīptābhir bādhyate pṛtanā tava
f vāhanāny aprahṛṣṭāni rudantīva viśāṃ pate
f upāsate ca sainyāni gṛdhrās tava samantataḥ
f tapsyase vāhinīṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthabāṇaprapīḍitām
f anuṣṇāṅgāś ca saṃsvinnā jṛmbhante cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
f viṣṭambhantīha mātaṅgā muñcanty aśrūṇi vājinaḥ
f sadā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca utsṛjante punaḥ punaḥ
f lohitārdrā ca pṛthivī diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradhūpitāḥ
f na ca sūryaḥ pratapati mahad vedayate bhayam
f hastinaś cāpi vitrastā yodhāś cāpi vitatrasuḥ
a parābhūtā ca vaḥ senā na kaś cid yoddhum icchati
c vivarṇamukhabhūyiṣṭhāḥ sarve yodhā vicetasaḥ
d diśaṃ te dakṣiṇāṃ sarve viprekṣante punaḥ punaḥ
d mṛgāś ca pakṣiṇaś caiva savyam eva patanti naḥ
d vāditroddhuṣṭaghoṣāś ca na gāḍhaṃ prasvananti naḥ
d yathā meghasya ninado gambhīras tūrṇam āyataḥ
d śrūyate rathanirghoṣo nāyam anyo dhanaṃjayāt
d aśvānāṃ svanatāṃ śabdo vahatāṃ pākaśāsanim
d vānaraś ca dhvajo nityo niḥsaṅgaṃ dhūyate mahān
d śaṅkhaśabdena pārthasya karṇau me badhirīkṛtau
d sarvasainyaṃ ca vitrastaṃ nāyam anyo dhanaṃjayāt
d rājānam agrataḥ kṛtvā duryodhanam ariṃdamam
e gāḥ saṃprasthāpya tiṣṭhāmo vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
f pravibhajya tridhā senāṃ samucchritya dhvajān api
f dikṣu gulmā niveśyantāṃ yattā yotsyāmahe 'rjunam
f śitair bāṇaiḥ pratapyemāṃ camūm eṣa dhanaṃjayaḥ
f mūrdhni sarvanarendrāṇāṃ vāmapādaṃ kariṣyati
f na hy eṣa śakyo bībhatsur jetuṃ devāsurair api
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a atha duryodhano rājā samare bhīṣmam abravīt
c droṇaṃ ca rathaśārdūlaṃ kṛpaṃ ca sumahāratham
a ukto 'yam artha ācāryo mayā karṇena cāsakṛt
c punar eva ca vakṣyāmi na hi tṛpyāmi taṃ bruvan
a parājitair hi vastavyaṃ taiś ca dvādaśa vatsarān
c vane janapade 'jñātair eṣa eva paṇo hi naḥ
a teṣāṃ na tāvan nirvṛttaṃ vartate tu trayodaśam
c ajñātavāsaṃ bībhatsur athāsmābhiḥ samāgataḥ
a anivṛtte tu nirvāse yadi bībhatsur āgataḥ
c punar dvādaśa varṣāṇi vane vatsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a lobhād vā te na jānīyur asmān vā moha āviśat
c hīnātiriktam eteṣāṃ bhīṣmo veditum arhati
a arthānāṃ tu punar dvaidhe nityaṃ bhavati saṃśayaḥ
b svārthe sarve vimuhyanti ye 'pi dharmavido janāḥ
c anyathā cintito hy arthaḥ punar bhavati cānyathā
a uttaraṃ mārgamāṇānāṃ matsyasenāṃ yuyutsatām
c yadi bībhatsur āyātas teṣāṃ kaḥ syāt parāṅmukhaḥ
a trigartānāṃ vayaṃ hetor matsyān yoddhum ihāgatāḥ
c matsyānāṃ viprakārāṃs te bahūn asmān akīrtayan
a teṣāṃ bhayābhipannānāṃ tad asmābhiḥ pratiśrutam
a   trastānāṃ trāṇam icchatām
a abhayaṃ yācamānānāṃ
c prathamaṃ tair grahītavyaṃ matsyānāṃ godhanaṃ mahat
a saptamīm aparāhṇe vai tathā nas taiḥ samāhitam
c aṣṭamyāṃ punar asmābhir ādityasyodayaṃ prati
d imā gāvo gṛhītavyā gate matsye gavāṃ padam
d ity eṣa niścayo 'smākaṃ mantro 'bhūn nāgasāhvaye
d pāṇḍavānāṃ parijñāne sarveṣāṃ naḥ parasparam
a te vā gāvo na paśyanti yadi va syuḥ parājitāḥ
c asmān vāpy atisaṃdhāya kuryur matsyena saṃgatam
a atha vā tān upāyāto matsyo jānapadaiḥ saha
c sarvayā senayā sārdham asmān yoddhum upāgataḥ
c   saṃvṛto bhīmarūpayā
c āyātaḥ kevalāṃ rātrim
a teṣām eva mahāvīryaḥ kaś cid eva puraḥsaraḥ
c asmāñ jetum ihāyāto matsyo vāpi svayaṃ bhavet
a yady eṣa rājā matsyānāṃ yadi bībhatsur āgataḥ
c sarvair yoddhavyam asmābhir iti naḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ
d śarair enaṃ suniśitaiḥ pātayiṣyāmi bhūtale
a atha kasmāt sthitā hy ete ratheṣu rathasattamāḥ
c bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaś caiva vikarṇo drauṇir eva ca
a saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ sarve kāle hy asmin mahārathāḥ
c nānyatra yuddhāc chreyo 'sti tathātmā praṇidhīyatām
d sarvalokena vā yuddhaṃ devair vāstu savāsavaiḥ
a ācchinne godhane 'smākam api devena vajriṇā
c yamena vāpi saṃgrāme ko hāstinapuraṃ vrajet
a śarair abhipraṇunnānāṃ bhagnānāṃ gahane vane
c ko hi jīvet padātīnāṃ bhaved aśveṣu saṃśayaḥ
e ācāryaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā tathā nītir vidhīyatām
f duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā rāṃdheyas tv abravīd vacaḥ
a jānāti hi mataṃ teṣām atas trāsayatīva naḥ
c arjunenāsya saṃprītim adhikām upalakṣaye
a tathā hi dṛṣṭvā bībhatsum upāyāntaṃ praśaṃsati
c yathā senā na bhajyeta tathā nītir vidhīyatām
d heṣitaṃ hy upaśṛṇvāne droṇe sarvaṃ vighaṭṭitam
a adeśikā mahāraṇye grīṣme śatruvaśaṃ gatā
c yathā na vibhramet senā tathā nītir vidhīyatām
d iṣṭā hi pāṇḍavā nityam ācāryasya viśeṣataḥ
d āsayann aparārthāś ca kathyate sma svayaṃ tathā
a aśvānāṃ heṣitaṃ śrutvā kā praśaṃsā bhavet pare
c sthāne vāpi vrajanto vā sadā heṣanti vājinaḥ
a sadā ca vāyavo vānti nityaṃ varṣati vāsavaḥ
c stanayitnoś ca nirghoṣaḥ śrūyate bahuśas tathā
d bhīṣayan pāṇḍaveyebhyo bhavān sarvān imāñ janān
d pramukhe sarvasainyānām abaddhaṃ bahu bhāṣate
d yathaivāśvān mārgamāṇās tān evābhiparīpsavaḥ
d heṣitāny eva śṛṇvanti syād idaṃ bhavatas tathā
a kim atra kāryaṃ pārthasya kathaṃ vā sa praśasyate
c anyatra kāmād dveṣād vā roṣād vāsmāsu kevalāt
a ācāryā vai kāruṇikāḥ prājñāś cāpāyadarśinaḥ
c naite mahābhaye prāpte saṃpraṣṭavyāḥ kathaṃ cana
a prāsādeṣu vicitreṣu goṣṭhīṣv āvasatheṣu ca
c kathā vicitrāḥ kurvāṇāḥ paṇḍitās tatra śobhanāḥ
a bahūny āścaryarūpāṇi kurvanto janasaṃsadi
c iṣvastre cārusaṃdhāne paṇḍitās tatra śobhanāḥ
a pareṣāṃ vivarajñāne manuṣyācariteṣu ca
b hastyaśvarathacaryāsu kharoṣṭrājāvikarmaṇi
b godhaneṣu pratolīṣu varadvāramukheṣu ca
c annasaṃskāradoṣeṣu paṇḍitās tatra śobhanāḥ
a paṇḍitān pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā pareṣāṃ guṇavādinaḥ
c vidhīyatāṃ tathā nītir yathā vadhyeta vai paraḥ
a gāvaś caiva pratiṣṭhantāṃ senāṃ vyūhantu māciram
c ārakṣāś ca vidhīyantāṃ yatra yotsyāmahe parān
d yathāsmākaṃ jayo vīra cintanīyas tathā tvayā
 karṇa uvāca
a sarvān āyuṣmato bhītān saṃtrastān iva lakṣaye
c ayuddhamanasaś caiva sarvāṃś caivānavasthitān
d yady eṣa jāmadagnyo vā yadi vendraḥ puraṃdaraḥ
a yady eṣa rājā matsyānāṃ yadi bībhatsur āgataḥ
c aham āvārayiṣyāmi veleva makarālayam
a mama cāpapramuktānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
c nāvṛttir gacchatām asti sarpāṇām iva sarpatām
a rukmapuṅkhāḥ sutīkṣṇāgrā muktā hastavatā mayā
c chādayantu śarāḥ pārthaṃ śalabhā iva pādapam
a śarāṇāṃ puṅkhasaktānāṃ maurvyābhihatayā dṛḍham
c śrūyatāṃ talayoḥ śabdo bheryor āhatayor iva
d ekaikaṃ caturaḥ pañca kva cit ṣaṣṭiṃ kva cic chatam
d mayā paśyata matsyānām iṣubhir nihatān rathān
d ekaṃ dvau caturaḥ pañca kva cit ṣaṣṭiṃ kva cic chatam
d hatān paśyata mātaṅgān kīrṇān ekeṣuṇā mayā
d madbāhumuktair iṣubhis tailadhautaiḥ patatribhiḥ
d khadyotair iva saṃvṛttam antarikṣaṃ vyarājatām
a samāhito hi bībhatsur varṣāṇy aṣṭau ca pañca ca
c jātasnehaś ca yuddhasya mayi saṃprahariṣyati
a pātrībhūtaś ca kaunteyo brāhmaṇo guṇavān iva
c śaraughān pratigṛhṇātu mayā muktān sahasraśaḥ
a eṣa caiva maheṣvāsas triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
c ahaṃ cāpi kuruśreṣṭhā arjunān nāvaraḥ kva cit
d mama hastapramuktānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
d nivṛttir gacchatāṃ nāsti vaiśvānarasamatviṣām
a itaś cetaś ca nirmuktaiḥ kāñcanair gārdhravājitaiḥ
c dṛśyatām adya vai vyoma khadyotair iva saṃvṛtam
d tumulaḥ śrūyatāṃ nādaḥ ṣaṭpadāṃ gāyatām iva
d matkārmukavimuktānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
d kaḥ sahetāgrataḥ sthātum api sarvaiḥ surāsuraiḥ
a adyāham ṛṇam akṣayyaṃ purā vācā pratiśrutam
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya dāsyāmi nihatya samare 'rjunam
a antarā chidyamānānāṃ puṅkhānāṃ vyatiśīryatām
c śalabhānām ivākāśe pracāraḥ saṃpradṛśyatām
a indrāśanisamasparśaṃ mahendrasamatejasam
c ardayiṣyāmy ahaṃ pārtham ulkābhir iva kuñjaram
d rathād atirathaṃ śūraṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
d vivaśaṃ pārtham ādāsye garutmān iva pannagam
a tam agnim iva durdharṣam asiśaktiśarendhanam
c pāṇḍavāgnim ahaṃ dīptaṃ pradahantam ivāhitān
a aśvavegapurovāto rathaughastanayitnumān
c śaradhāro mahāmeghaḥ śamayiṣyāmi pāṇḍavam
d nirdahantam anīkāni śamayiṣye 'rjunānalam
d kṣudrakair vividhair bhallair nipatadbhiś ca māmakaiḥ
d saṃmūḍhacetāḥ kaunteyaḥ kartavyaṃ nābhipadyate
a matkārmukavinirmuktāḥ pārtham āśīviṣopamāḥ
c śarāḥ samabhisarpantu valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
d sutejanai rukmapuṅkhaiḥ supītair nataparvabhiḥ
d ācitaṃ paśya kaunteyaṃ karṇikārair ivācalam
d barhibarhiṇavājānāṃ barhiṇāṃ barhiṇām iva
d patatāṃ patatāṃ ghoṣaḥ patatāṃ patatām iva
a jāmadagnyān mayā hy astraṃ yat prāptam ṛṣisattamāt
c tad upāśritya vīryaṃ ca yudhyeyam api vāsavam
a dhvajāgre vānaras tiṣṭhan bhallena nihato mayā
c adyaiva patatāṃ bhūmau vinadan bhairavān ravān
a śatror mayābhipannānāṃ bhūtānāṃ dhvajavāsinām
c diśaḥ pratiṣṭhamānānām astu śabdo divaṃ gataḥ
d kruddhenāstraṃ mayā muktaṃ nirdahet pṛthivīm imām
d sthitaṃ saṃgrāmaśirasi pārtham ekākinaṃ kimu
a adya duryodhanasyāhaṃ śalyaṃ hṛdi cirasthitam
c samūlam uddhariṣyāmi bībhatsuṃ pātayan rathāt
a hatāśvaṃ virathaṃ pārthaṃ pauruṣe paryavasthitam
c niḥśvasantaṃ yathā nāgam adya paśyantu kauravāḥ
a kāmaṃ gacchantu kuravo dhanam ādāya kevalam
c ratheṣu vāpi tiṣṭhanto yuddhaṃ paśyantu māmakam
d paśyantu vīryam iha māmakam adya nāma
d magne jane samanujāḥ surasiddhasaṃghāḥ
d śakrātmajasya samare virathīkṛtasya
d evaṃ punaḥ sa virarāma kṛpo babhāṣe
 kṛpa uvāca
 vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
 tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā nītiśāstraviśāradaḥ
 ācāryaḥ kuruvīrāṇāṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato 'bravīt
a sadaiva tava rādheya yuddhe krūratarā matiḥ
c nārthānāṃ prakṛtiṃ vettha nānubandham avekṣase
a nayā hi bahavaḥ santi śāstrāṇy āśritya cintitāḥ
c teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ tu pāpiṣṭhaṃ vedayanti purāvidaḥ
a deśakālena saṃyuktaṃ yuddhaṃ vijayadaṃ bhavet
c hīnakālaṃ tad eveha phalavan na bhavaty uta
e deśe kāle ca vikrāntaṃ kalyāṇāya vidhīyate
a ānukūlyena kāryāṇām antaraṃ saṃvidhīyatām
c bhāraṃ hi rathakārasya na vyavasyanti paṇḍitāḥ
a paricintya tu pārthena saṃnipāto na naḥ kṣamaḥ
b eko hi samare śatrūn samarthaḥ pratibādhitum
c ekaḥ kurūn abhyarakṣad ekaś cāgnim atarpayat
a ekaś ca pañca varṣāṇi brahmacaryam adhārayat
c ekaḥ subhadrām āropya dvairathe kṛṣṇam āhvayat
d ekaḥ kirātarūpeṇa sthitaṃ śarvam ayodhayat
e asminn eva vane kṛṣṇo hṛtāṃ kṛṣṇām avājayat
a ekaś ca pañca varṣāṇi śakrād astrāṇy aśikṣata
b eko deveśvaraṃ jitvā astrarājam avāptavān
c ekaḥ sāṃyaminīṃ jitvā kurūṇām akarod yaśaḥ
a eko gandharvarājānaṃ citrasenam ariṃdamaḥ
c vijigye tarasā saṃkhye senāṃ cāsya sudurjayām
d pāñcālīṃ śrīmatīṃ prāptaḥ kṣatraṃ jitvā svayaṃvare
d ādāya gatavān pārtho bhavān kva nu gatas tadā
a tathā nivātakavacāḥ kālakhañjāś ca dānavāḥ
c daivatair apy avadhyās te ekena yudhi pātitāḥ
a ekena hi tvayā karṇa kiṃ nāmeha kṛtaṃ purā
c ekaikena yathā teṣāṃ bhūmipālā vaśīkṛtāḥ
a indro 'pi hi na pārthena saṃyuge yoddhum arhati
c yas tenāśaṃsate yoddhuṃ kartavyaṃ tasya bheṣajam
a āśīviṣasya kruddhasya pāṇim udyamya dakṣiṇam
c avimṛśya pradeśinyā daṃṣṭrām ādātum icchasi
a atha vā kuñjaraṃ mattam eka eva caran vane
c anaṅkuśaṃ samāruhya nagaraṃ gantum icchasi
a samiddhaṃ pāvakaṃ vāpi ghṛtamedovasāhutam
b prāvṛtaḥ kuśacīreṇa patituṃ mūrkha manyase
c ghṛtāktaś cīravāsās tvaṃ madhyenottartum icchasi
a ātmānaṃ yaḥ samudbadhya kaṇṭhe baddhvā mahāśilām
c samudraṃ pratared dorbhyāṃ tatra kiṃ nāma pauruṣam
a akṛtāstraḥ kṛtāstraṃ vai balavantaṃ sudurbalaḥ
c tādṛśaṃ karṇa yaḥ pārthaṃ yoddhum icchet sa durmatiḥ
a asmābhir eṣa nikṛto varṣāṇīha trayodaśa
c siṃhaḥ pāśavinirmukto na naḥ śeṣaṃ kariṣyati
a ekānte pārtham āsīnaṃ kūpe 'gnim iva saṃvṛtam
c ajñānād abhyavaskandya prāptāḥ smo bhayam uttamam
d utsṛṣṭaṃ tūlarāśau tu eko 'gniṃ śamayet katham
a saha yudhyāmahe pārtham āgataṃ yuddhadurmadam
c sainyās tiṣṭhantu saṃnaddhā vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
d yuddhāyāvasthitaṃ pārtham āgataṃ pākaśāsanim
a droṇo duryodhano bhīṣmo bhavān drauṇis tathā vayam
c sarve yudhyāmahe pārthaṃ karṇa mā sāhasaṃ kṛthāḥ
d na hy asaṃhatya samare pārthaṃ jeṣyāmahe vayam
a vayaṃ vyavasitaṃ pārthaṃ vajrapāṇim ivodyatam
c ṣaḍrathāḥ pratiyudhyema tiṣṭhema yadi saṃhatāḥ
a vyūḍhānīkāni sainyāni yattāḥ paramadhanvinaḥ
c yudhyāmahe 'rjunaṃ saṃkhye dānavā vāsavaṃ yathā
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d kṛpasya tu vacaḥ śrutvā karṇo rājan yudhāṃ patiḥ
d punaḥ provāca saṃkruddho garhayan brāhmaṇaṃ kṛpam
d lakṣayāmy aham ācāryaṃ bhayād bhaktiṃ gataṃ ripau
d bhītena hi na yoddhavyam ahaṃ yotsye dhanaṃjayam
d nanu vāruṇam āgneyaṃ yāmyaṃ vāyavyam eva ca
d astraṃ brahmaśiraś caiva sattvahīnaś ca te vṛthā
d mitrakāryaṃ kṛtam idaṃ pitāputrair mahārathaiḥ
d bhartṛpiṇḍaś ca nirdiṣṭo yatheṣṭaṃ gantum arhatha
d bhikṣāṃ harasva tvaṃ nityaṃ yajñān anucarasva ca
d āmantraṇaṃ hi bhuṅkṣvādya māsmān yuddhena bhīṣaya
d bhārgavāstraṃ mayā muktaṃ nirdahet pṛthivīm imām
d kiṃ punaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇām ekam arjunam āhave
d āgamiṣyanti padavīṃ mātsyāḥ pāṇḍavam āśritāḥ
d tān ahaṃ nihaniṣyāmi bhavatā gamyatāṃ gṛham
d tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā aśvatthāmā pratāpavān
d uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho duryodhanam avekṣya ca
d yattāḥ sarve rathaśreṣṭhaṃ parivārya samantataḥ
d ṣaḍrathāḥ parikīryantāṃ vajrapāṇim ivāsurāḥ
 aśvatthāmovāca
a na ca tāvaj jitā gāvo na ca sīmāntaraṃ gatāḥ
c na hāstinapuraṃ prāptās tvaṃ ca karṇa vikatthase
d bahūni dharmaśāstrāṇi paṭhanti dvijasattamāḥ
d teṣu kiṃ svid idaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dyūte jīyeta yan nṛpaḥ
a saṃgrāmān subahūñ jitvā labdhvā ca vipulaṃ dhanam
c vijitya ca parāṃ bhūmiṃ nāhuḥ kiṃ cana pauruṣam
a pacaty agnir avākyas tu tūṣṇīṃ bhāti divākaraḥ
c tūṣṇīṃ dhārayate lokān vasudhā sacarācarān
a cāturvarṇyasya karmāṇi vihitāni manīṣibhiḥ
c dhanaṃ yair adhigantavyaṃ yac ca kurvan na duṣyati
a adhītya brāhmaṇo vedān yājayeta yajeta ca
c kṣatriyo dhanur āśritya yajetaiva na yājayet
e vaiśyo 'dhigamya dravyāṇi brahmakarmāṇi kārayet
f śūdraḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuryāt triṣu varṇeṣu nityaśaḥ
f vandanāyogavidhibhir vaitasīṃ vṛttim āsthitaḥ
a vartamānā yathāśāstraṃ prāpya cāpi mahīm imām
c sat kurvanti mahābhāgā gurūn suviguṇān api
d kā jātis teṣu sūteyaṃ ke 'nyamantrāḥ kriyāś ca kāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d keyaṃ varṇeṣu yā rājño vaktṛbhoktṛniyantṛṣu
d duryodhanam abhiprekṣya karṇaṃ ca kurusaṃsadi
d aśvatthāmā bhṛśaṃ kruddho duryodhanam atarjayat
a prāpya dyūtena ko rājyaṃ kṣatriyas toṣṭum arhati
c tathā nṛśaṃsarūpeṇa yathānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥ
d yad vṛttaṃ prākṛtaiś cīrṇaṃ loke sadbhir vigarhitam
a tathāvāpteṣu vitteṣu ko vikatthed vicakṣaṇaḥ
b buddhimān nītimān rājā kṣatriyo yadi vetaraḥ
c nikṛtyā vañcanāyogaiś caran vaitaṃsiko yathā
a katamad dvairathaṃ yuddhaṃ yatrājaiṣīr dhanaṃjayam
c nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca dhanaṃ yeṣāṃ tvayā hṛtam
a yudhiṣṭhiro jitaḥ kasmin bhīmaś ca balināṃ varaḥ
c indraprasthaṃ tvayā kasmin saṃgrāme nirjitaṃ purā
a tathaiva katamaṃ yuddhaṃ yasmin kṛṣṇā jitā tvayā
c ekavastrā sabhāṃ nītā duṣṭakarman rajasvalā
a mūlam eṣāṃ mahat kṛttaṃ sārārthī candanaṃ yathā
c karma kārayithāḥ śūra tatra kiṃ viduro 'bravīt
a yathāśakti manuṣyāṇāṃ śamam ālakṣayāmahe
c anyeṣāṃ caiva sattvānām api kīṭapipīlike
a draupadyās taṃ parikleśaṃ na kṣantuṃ pāṇḍavo 'rhati
c duḥkhāya dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ prādurbhūto dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tvaṃ punaḥ paṇḍito bhūtvā vācaṃ vaktum ihecchasi
c vairāntakaraṇo jiṣṇur na naḥ śeṣaṃ kariṣyati
a naiṣa devān na gandharvān nāsurān na ca rākṣasān
c bhayād iha na yudhyeta kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a yaṃ yam eṣo 'bhisaṃkruddhaḥ saṃgrāme 'bhipatiṣyati
c vṛkṣaṃ garuḍavegena vinihatya tam eṣyati
a tvatto viśiṣṭaṃ vīryeṇa dhanuṣy amararāṭsamam
c vāsudevasamaṃ yuddhe taṃ pārthaṃ ko na pūjayet
a daivaṃ daivena yudhyeta mānuṣeṇa ca mānuṣam
c astreṇāstraṃ samāhanyāt ko 'rjunena samaḥ pumān
d evam ābhāṣya rādheyaṃ duryodhanam athābravīt
a putrād anantaraḥ śiṣya iti dharmavido viduḥ
c etenāpi nimittena priyo droṇasya pāṇḍavaḥ
a yathā tvam akaror dyūtam indraprasthaṃ yathāharaḥ
c yathānaiṣīḥ sabhāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ tathā yudhyasva pāṇḍavam
a ayaṃ te mātulaḥ prājñaḥ kṣatradharmasya kovidaḥ
c durdyūtadevī gāndhāraḥ śakunir yudhyatām iha
a nākṣān kṣipati gāṇḍīvaṃ na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
c jvalato niśitān bāṇāṃs tīkṣṇān kṣipati gāṇḍivam
a na hi gāṇḍīvanirmuktā gārdhrapatrāḥ sutejanāḥ
c antareṣv avatiṣṭhanti girīṇām api dāraṇāḥ
a antakaḥ śamano mṛtyus tathāgnir vaḍavāmukhaḥ
b kṣuradhārā viṣaṃ sarpo vahnir ity ekataḥ striyaḥ
c kuryur ete kva cic cheṣaṃ na tu kruddho dhanaṃjayaḥ
d yathā sabhāyāṃ dyūtaṃ tvaṃ mātulena sahākaroḥ
d tathā yudhyasva saṃgrāme saubalena surakṣitaḥ
a yudhyatāṃ kāmam ācāryo nāhaṃ yotsye dhanaṃjayam
c matsyo hy asmābhir āyodhyo yady āgacched gavāṃ padam
d karṇa uvāca
d sadaiva droṇaputro 'yaṃ pāpātmā pāpapauruṣaḥ
d kim atra kāryaṃ pārthena kathaṃ vā sa praśasyate
d anyatra kāmān mohād vā lobhād vāsmāsu kevalāt
d praśaṃsati durātmānaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ pāpapauruṣam
d māṃ cāpi nindate nityaṃ dviṣatasyaiva kāmyayā
d tasmād ayaṃ sudurbuddhiḥ paśyatāṃ mama pauruṣam
d aśvatthāmovāca
d vākchūrā brāhmaṇāḥ proktā bāhuśūrāś ca kṣatriyāḥ
d karṇa uvāca
d dhanuṣā cārjunaḥ śūraḥ karṇaḥ śūro manorathaiḥ
d sadā bhīṣayate sarvāṃ vāhinīṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥ
d prītyā ca pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ darśayann ahitaṃ tava
d sadā ca vāyavo vānti nityaṃ varṣati vāsavaḥ
d arjunaṃ samare jitvā labdhvā ca vijayaṃ mahat
d tataś chetsyāmi khaḍgena śiras te brāhmaṇādhama
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d evam ukte tu vacane karṇenāmitrasūdana
d aśvatthāmā tato rājan khaḍgaṃ jagrāha carma ca
d gṛhītvā vimalaṃ khaḍgaṃ carma cādāya suprabham
d dudrāva yoddhuṃ taṃ karṇaṃ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā
d tasmin gṛhīte khaḍge tu karṇo 'pi rathināṃ varaḥ
d uttatāra rathāt tūrṇaṃ gṛhṇan khaḍgaṃ sa vīryavān
d tatas tau tu mahāvīryau dhṛtāstrau yuddhadurmadau
d anyonyasya vadhaṃ prepsū siṃhāv iva madotkaṭau
d tau dṛṣṭvā sumahāvīryau yuddhāya samavasthitau
d duryodhanas tatas tūrṇaṃ rathād uttīrya vegavān
d abhigamya guroḥ putram aśvatthāmānam abravīt
d aśvatthāman guroḥ putra kṣamyatāṃ dvijasattama
d karṇo vaktuṃ na jānāti brāhmaṇāś cātikopanāḥ
d tvayi saṃnihito bhāro yuddhasyaiṣa viniścayaḥ
d sa tathābhihito rājan rājñā caiva nivāritaḥ
d svarathaṃ prāpya tūrṇaṃ vai na ca kiṃ cid uvāca ha
d karṇo 'pi svaṃ rathaṃ tūrṇam āruroha nṛpājñayā
 vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
 tataḥ śāṃtanavas tatra dharmārthakuśalaṃ hitam
 duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃsadi
 bhīṣma uvāca
a sādhu paśyati vai droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ sādhv anupaśyati
b ācāryaputraḥ sahajaṃ niścitaṃ sādhu bhāṣate
c karṇas tu kṣatradharmeṇa yathāvad yoddhum icchati
a ācāryo nābhiṣaktavyaḥ puruṣeṇa vijānatā
c deśakālau tu saṃprekṣya yoddhavyam iti me matiḥ
a yasya sūryasamāḥ pañca sapatnāḥ syuḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c katham abhyudaye teṣāṃ na pramuhyeta paṇḍitaḥ
a svārthe sarve vimuhyanti ye 'pi dharmavido janāḥ
b tasmāt tattvaṃ na jānāti yat tu kāryaṃ narādhipaḥ
b dhārtarāṣṭro hi durbuddhiḥ paśyann api dhanaṃjayam
b naiva paśyati nāghrāti mandaḥ krodhavaśaṃ gataḥ
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b evam uktvā tu rājānaṃ punar drauṇim uvāca ha
b prāñjalir bharataśreṣṭhaḥ sāmnā buddhimatāṃ varaḥ
c tasmād rājan bravīmy eṣa vākyaṃ te yadi rocate
a karṇo yad abhyavocan nas tejaḥsaṃjananāya tat
c ācāryaputraḥ kṣamatāṃ mahat kāryam upasthitam
a nāyaṃ kālo virodhasya kaunteye samupasthite
c kṣantavyaṃ bhavatā sarvam ācāryeṇa kṛpeṇa ca
d balasya vyasanāny āhus tāni dhīrā manīṣiṇaḥ
d mukhe bhedaṃ ca teṣāṃ tu pāpiṣṭhaṃ viduṣāṃ matam
a bhavatāṃ hi kṛtāstratvaṃ yathāditye prabhā tathā
c yathā candramaso lakṣma sarvathā nāpakṛṣyate
e evaṃ bhavatsu brāhmaṇyaṃ brahmāstraṃ ca pratiṣṭhitam
a catvāra ekato vedāḥ kṣātram ekatra dṛśyate
c naitat samastam ubhayaṃ kasmiṃś cid anuśuśrumaḥ
a anyatra bhāratācāryāt saputrād iti me matiḥ
b vedāntāś ca purāṇāni itihāsaṃ purātanam
b jāmadagnyam ṛte rājan ko droṇād adhiko bhavet
c brahmāstraṃ caiva vedāś ca naitad anyatra dṛśyate
a ācāryaputraḥ kṣamatāṃ nāyaṃ kālaḥ svabhedane
c sarve saṃhatya yudhyāmaḥ pākaśāsanim āgatam
a balasya vyasanānīha yāny uktāni manīṣibhiḥ
c mukhyo bhedo hi teṣāṃ vai pāpiṣṭho viduṣāṃ mataḥ
 aśvatthāmovāca
 naiva nyāyyam idaṃ vācyam asmākaṃ puruṣarṣabha
 kiṃ tu roṣaparītena guruṇā bhāṣitā guṇāḥ
 śatror api guṇā grāhyā doṣā vācyā guror api
 duryodhana uvāca
 sarvathā sarvayatnena putre śiṣye hitaṃ vadet
a ācārya eva kṣamatāṃ śāntir atra vidhīyatām
c abhiṣajyamāne hi gurau tadvṛttaṃ roṣakāritam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato duryodhano droṇaṃ kṣamayām āsa bhārata
c saha karṇena bhīṣmeṇa kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā
 droṇa uvāca
a yad eva prathamaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
c tenaivāhaṃ prasanno vai param atra vidhīyatām
a yathā duryodhane 'yatte nāgaḥ spṛśati sainikān
c sāhasād yadi vā mohāt tathā nītir vidhīyatām
a vanavāse hy anirvṛtte darśayen na dhanaṃjayaḥ
c dhanaṃ vālabhamāno 'tra nādya naḥ kṣantum arhati
a yathā nāyaṃ samāyujyād dhārtarāṣṭrān kathaṃ cana
c yathā ca na parājayyāt tathā nītir vidhīyatām
a uktaṃ duryodhanenāpi purastād vākyam īdṛśam
c tad anusmṛtya gāṅgeya yathāvad vaktum arhasi
 bhīṣma uvāca
a kalāṃśās tāta yujyante muhūrtāś ca dināni ca
c ardhamāsāś ca māsāś ca nakṣatrāṇi grahās tathā
a ṛtavaś cāpi yujyante tathā saṃvatsarā api
c evaṃ kālavibhāgena kālacakraṃ pravartate
a teṣāṃ kālātirekeṇa jyotiṣāṃ ca vyatikramāt
c pañcame pañcame varṣe dvau māsāv upajāyataḥ
a teṣām abhyadhikā māsāḥ pañca dvādaśa ca kṣapāḥ
c trayodaśānāṃ varṣāṇām iti me vartate matiḥ
d pūrvedyur eva nirvṛtte tato bībhatsur āgataḥ
d gate varṣadvaye caiva pañcapakṣe dinadvaye
d divasasyāṣṭame bhāge pataty eko 'dhimāsakaḥ
a sarvaṃ yathāvac caritaṃ yad yad ebhiḥ pariśrutam
c evam etad dhruvaṃ jñātvā tato bībhatsur āgataḥ
a sarve caiva mahātmānaḥ sarve dharmārthakovidāḥ
c yeṣāṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā kasmād dharme 'parādhnuyuḥ
d kāmāt krodhāc ca lobhāc ca kāmakrodhabhayād api
d snehād vā yadi vā mohād dharmaṃ nātyeti dharmajaḥ
a alubdhāś caiva kaunteyāḥ kṛtavantaś ca duṣkaram
c na cāpi kevalaṃ rājyam iccheyus te 'nupāyataḥ
a tadaiva te hi vikrāntum īṣuḥ kauravanandanāḥ
c dharmapāśanibaddhās tu na celuḥ kṣatriyavratāt
a yac cānṛta iti khyāyed yac ca gacchet parābhavam
c vṛṇuyur maraṇaṃ pārthā nānṛtatvaṃ kathaṃ cana
a prāpte tu kāle prāptavyaṃ notsṛjeyur nararṣabhāḥ
c api vajrabhṛtā guptaṃ tathāvīryā hi pāṇḍavāḥ
a pratiyudhyāma samare sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
b āgataṃ phālgunaṃ rājan sarve tatra na saṃśayaḥ
c tasmād yad atra kalyāṇaṃ loke sadbhir anuṣṭhitam
e tat saṃvidhīyatāṃ kṣipraṃ mā no hy artho 'tigāt parān
a na hi paśyāmi saṃgrāme kadā cid api kaurava
c ekāntasiddhiṃ rājendra saṃprāptaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
a saṃpravṛtte tu saṃgrāme bhāvābhāvau jayājayau
c avaśyam ekaṃ spṛśato dṛṣṭam etad asaṃśayam
a tasmād yuddhāvacarikaṃ karma vā dharmasaṃhitam
c kriyatām āśu rājendra saṃprāpto hi dhanaṃjayaḥ
d eko 'pi samare pārthaḥ pṛthivīṃ nirdahec charaiḥ
d bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitas tāta kiṃ punaḥ kauravān raṇe
d tasmāt saṃdhiṃ kuruśreṣṭha kuruṣva yadi manyase
 duryodhana uvāca
a nāhaṃ rājyaṃ pradāsyāmi pāṇḍavānāṃ pitāmaha
b grāmaṃ senāṃ ca dāsīṃ ca svalpaṃ dravyam api prabho
c yuddhāvacārikaṃ yat tu tac chīghraṃ saṃvidhīyatām
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d bhīṣmasyoparate vākye tathā duryodhanasya ca
d prāptam arthyaṃ ca yad vākyaṃ droṇaś cāha dvijottamaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
 yat tu yuddhāya caritaṃ bhaved vā dharmasaṃhitam
 kas tvayā sadṛśo loke bhūyas tvaṃ vaktum arhasi
a atra yā māmakī buddhiḥ śrūyatāṃ yadi rocate
b sarvathā hi mayā śreyo vaktavyaṃ kurunandana
c kṣipraṃ balacaturbhāgaṃ gṛhya gaccha puraṃ prati
e tato 'paraś caturbhāgo gāḥ samādāya gacchatu
a vayaṃ tv ardhena sainyena pratiyotsyāma pāṇḍavam
b ahaṃ droṇaś ca karṇaś ca aśvatthāmā kṛpas tathā
b pratiyotsyāma bībhatsum āgataṃ kṛtaniścayam
b evaṃ rājā suguptaḥ syān na klaibyam anupaśyati
c matsyaṃ vā punar āyātam atha vāpi śatakratum
d aham āvārayiṣyāmi veleva makarālayam
d yudhyāma saha saṃhatya pākaśāsanim āgatam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d droṇasyoparate vākye bhīṣmaḥ provāca buddhimān
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d tad vākyaṃ ruruce teṣāṃ bhīṣmeṇoktaṃ mahātmanā
d tathā hi kṛtavān rājā kauravāṇām anantaram
d bhīṣmaḥ prasthāpya rājānaṃ godhanaṃ tad anantaram
d senāmukhyān vyavasthāpya vyūhituṃ saṃpracakrame
a ācāryo madhyatas tiṣṭhatv aśvatthāmā tu savyataḥ
c kṛpaḥ śāradvato dhīmān pārśvaṃ rakṣatu dakṣiṇam
d vikarṇaś ca mahāvīryo durmukhaś ca paraṃtapaḥ
d śakuniḥ saubalaś caiva duḥsahaś ca mahābalaḥ
d droṇasya pārśvam ajitāḥ pālayantu mahārathāḥ
a agrataḥ sūtaputras tu karṇas tiṣṭhatu daṃśitaḥ
c ahaṃ sarvasya sainyasya paścāt sthāsyāmi pālayan
d sarve mahārathāḥ śūrā maheṣvāsā mahābalāḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yudhyantu pāṇḍavaśreṣṭham āgataṃ yatnato yudhi
d abhedyaṃ parasainyānāṃ vyūhaṃ vyūhya kurūttamaḥ
d vajragarbhaṃ vrīhimukhaṃ padmacandrārdhamaṇḍalam
d tasya vyūhasya paścārdhe bhīṣmaś cāthodyatāyudhaḥ
d sauvarṇaṃ tālam ucchritya rathe tiṣṭhann aśobhata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu kauraveyair mahārathaiḥ
c upāyād arjunas tūrṇaṃ rathaghoṣeṇa nādayan
a dadṛśus te dhvajāgraṃ vai śuśruvuś ca rathasvanam
c dodhūyamānasya bhṛśaṃ gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanam
d trikośamātraṃ gatvā tu pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
d senāmukham abhiprekṣya pārtho vairāṭim abravīt
d rājānaṃ nātra paśyāmi rathānīke vyavasthitam
d dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āsthāya kuravo yānty udaṅmukhāḥ
d utsṛjyaitad rathānīkaṃ maheṣvāsābhirakṣitam
d gavāgram abhito yāhi yāvat paśyāmi me ripum
d gavāgram abhito gatvā gāś cāśu vinivartaya
d yāvad ete nivartante kuravo javam āsthitāḥ
d tāvad eva paśūn sarvān nivartiṣye tavābhibho
d ity uktvā samare pārtho vairāṭim aparājitaḥ
d savyaṃ pakṣam anuprāpya javenāśvān acodayat
d tato 'bhyavādayat pārtho bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ kṛpam
d dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ tathācāryaṃ droṇaṃ ca niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
d droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca pṛṣatkair abhyavādayat
a tatas tat sarvam ālokya droṇo vacanam abravīt
b droṇaḥ
b na kaś cid yoddhum iccheta na ca guptaṃ svajīvitam
b ayaṃ vīraś ca śūraś ca durdharṣaś caiva saṃyuge
c mahāratham anuprāptaṃ dṛṣṭvā gāṇḍīvadhanvinam
a etad dhvajāgraṃ pārthasya dūrataḥ saṃprakāśate
c eṣa ghoṣaḥ sajalado roravīti ca vānaraḥ
d avasthāya rathaṃ yāti gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṣipan dhanuḥ
d aśvānāṃ stanatāṃ śabdo vahatāṃ pākaśāsanim
d rathasyāmbudharasyeva śrūyate bhṛśadāruṇaḥ
d dārayann iva tejasvī vasudhāṃ vāsavātmajaḥ
d eṣa udāra āyāti rathe ca rathināṃ varaḥ
a eṣa tiṣṭhan rathaśreṣṭho rathe rathavarapraṇut
b eṣa dṛṣṭvā rathānīkam asmākam arimardanaḥ
b hrīmān vadānyo dhṛtimān satkaroti ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c utkarṣati dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ gāṇḍīvam aśanisvanam
a imau hi bāṇau sahitau pādayor me vyavasthitau
b bandhur āgrau nikhātau me citrapuṅkhāvajihmagau
c aparau cāpy atikrāntau karṇau saṃspṛśya me śarau
d saṃspṛśantāvatikrāntau pṛṣṭvaivānāmayaṃ bhṛśam
d ciradṛṣṭo 'yam asmābhiḥ prajñāvān bāndhavapriyaḥ
d atīva jvalito lakṣmyā pāṇḍuputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a niruṣya hi vane vāsaṃ kṛtvā karmātimānuṣam
c abhivādayate pārthaḥ śrotre ca paripṛcchati
d kuśalaṃ paripṛṣṭvā ca gatās te kaṅkavāsasaḥ
d amarṣeṇābhisaṃpūrṇo duḥkhena pratibodhitaḥ
d adyemāṃ bhāratīṃ senām eko nāśayate dhruvam
d dvyadhikaṃ daśa uṣya vatsarāṇāṃ
d svajanenāviditas trayodaśaṃ ca
d jvalate ratham āsthitaḥ kirīṭī
d tama iva rātrijam abhyudasya sūryaḥ
d rathī śarī cārutalī niṣaṅgī
d śaṅkhī patākī kavacī kirīṭī
d khaḍgī ca dhanvī ca vibhāti pārthaḥ
d śikhī vṛtaḥ srugbhir ivājyasiktaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tam adūram upāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavam arjunam
d nārayaḥ prekṣituṃ śekus tapasyantaṃ yathā ravim
d sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā rathānīkaṃ pārthaḥ sārathim abravīt
 arjuna uvāca
a iṣupāte ca senāyā hayān saṃyaccha sārathe
c yāvat samīkṣe sainye 'smin kvāsau kurukulādhamaḥ
d ratnavaiḍūryavikṛtaṃ maṇipravarabhūṣitam
d parijānāmy ahaṃ tasya dhvajaṃ dūrāt samucchritam
d yady enam iha paśyāmi durbuddhim atimāninam
d yamāya preṣayiṣyāmi sahāyo 'sya yadīśvaraḥ
a sarvān anyān anādṛtya dṛṣṭvā tam atimāninam
c tasya mūrdhni patiṣyāmi tata ete parājitāḥ
a eṣa vyavasthito droṇo drauṇiś ca tadanantaram
c bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaś ca karṇaś ca maheṣvāsā vyavasthitāḥ
a rājānaṃ nātra paśyāmi gāḥ samādāya gacchati
c dakṣiṇaṃ mārgam āsthāya śaṅke jīvaparāyaṇaḥ
a utsṛjyaitad rathānīkaṃ gaccha yatra suyodhanaḥ
c tatraiva yotsye vairāṭe nāsti yuddhaṃ nirāmiṣam
e taṃ jitvā vinivartiṣye gāḥ samādāya vai punaḥ
f c siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgasyeva patiṣye tasya mūrdhani
f haniṣyāmi tam evāśu śarair gāṇḍīvaniḥsṛtaiḥ
f d tasmin hate bhaviṣyanti sarva eva parājitāḥ
f śaraiḥ samarpayiṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sasaubalam
f asabhyānāṃ ca vaktāraṃ kurūṇāṃ kila kilbiṣam
f ad rājānaṃ neha paśyāmi nirāmiṣam idaṃ balam
f abhidrave ha rājānaṃ vyaktam ity atra nirbhayaḥ
f ab āsthito madhyamācāryo hy aśvatthāmā tv anantaram
f cd kṛpakarṇau purastāt tu maheṣvāsau vyavasthitau
f bhūriśravāḥ somadatto bāhlīkaś ca jayadrathaḥ
f c dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā yuddhaviśāradāḥ
f sālvarājo dyumatseno vṛṣasenaś ca saubalaḥ
f daśārṇaś caiva kāliṅgo vāmaṃ pakṣaṃ samāśritāḥ
f pṛṣṭhataḥ kurumukhyas tu bhīṣmas tiṣṭhati daṃsitaḥ
f ardhasainyena balavān sarveṣāṃ naḥ pitāmahaḥ
f ab duryodhanaṃ na paśyāmi kva nu rājā sa gacchati
f ab utsṛjaitad rathānīkaṃ yāhi yatra suyodhanaḥ
f ef taṃ hatvā vinivartiṣye gāḥ sa ādāya gacchati
f gavāgram abhito yāhi yatra rājā bhaviṣyati
f ity uktvā samare pārtho vairāṭim aparājitaḥ
f saṃspṛśāno dhanur divyaṃ tvaramāṇo 'gamat tadā
f tato bhīṣmo 'bravīd vākyaṃ kurumadhye paraṃtapaḥ
f ciradṛṣṭo 'yam asmābhir dharmajño bāndhavapriyaḥ
f atīva jvalate lakṣmyā pākaśāsanir acyutaḥ
f eṣa duryodhanaṃ pārtho mārgate vikṛtiṃ smaran
f senām atyartham ālokya tvarate grahaṇe kṛtam
f mṛgaṃ siṃha ivādātum īkṣate pākaśāsaniḥ
f paścād ete pradātavyā iti me vartate matiḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ sa vairāṭir hayān saṃyamya yatnataḥ
c niyamya ca tato raśmīn yatra te kurupuṃgavāḥ
e acodayat tato vāhān yato duryodhanas tataḥ
a utsṛjya rathavaṃśaṃ tu prayāte śvetavāhane
c abhiprāyaṃ viditvāsya droṇo vacanam abravīt
a naiṣo 'ntareṇa rājānaṃ bībhatsuḥ sthātum icchati
c tasya pārṣṇiṃ grahīṣyāmo javenābhiprayāsyataḥ
a na hy enam abhisaṃkruddham eko yudhyeta saṃyuge
c anyo devāt sahasrākṣāt kṛṣṇād vā devakīsutāt
d ācāryapravarād vāpi bhāradvājān mahārathāt
a kiṃ no gāvaḥ kariṣyanti dhanaṃ vā vipulaṃ tathā
c duryodhanaḥ pārthajale purā naur iva majjati
d ity uktvā samare bhīṣmaḥ senayā saha kauravaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d anvadhāvat tadā pārthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya rakṣaṇe
d trikośamātraṃ gatvā tu pārtho vairāṭim abravīt
d iṣupātena senāyāḥ sthāpayāśvān ariṃdama
d etad agraṃ gavāṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mandaṃ vāhaya sārathe
d yāhy uttareṇa senāyā gāś caiva pravibhajya ca
d parikṣipya gavāṃ yūtham atra yotsye suyodhanam
d gacchanti satvaraṃ gāvaḥ sagopāḥ parimocaya
d tatra gatvā paśūn vīra sagopān parimocaya
d antareṇa ca senāyāḥ prāṅmukho gaccha cottara
d ime tv atirathāḥ sarve mama vīryaparākramam
d paśyantu kuravo yuddhe mahendrasyeva dānavāḥ
a tathaiva gatvā bībhatsur nāma viśrāvya cātmanaḥ
b niśitāgrāñ charāṃs tīkṣṇān mumocāntakasaṃnibhān
c śalabhair iva tāṃ senāṃ śaraiḥ śīghram avākirat
d nirāvakāśam abhavac charaiḥ kṣiptaiḥ kirīṭinā
d sā cāpi bahulā senā pārthabāṇābhipīḍitā
a kīryamāṇāḥ śaraughais tu yodhās te pārthacoditaiḥ
c nāpaśyan nāvṛtāṃ bhūmim antarikṣaṃ ca patribhiḥ
d gāś caiva hi na paśyanti pārthamuktair ajihmagaiḥ
d arjunas tu tadā hṛṣṭo darśayan vīryam ātmanaḥ
d pīḍayām āsa sainyāni gāṇḍīvaprasṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ
a teṣāṃ nātmanino yuddhe nāpayāne 'bhavan matiḥ
c śīghratvam eva pārthasya pūjayanti sma cetasā
d candrāvadātaṃ sāmudraṃ kurusainyabhayaṃkaram
a tataḥ śaṅkhaṃ pradadhmau sa dviṣatāṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c visphārya ca dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ dhvaje bhūtāny acodayat
a tasya śaṅkhasya śabdena rathanemisvanena ca
b gāṇḍīvasya ca ghoṣeṇa pṛthivī samakampata
c amānuṣāṇāṃ teṣāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhvajavāsinām
d śabdena mahatā rājan saṃtrastaṃ godhanaṃ mahat
d viyadgatānāṃ devānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ raveṇa ca
a ūrdhvaṃ pucchān vidhunvānā rebhamāṇāḥ samantataḥ
c gāvaḥ pratinyavartanta diśam āsthāya dakṣiṇām
d tataḥ sa samare vīro bībhatsuḥ śatrupūgahā
d gopālāṃś codayām āsa gāś caitāś codayeti ca
d uttaraṃ cāha bībhatsur harṣayan pāṇḍunandanaḥ
d gavām agraṃ samīkṣasva gāś caivāśu nivartaya
d yāvad ete nivartante kuravo javam āsthitāḥ
d yāhy uttareṇa gāś caitāḥ sainyānāṃ ca nṛpātmaja
d paśyantu kuravaḥ sarve mama vīryaparākramam
d te lābham iva manvānāḥ kuravo 'rjunam āhave
d dṛṣṭvā yāntam adūrasthaṃ kṣipram abhyapatan rathaiḥ
d hastyaśvaparivāreṇa mahatābhivirājatā
d yodhaiḥ prāsāsihastaiś ca cāpabāṇodyatāyudhaiḥ
d tāny anīkāny aśobhanta kurūṇām ātatāyinām
d saṃsarpanta ivākāśe vidyutvanto balāhakāḥ
d tāni dṛṣṭvā hy anīkāni nivartitarathāni ca
d pārtho 'pi vāyuvad ghoraṃ sainyāgraṃ vyadhunoc charaiḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa śatrusenāṃ tarasā praṇudya
gās tā vijityātha dhanurdharāgryaḥ
c duryodhanāyābhimukhaṃ prayāto
bhūyo 'rjunaḥ priyam ājau cikīrṣan
a goṣu prayātāsu javena matsyān
kirīṭinaṃ kṛtakāryaṃ ca matvā
b paśūn samādāya tato nivṛttā
b gopāgaṇāḥ svān prayayuś ca rāṣṭrān
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b tatas trīṇi sahasrāṇi rathānāṃ ca dhanuṣmatām
b ghorāṇi kuruvīrāṇāṃ paryakīryanta bhārata
b karṇo rathasahasreṇa pratyatiṣṭhad dhanaṃjayam
b bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo dhīmān sahasreṇa puraskṛtaḥ
b tathā rathasahasreṇa bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
b paścād duryodhano 'tiṣṭhad dhastāvāpī śriyā jvalan
b atiṣṭhann avakāśeṣu pādātāḥ saha vājibhiḥ
b bhīmarūpāś ca mātaṅgās tomarāṅkuśacoditāḥ
b tāni dṛṣṭvā hy anīkāni vitatāni mahātmanām
b vairāṭim uttaraṃ taṃ tu pratyabhāṣata pāṇḍavaḥ
b varmitā vājino 'tiṣṭhan sahārūḍhaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
b tatra tatrāvakāśeṣu pādātāś ca sahasraśaḥ
c duryodhanāyābhimukhaṃ prayāntaṃ
kurupravīrāḥ sahasābhipetuḥ
d uttara uvāca
d puraṃ pratinivartasva pārtha praharatāṃ vara
d gāvas tvayā jitāś cemāḥ kiṃ yuddheneti vai vṛthā
d saṃdigdhe 'rthe na yudhyeta puṣṭe vāpi bale sati
d tvayaikena bahūnāṃ hi vigraheṇa tu kiṃ vṛthā
d śrutvaitad arjuno vākyaṃ vairāṭer bhītavat tadā
d prahasya prāha taṃ bhūyo mā bhaiḥ paśyeha kautukam
d bahūni dṛṣṭapūrvāṇi prāg yuddhāny uttara tvayā
d paśyemam evaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ bahūnām ekakena yat
d tato duryodhanaṃ yāntam arjunaṃ tarasā tadā
d rathāgryāḥ kauravendrasya nipetuḥ sahasākhilāḥ
a teṣām anīkāni bahūni gāḍhaṃ
vyūḍhāni dṛṣṭvā bahuladhvajāni
c matsyasya putraṃ dviṣatāṃ nihantā
vairāṭim āmantrya tato 'bhyuvāca
d arjunaḥ
d susaṃgṛhītair atha raśmibhis tvaṃ
d hayān niyamya prasamīkṣya yattaḥ
d saṃpreṣayāśu prativīram enaṃ
d vaikartanaṃ yodhayituṃ vṛṇomi
d yāṃ hastikakṣyāṃ bahudhā vicitrāṃ
d stambhe rathe paśyasi darśanīyām
d vivartamānaṃ jvalanaprakāśaṃ
d vaikartanasyaitad anīkam agryam
a etena tūrṇaṃ pratipādayemāñ
śvetān hayān kāñcanaraśmiyoktrān
c javena sarveṇa kuru prayatnam
āsādayaitad rathasiṃhavṛndam
a gajo gajeneva mayā durātmā
yo yoddhum ākāṅkṣati sūtaputraḥ
b tad adya yuddhaṃ kuruvīramadhye
b karomi taṃ yāhi tathāpravṛttaḥ
c tam eva māṃ prāpaya rājaputra
duryodhanāpāśrayajātadarpam
d taṃ pātayiṣyāmi rathasya madhye
d sahasranetro 'śanineva vṛtram
d gāṇḍīvamuktair iṣubhiḥ sitāgraiḥ
d śaraiḥ sutīkṣṇair hṛdayaṃ vibhidya
a sa tair hayair vātajavair bṛhadbhiḥ
putro virāṭasya suvarṇakakṣyaiḥ
c vidhvaṃsayaṃs tadrathinām anīkaṃ
tato 'vahat pāṇḍavam ājimadhye
d tam āpatantaṃ parameṇa tejasā
d samīkṣya vaikartanam abhyarakṣan
d abhyadravaṃs te rathavīravṛndā
d vyāghreṇa cākrāntam ivarṣabhaṃ raṇe
d citrāṅgadaś citrarathaś ca vīraḥ
d saṃgrāmajid duḥsahacitrasenau
d viviṃśatir durjayadurmukhau ca
d vikarṇaduḥśāsanasaubalāś ca
d śoṇo niṣedhaś ca tam anvayus te
d vaikartanaṃ śīghrataraṃ yuvānaḥ
d putrā yayus te sahasodarāś ca
d vaikartanaṃ pārthagataṃ samīkṣya
d pragṛhya cāpāni mahābalā raṇe
d dhanaṃjayaṃ paryakirañ charaughaiḥ
d teṣāṃ dṛḍhajyākṛtanaikatantrīṃ
d prāsopavīṇāṃ śarasaṃghakoṇām
d karāgrayantrāṃ sthiracāpadaṇḍāṃ
d vīṇām upāvādayad āśu pārthaḥ
a taṃ citraseno viśikhair vipāṭhaiḥ
saṃgrāmajic chatrusaho jayaś ca
c pratyudyayur bhāratam āpatantaṃ
mahārathāḥ karṇam abhīpsamānāḥ
a tataḥ sa teṣāṃ puruṣapravīraḥ
śarāsanārciḥ śaravegatāpaḥ
c vrātān rathānām adahat sa manyur
vanaṃ yathāgniḥ kurupuṃgavānām
a tasmiṃs tu yuddhe tumule pravṛtte
pārthaṃ vikarṇo 'tirathaṃ rathena
c vipāṭhavarṣeṇa kurupravīro
bhīmena bhīmānujam āsasāda
a tato vikarṇasya dhanur vikṛṣya
jāmbūnadāgryopacitaṃ dṛḍhajyam
c apātayad dhvajam asya pramathya
chinnadhvajaḥ so 'py apayāj javena
a taṃ śātravāṇāṃ gaṇabādhitāraṃ
karmāṇi kurvāṇam amānuṣāṇi
c śatruṃtapaḥ kopam amṛṣyamāṇaḥ
samarpayat kūrmanakhena pārtham
a sa tena rājñātirathena viddho
vigāhamāno dhvajinīṃ kurūṇām
c śatruṃtapaṃ pañcabhir āśu viddhvā
tato 'sya sūtaṃ daśabhir jaghāna
a tataḥ sa viddho bharatarṣabheṇa
bāṇena gātrāvaraṇātigena
c gatāsur ājau nipapāta bhūmau
nago nagāgrād iva vātarugṇaḥ
a ratharṣabhās te tu ratharṣabheṇa
vīrā raṇe vīratareṇa bhagnāḥ
c cakampire vātavaśena kāle
prakampitānīva mahāvanāni
a hatās tu pārthena narapravīrā
bhūmau yuvānaḥ suṣupuḥ suveṣāḥ
c vasupradā vāsavatulyavīryāḥ
parājitā vāsavajena saṃkhye
e suvarṇakārṣṇāyasavarmanaddhā
nāgā yathā haimavatāḥ pravṛddhāḥ
a tathā sa śatrūn samare vinighnan
gāṇḍīvadhanvā puruṣapravīraḥ
c cacāra saṃkhye pradiśo diśaś ca
dahann ivāgnir vanam ātapānte
a prakīrṇaparṇāni yathā vasante
viśātayitvātyanilo nudan khe
c tathā sapatnān vikiran kirīṭī
cacāra saṃkhye 'tiratho rathena
a śoṇāśvavāhasya hayān nihatya
vaikartanabhrātur adīnasattvaḥ
c ekena saṃgrāmajitaḥ śareṇa
śiro jahārātha kirīṭamālī
a tasmin hate bhrātari sūtaputro
vaikartano vīryam athādadānaḥ
c pragṛhya dantāv iva nāgarājo
maharṣabhaṃ vyāghra ivābhyadhāvat
a sa pāṇḍavaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkair
vaikartanaḥ śīghram upājaghāna
c vivyādha gātreṣu hayāṃś ca sarvān
virāṭaputraṃ ca śarair nijaghne
d tam āpatantaṃ sahasā kirīṭī
d vaikartanaṃ vai tarasābhipatya
d pragṛhya vegaṃ nyapataj javena
d nāgaṃ garutmān iva citrapakṣaḥ
d tāv uttamau sarvadhanurdharāṇāṃ
d mahābalau sarvasapatnasāhau
d karṇasya pārthasya niśamya yuddhaṃ
d didṛkṣamāṇāḥ kuravo 'bhitasthuḥ
d sa pāṇḍavas tūrṇam udīrṇakopaḥ
d kṛtāgasaṃ karṇam udīkṣya harṣāt
d kṣaṇena sāśvaṃ sarathaṃ sasārathim
d antardadhe ghoraśaraughavṛṣṭyā
d tataḥ suviddhāḥ sarathāḥ sanāgā
d yodhā vinedur bharatarṣabhāṇām
d antarhitā bhīṣmamukhāḥ sahāśvāḥ
d kirīṭinā kīrṇarathāḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d sa cāpi tān arjunabāhumuktāñ
d śarāñ śaraughaiḥ pratihatya karṇaḥ
d tasthau mahātmā sadhanuḥ sabāṇaḥ
d savisphuliṅgo 'gnir ivāśu karṇaḥ
d tatas tu jajñe talatālaśabdaḥ
d saśaṅkhabherīpraṇavapraṇādaḥ
d prakṣveḍitajyātalanisvanaṃ taṃ
d vaikartanaṃ pūjayatāṃ kurūṇām
d uddhūtalāṅgūlamahāpatākaṃ
d dhvajottamaṃ sākulabhīṣayantam
d gāṇḍīvanirhrādakṛtapraṇādaṃ
d kirīṭinaṃ prekṣya nanāda karṇaḥ
d sa cāpi vaikartanam ardayitvā
d sāśvaṃ sasūtaṃ sarathaṃ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d tam āvavarṣa prasabhaṃ kirīṭī
d pitāmahaṃ droṇakṛpau ca dṛṣṭvā
d sa cāpi pārthaṃ bahubhiḥ pṛṣatkair
d vaikartano megha ivābhyavarṣat
d tathaiva karṇaṃ ca kirīṭamālī
d saṃchādayām āsa śitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d tayoḥ sutīkṣṇān sṛjatoḥ śaraughān
d mahāśaraughāstravivardhane raṇe
d rathe vilagnāv iva candrasūryau
d ghanāntareṇānudadarśa lokaḥ
d athāśukārī caturo hayāṃś ca
d vivyādha karṇo niśitaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ
d tribhiś ca yantāram amṛṣyamāṇo
d vivyādha tūrṇaṃ tribhir asya ketum
d tenātividdhaḥ samarāvamardī
d prabodhitaḥ siṃha iva prasuptaḥ
d gāṇḍīvadhanvā ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇām
d ajihmagaiḥ karṇam iyāya jiṣṇuḥ
d śarāstravṛṣṭyā nihato mahātmā
d prāduścakārātimanuṣyakarma
d prācchādayat karṇarathaṃ pṛṣatkair
d lokān imān sūrya ivāṃśujālaiḥ
a sa hastinevābhihato gajendraḥ
pragṛhya bhallān niśitān niṣaṅgāt
c ākarṇapūrṇaṃ ca dhanur vikṛṣya
vivyādha bāṇair atha sūtaputram
a athāsya bāhūruśirolalāṭaṃ
grīvāṃ rathāṅgāni parāvamardī
c sthitasya bāṇair yudhi nirbibheda
gāṇḍīvamuktair aśaniprakāśaiḥ
a sa pārthamuktair viśikhaiḥ praṇunno
gajo gajeneva jitas tarasvī
c vihāya saṃgrāmaśiraḥ prayāto
vaikartanaḥ pāṇḍavabāṇataptaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a apayāte tu rādheye duryodhanapurogamāḥ
c anīkena yathāsvena śarair ārcchanta pāṇḍavam
a bahudhā tasya sainyasya vyūḍhasyāpatataḥ śaraiḥ
b tataḥ prahasya bībhatsuḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ
b divyam astraṃ prakurvāṇaḥ pratyayād rathasattamān
b yathā raśmibhir ādityaḥ pracchādayati medinīm
b tathā gāṇḍīvanirmuktāś chādayanti śarā diśaḥ
b na rathānāṃ na cāśvānāṃ na dhvajānāṃ na varmaṇām
b atividdhaiḥ śitair bāṇair āsīd dvyaṅgulam antaram
b daivayogād dhi pārthasya hayānām uttarasya ca
b śikṣābalopapannatvād astrāṇāṃ ca parikramāt
b dhvajagāṇḍīvayoś cāpi daivī māyākṛteti ca
b itas tataś ca saṃyāne dūre vāpy atha vāntike
b durge viṣamajāte vā sthale nimne tathā kṣitau
b na ca rudhyed gatis tasya rathasya manaso yathā
b samareṣu tu vidvāṃsas tasya tāṃs tān parākramān
b vīryam atyadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathā pārthasya tad balam
b tresur eva pare bhītāḥ parāṅmukharathā api
b kālāgnim iva bībhatsuṃ nirdahantam iva prajāḥ
b nārayaḥ prekṣituṃ śekur jvalantam iva pāvakam
b tāni bhinnāny anīkāni rejur arjunamārgaṇaiḥ
b tigmāṃśoś ca vanāgrāṇi vyāptānīva gabhastibhiḥ
b aśokānāṃ vanānīva saṃcitaiḥ kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ
b pārthaḥ saṃrañjayām āsa rudhireṇākulaṃ balam
b sahasraśo 'rjunaśaraiś chinnāny uccāvacāni ca
b chatrāṇi ca patākāś ca khe 'bhyuvāha sadāgatiḥ
b ye hy arjunabalatrastāḥ paripetur diśo daśa
b rathāṅgadeśam utsṛjya pārthacchinnayugā hayāḥ
b nikṛttapūrvacaraṇās te nipetuḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
b śirobhiḥ prathamaṃ jagmur medinīṃ jaghanair hayāḥ
b cakṣur nakhaviṣāṇeṣu dantaveṣṭeṣu ca dvipān
b marmasv anyeṣu cāhatya tathā nighnan gajottamān
b kauravāṇāṃ gajānāṃ tu śarīrair gatacetasām
b kṣaṇena saṃvṛtā bhūmir meghair iva nabhastalam
b astrair divyair mahābāhur arjunaḥ pradahann iva
b vaḍavāmukhasaṃbhūtaḥ kālāgnir iva sarvataḥ
b yathā yugāntasamaye sarvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
b kālapakvam aśeṣeṇa dhakṣyed ugraśikhaḥ śikhī
b tadvat pārtho 'stratejobhir dhanuṣo nisvanena ca
b daivād vīryāc ca bībhatsus tasmin dauryodhane bale
b raṇaśaktim amitrāṇāṃ prāyeṇāpanināya saḥ
b ceṣṭāṃ prāyeṇa bhūtānāṃ rātriḥ prāṇabhṛtām iva
b so 'tīyāt sahasā śatrūn sahasā cābhipedivān
b śīghraṃ dūraṃ dṛḍhāmogham astram asyātimānuṣam
b khagayānābhisaṃvītaiḥ khaṃviṣṭaiḥ khagamair iva
b arjunena kham āvavre lohitaprāṇapaiḥ khagaiḥ
b arjunāstravinirmuktāḥ śarā gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
b tārkṣyavegā ivākāśe na sasarjuḥ parātmasu
b varmāṇi sārathīṃś caiva haimajālāni vājinām

a asaṃbhrānto rathe tiṣṭha sameṣu viṣameṣu ca

a aham indrasya vacanāt saṃgrāme 'bhyahanaṃ purā
b mātaliṃ sārathiṃ kṛtvā nivātakavacān raṇe

d mayā kurūṇāṃ vṛndāni pātyamānāni paśya vai

b rathasiṃhagaṇair yuktaṃ dhanur vallīsamākulam

b sauryaṃ sūryād ahaṃ vedmi yāmyaṃ daṇḍadharād api

d ādānasaṃdhānavikarṣaṇādi

d divyāstrayoge khalu ye prakārās
d tattadguromukhataḥ śikṣitā me
d prasthāpanaṃ yad divyāstraṃ tathā saṃmohanaṃ param

d anye 'pi citrābharaṇā yuvāno mṛṣṭakuṇḍalāḥ
a taṃ citramālyābharaṇāḥ kṛtavidyā manasvinaḥ
c āgacchan bhīmadhanvānaṃ maurvīṃ paryasya bāhubhiḥ
a duḥśāsano vikarṇaś ca duḥsaho 'tha viviṃśatiḥ
c āgatya bhīmadhanvānaṃ bībhatsuṃ paryavārayan

a taṃ vikarṇaḥ śarais tīkṣṇair gārdhrapatrair ajihmagaiḥ

a tatas tam api kaunteyaḥ śareṇānataparvaṇā
c lalāṭe 'bhyahanat tūrṇaṃ sa viddhaḥ prāpatad rathāt
a tataḥ pārtham abhidrutya duḥsahaḥ saviviṃśatiḥ
c avākirac charais tīkṣṇaiḥ parīpsan bhrātaraṃ raṇe
a tāv ubhau gārdhrapatrābhyāṃ niśitābhyāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ
c viddhvā yugapad avyagras tayor vāhān asūdayat
a tau hatāśvau vividdhāṅgau dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajāv ubhau
c abhipatya rathair anyair apanītau padānugaiḥ
d tathaiva kruddhaḥ subalasya putro
d bāṇaiś ca pītair niśitair dhanurdharam
d tribhiś ca vivyādha nanāda śūraḥ
d punaś ca vivyādha tribhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā samāyāntaṃ nadantaṃ raṇamūrdhani
d jagrāha śūro niśitāṃs trayodaśa śilīmukhān
d ekena cāpaṃ hastāc ca caturbhiś caturo hayān
d dvābhyāṃ ca mukuṭaṃ tasya śiras tv ekena sārathiḥ

d tathā tadainaṃ hṛdaye tribhir bāṇair ajihmagaiḥ

d vidrāvya ca raṇe pārtho raṇabhūmiṃ vyarājayat

d adṛśyata śiraś chinnam anīkaṃ hemakuṇḍalam
d evaṃ tat prahataṃ sainyaṃ samantāt pradrutaṃ bhayāt
d sarvā diśaś cānudiśaḥ kaunteyasyābhito ratham
d arjunasya śarās tīkṣṇā gāṇḍīvāt tasya niḥsṛtāḥ
d dhāvanta iva pārthasya niramitraṃ cikīrṣavaḥ
d yayuḥ puṅkhāgrapātena phalgunasya patatriṇaḥ
d ādadānā rathebhyaś ca prāṇān bāhūñ śirāṃsi ca
d ākāśe samadṛśyanta haṃsānām iva paṅktayaḥ
d kṣipato laghu citraṃ ca savyaṃ dakṣiṇam asyataḥ
d pārthasya viśikhā jagmuḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
d pramathann uttamāṅgāni sotsedhāni dhanuṣmatām
d prāhiṇot triśataṃ yodhān kurūṇām ātatāyinām
d pravṛttān rathanīḍebhyaḥ kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ
d pragāḍhadhanvā kaunteyo labdhalakṣaḥ pratāpavān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a atha saṃgamya sarve tu kauravāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ
c arjunaṃ sahitā yattāḥ pratyayudhyanta bhārata
d etasminn antare kruddho bhīṣmo droṇam athābravīt
d dṛṣṭvā kṛpaṃ phalgunena pīḍitaṃ ca jitaṃ raṇe
d ekaikam asmān saṃgrāme parājayati phalgunaḥ
d ahaṃ droṇaś ca karṇaś ca drauṇir gautama eva ca
d anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā vayaṃ jeṣyāma vāsavim
a sa sāyakamayair jālaiḥ sarvatas tān mahārathān
c prācchādayad ameyātmā nīhāra iva parvatān
a nadadbhiś ca mahānāgair heṣamāṇaiś ca vājibhiḥ
c bherīśaṅkhaninādaiś ca sa śabdas tumulo 'bhavat
a narāśvakāyān nirbhidya lohāni kavacāni ca
c pārthasya śarajālāni viniṣpetuḥ sahasraśaḥ
a tvaramāṇaḥ śarān asyan pāṇḍavaḥ sa babhau raṇe
c madhyaṃdinagato 'rciṣmāñ śaradīva divākaraḥ

c trastāni sarvabhūtāni vyagacchanta mahāhavāt

a darśayitvā tathātmānaṃ raudraṃ rudraparākramaḥ
b jaghāna samare yodhāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c avaruddhaś caran pārtho daśavarṣāṇi trīṇi ca

a tasya tad dahataḥ sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā caiva parākramam
c sarve śāntiparā yodhā dhārtarāṣṭrasya paśyataḥ
d yathā nalavanaṃ nāgaḥ prabhinnaḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanaḥ
d paraṃ sarvān apāmṛdnād arjunaḥ śastratejasā
a vitrāsayitvā tat sainyaṃ drāvayitvā mahārathān
c arjuno jayatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paryavartata bhārata
d tasya mārgān vicarato nighnataś ca raṇājire
a prāvartayan nadīṃ ghorāṃ śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīm
c asthiśaivalasaṃbādhāṃ yugānte kālanirmitām
a śaracāpaplavāṃ ghorāṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamām
b tanutroṣṇīṣasaṃbādhāṃ nāgakūrmamahādvipām
b medovasāsṛk pravahāṃ mahābhayavivardhinīm
b raudrarūpāṃ mahābhīmāṃ śvāpadair abhināditām
b tīkṣṇaśastramahāgrāhāṃ kravyādagaṇasevitām
b muktāhārormikalilāṃ citrālaṃkārabhūṣitām

b raudrarūpāṃ mahābhīmāṃ śaradundubhiniḥsvanām
b prāvartayan nadīṃ ghorāṃ piśācagaṇasevitām
b karavālāsipāṭhīnāṃ cāmaroṣṇīṣaphenilām
b aśvagrīvamahāvartāṃ kabandhajalamānuṣām
b kākakaṅkarutāṃ tīvrāṃ sārasakrauñcanāditām
c mahārathamahādvīpāṃ śaṅkhadundubhinisvanām
d siṃhanādamahānādāṃ śaṅkhakambukasaṃkulām

d padātimatsyakalilāṃ gajaśīrṣakakacchapām
d gomāyumṛgasaṃghuṣṭāṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamām
d prāvartayan nadīṃ ghorāṃ piśācagaṇasevitām
d apārām anapārāṃ ca raktodāṃ sarvato vṛtām
e cakāra mahatīṃ pārtho nadīm uttaraśoṇitām
f gajavarṣmamahādvīpām aśvadehamahāśilām
f padātidehasaṃghāṭāṃ rathāvalimahātarum
f keśaśāḍvalasaṃcchannāṃ sutarāṃ bhītidāṃ nṛṇām

f dustarāṃ bhīrumartyānāṃ śūrāṇāṃ sutarāṃ nṛpa
f prāvartayan nadīm evaṃ bhīṣaṇāṃ pākaśāsaniḥ
a ādadānasya hi śarān saṃdhāya ca vimuñcataḥ
c vikarṣataś ca gāṇḍīvaṃ na kiṃ cid dṛśyate 'ntaram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a atha duryodhanaḥ karṇo duḥśāsanaviviṃśatī
c droṇaś ca saha putreṇa kṛpaś cātiratho raṇe
a punar īyuḥ susaṃrabdhā dhanaṃjayajighāṃsayā
c visphārayantaś cāpāni balavanti dṛḍhāni ca
a tān prakīrṇapatākena rathenādityavarcasā
c pratyudyayau mahārāja samastān vānaradhvajaḥ
a tataḥ kṛpaś ca karṇaś ca droṇaś ca rathināṃ varaḥ
c taṃ mahāstrair mahāvīryaṃ parivārya dhanaṃjayam
d abhyavarṣan susaṃkruddhā mahāmeghā ivācalam
a śaraughān samyag asyanto jīmūtā iva vārṣikāḥ
c vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi prapatantaṃ kirīṭinam
a iṣubhir bahubhis tūrṇaṃ samare lomavāhibhiḥ
c adūrāt paryavasthāya pūrayām āsur ādṛtāḥ
d nottarasya ca gātrāṇāṃ cakrayor na ca vājinām
a tathāvakīrṇasya hi tair divyair astraiḥ samantataḥ
c na tasya dvyaṅgulam api vivṛtaṃ samadṛśyata
a tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur divyam aindraṃ mahārathaḥ
c astram ādityasaṃkāśaṃ gāṇḍīve samayojayat
d mohayitvā tu tān sarvān sa tatra hy astratejasā
d ardayām āsa vai bāṇair arjunaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
d duryodhanaṃ trisaptatyā śakuniṃ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ
d droṇam ekena bāṇena kṛpaṃ dvābhyāṃ mahābalaḥ
d aśītyā sūtaputraṃ tu ṣaṣṭyā drauṇiṃ tathaiva ca
d duḥśāsanamukhān sarvān sa tatra hy astratejasā
d ardayām āsa tair bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavo 'strabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d nākṣāṇāṃ na ca cakrāṇāṃ na rathānāṃ na vājinām
a sa raśmibhir ivādityaḥ pratapan samare balī
c kirīṭamālī kaunteyaḥ sarvān prācchādayat kurūn
a yathā balāhake vidyut pāvako vā śiloccaye
c tathā gāṇḍīvam abhavad indrāyudham ivātatam
a yathā varṣati parjanye vidyud vibhrājate divi
b dyotayantī diśaḥ sarvāḥ pṛthivīṃ ca samantataḥ
c tathā daśa diśaḥ sarvāḥ patad gāṇḍīvam āvṛṇot
a trastāś ca rathinaḥ sarve babhūvus tatra sarvaśaḥ
c sarve śāntiparā bhūtvā svacittāni na lebhire
d evaṃ te sainikās tatra dhārtarāṣṭrasya paśyataḥ
e saṃgrāmavimukhāḥ sarve yodhās te hatacetasaḥ
a evaṃ sarvāṇi sainyāni bhagnāni bharatarṣabha
c prādravanta diśaḥ sarvā nirāśāni svajīvite
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo durādharṣaḥ pratāpavān
c vadhyamāneṣu yodheṣu dhanaṃjayam upādravat
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d evaṃ vidrāvya tat sainyaṃ pārtho bhīṣmam upādravat
d trasteṣu sarvasainyeṣu kauravyasya mahātmanaḥ
d narasiṃham upāyāntaṃ jigīṣantaṃ parān raṇe
d vṛṣaseno 'bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ yoddhukāmo dhanaṃjayam
d tasya pārthas tadā kṣipraṃ kṣuradhāreṇa kārmukam
d nyakṛntad gṛdhrapatreṇa jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
d athainaṃ pañcabhir bhūyaḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
