d duḥśāsano vikarṇaś ca śakuniś ca viviṃśatiḥ
d āyāntaṃ bhīmadhanvānaṃ paryakīryanta pāṇḍavam
d teṣāṃ pārtho raṇe kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
d yugaṃ dhvajam atheṣāṃ ca ciccheda tarasā raṇe
d te nikṛttadhvajāḥ sarve chinnakārmukaveṣṭanāḥ
d raṇamadhyād apayayuḥ pārthabāṇābhipīḍitāḥ
d tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur vairāṭim idam abravīt
d etaṃ me prāpayedānīṃ tālaṃ sauvarṇam ucchritam
d meghamadhye yathā vidyud uccarantī punaḥ punaḥ
d asau śāṃtanavo bhīṣmas tatra yāhi paraṃtapa
d astrāṇi tasya divyāni darśayiṣyāmi saṃyuge
d ghorarūpāṇi citrāṇi laghūni ca gurūṇi ca
d tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vairāṭiḥ pārthasārathiḥ
d vāhayac coditas tena rathaṃ bhīṣmarathaṃ prati
d atha taṃ coditaṃ dṛṣṭvā phalgunasya rathottamam
d vāyuneva mahāmeghaṃ sahasābhisamīritam
d taṃ pratyayāc ca gāṅgeyo rathenādityavarcasā
d āyāntam arjunaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
d pratyujjagāma yuddhārthī maharṣabha ivarṣabham
a pragṛhya kārmukaśreṣṭhaṃ jātarūpapariṣkṛtam
c śarān ādāya tīkṣṇāgrān marmabhedapramāthinaḥ
a pāṇḍureṇātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani
c śuśubhe sa naravyāghro giriḥ sūryodaye yathā
a pradhmāya śaṅkhaṃ gāṅgeyo dhārtarāṣṭrān praharṣayan
c pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya bībhatsuṃ samavārayat
a tam udvīkṣya tathāyāntaṃ kaunteyaḥ paravīrahā
b devadattaṃ mahāśaṅkhaṃ pradadhmau yudhi vīryavān
b tau śaṅkhanādāvatyarthaṃ bhīṣmapāṇḍavayos tadā
b nādayām āsatur dyāṃ ca khaṃ ca bhūmiṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c pratyagṛhṇāt prahṛṣṭātmā dhārādharam ivācalaḥ
d antarikṣe prajalpanti sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
d yad arjunaḥ kurūn sarvān prākṛntac chastratejasā
d kuruśreṣṭhāv imau vīrau raṇe bhīṣmadhanaṃjayau
d sarvāstrakuśalau loke etāv atirathāv ubhau
d ubhau devamanuṣyeṣu viśrutau svaparākramaiḥ
d ubhau paramasaṃrabdhāv ubhau dīptadhanurdharau
d samāgatau naravyāghrau vyāghrāv iva tarasvinau
d ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau sūryasyāgneś ca bhārata
d vāsudevasya sadṛśau kārtavīryasamāv ubhau
d ubhau viśrutakarmāṇāv ubhau śūrau mahābalau
d sarvāstraviduṣāṃ śreṣṭhau sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varau
d agner indrasya somasya yamasya dhanadasya ca
d anayoḥ sadṛśaṃ vīryaṃ mitrasya varuṇasya ca
d ko vā kuntīsutaṃ yuddhe dvairathenopayāsyati
d ṛte śāṃtanavād anyaḥ kṣatriyo bhuvi vidyate
d iti saṃpūjayām āsur bhīṣmaṃ dṛṣṭvārjunaṃ gatam
d raṇe saṃprahariṣyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā devāḥ savāsavāḥ
d atha bahuvidhaśaṅkhatūryaghoṣair
d vividharavaiḥ saha siṃhanādamiśraiḥ
d kuruvṛṣabham apūjayat kurūṇāṃ
d balam amarādhiapasainyasaprabhaṃ tat
a tato bhīṣmaḥ śarān aṣṭau dhvaje pārthasya vīryavān
c samaparyan mahāvegāñ śvasamānān ivoragān
a te dhvajaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya samāsādya patatriṇaḥ
c jvalantaḥ kapim ājaghnur dhvajāgranilayāṃś ca tān
d sārathiṃ ca hayāṃś cāsya vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ
d urasy atāḍayat pārthaṃ tribhir evāyasaiḥ śaraiḥ
d tato 'rjunaḥ śarais tīkṣṇair viddhvā kurupitāmaham
a tato bhallena mahatā pṛthudhāreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
c chatraṃ ciccheda bhīṣmasya tūrṇaṃ tad apatad bhuvi
a dhvajaṃ caivāsya kaunteyaḥ śarair abhyahanad dṛḍham
c śīghrakṛd rathavāhāṃś ca tathobhau pārṣṇisārathī
d amṛṣyamāṇas tad bhīṣmo jānann api ca pāṇḍavam
d divyenāstreṇa mahatā dhanaṃjayam avākirat
d tathaiva pāṇḍavo bhīṣmaṃ divyam astram udīrayan
d pratyagṛhṇād adīnātmā mahāmegham ivācalaḥ
a tayos tad abhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
c bhīṣmasya saha pārthena balivāsavayor iva
d praikṣanta kuravaḥ sarve yodhāś ca sahasainikāḥ
d saṃtataṃ śaramālābhir ākāśaṃ samapadyata
d ambudair iva dhārābhis tayoḥ kārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥ
a bhallair bhallāḥ samāgamya bhīṣmapāṇḍavayor yudhi
c antarikṣe vyarājanta khadyotāḥ prāvṛṣīva hi
a agnicakram ivāviddhaṃ savyadakṣiṇam asyataḥ
c gāṇḍīvam abhavad rājan pārthasya sṛjataḥ śarān
a sa taiḥ saṃchādayām āsa bhīṣmaṃ śaraśataiḥ śitaiḥ
c parvataṃ vāridhārābhiś chādayann iva toyadaḥ
a tāṃ sa velām ivoddhūtāṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitām
c vyadhamat sāyakair bhīṣmo arjunaṃ saṃnivārayat
a tatas tāni nikṛttāni śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥ
c samare 'bhivyaśīryanta phalgunasya rathaṃ prati
a tataḥ kanakapuṅkhānāṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitām
c pāṇḍavasya rathāt tūrṇaṃ śalabhānām ivāyatim
e vyadhamat tāṃ punas tasya bhīṣmaḥ śaraśataiḥ śitaiḥ
f patadbhiḥ khagavājaiś ca dyaur āsīt saṃvṛtā śaraiḥ
f tataḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śarajālāni pāṇḍavaḥ
f tāvanti śarajālāni bhīṣmaḥ pārthāya prāhiṇot
f sāśvaṃ sasūtaṃ sarathaṃ ca pārthaṃ
f samācinod bhārata vatsadantaiḥ
f pracchādayām āsa diśaś ca sarvā
f nabhaś ca bāṇais tapanīyapuṅkhaiḥ
a tatas te kuravaḥ sarve sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan
c duṣkaraṃ kṛtavān bhīṣmo yad arjunam ayodhayat
a balavāṃs taruṇo dakṣaḥ kṣiprakārī ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c ko 'nyaḥ samarthaḥ pārthasya vegaṃ dhārayituṃ raṇe
a ṛte śāṃtanavād bhīṣmāt kṛṣṇād vā devakīsutāt
c ācāryapravarād vāpi bhāradvājān mahābalāt
a astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya krīḍataḥ puruṣarṣabhau
c cakṣūṃṣi sarvabhūtānāṃ mohayantau mahābalau
a prājāpatyaṃ tathaivaindram āgneyaṃ ca sudāruṇam
c kauberaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva yāmyaṃ vāyavyam eva ca
e prayuñjānau mahātmānau samare tau viceratuḥ
a vismitāny atha bhūtāni tau dṛṣṭvā saṃyuge tadā
c sādhu pārtha mahābāho sādhu bhīṣmeti cābruvan
a nedaṃ yuktaṃ manuṣyeṣu yo 'yaṃ saṃdṛśyate mahān
c mahāstrāṇāṃ saṃprayogaḥ samare bhīṣmapārthayoḥ
a evaṃ sarvāstraviduṣor astrayuddham avartata
b astrayuddhe tu nirvṛtte śarayuddham avartata
c atha jiṣṇur upāvṛtya pṛthudhāreṇa kārmukam
e cakarta bhīṣmasya tadā jātarūpapariṣkṛtam
a nimeṣāntaramātreṇa bhīṣmo 'nyat kārmukaṃ raṇe
c samādāya mahābāhuḥ sajyaṃ cakre mahābalaḥ
e śarāṃś ca subahūn kruddho mumocāśu dhanaṃjaye
a arjuno 'pi śarāṃś citrān bhīṣmāya niśitān bahūn
c cikṣepa sumahātejās tathā bhīṣmaś ca pāṇḍave
a tayor divyāstraviduṣor asyator aniśaṃ śarān
c na viśeṣas tadā rājaṃl lakṣyate sma mahātmanoḥ
a athāvṛṇod daśa diśaḥ śarair atirathas tadā
c kirīṭamālī kaunteyaḥ śūraḥ śāṃtanavas tathā
a atīva pāṇḍavo bhīṣmaṃ bhīṣmaś cātīva pāṇḍavam
c babhūva tasmin saṃgrāme rājaṃl loke tad adbhutam
a pāṇḍavena hatāḥ śūrā bhīṣmasya ratharakṣiṇaḥ
c śerate sma tadā rājan kaunteyasyābhito ratham
a tato gāṇḍīvanirmuktā niramitraṃ cikīrṣavaḥ
c āgacchan puṅkhasaṃśliṣṭāḥ śvetavāhanapatriṇaḥ
a niṣpatanto rathāt tasya dhautā hairaṇyavāsasaḥ
c ākāśe samadṛśyanta haṃsānām iva paṅktayaḥ
a tasya tad divyam astraṃ hi pragāḍhaṃ citram asyataḥ
c prekṣante smāntarikṣasthāḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvā paramaprīto gandharvaś citram adbhutam
c śaśaṃsa devarājāya citrasenaḥ pratāpavān
a paśyemān arinirdārān saṃsaktān iva gacchataḥ
c citrarūpam idaṃ jiṣṇor divyam astram udīryataḥ
a nedaṃ manuṣyāḥ śraddadhyur na hīdaṃ teṣu vidyate
c paurāṇānāṃ mahāstrāṇāṃ vicitro 'yaṃ samāgamaḥ
d ādadānasya hi śarān saṃdhāya ca vimuñcataḥ
d vikarṣataś ca gāṇḍīvaṃ nāntaraṃ samadṛśyata
a madhyaṃdinagataṃ sūryaṃ pratapantam ivāmbare
c na śaknuvanti sainyāni pāṇḍavaṃ prativīkṣitum
d tathaiva bhīṣmaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ draṣṭuṃ notsahate janaḥ
a ubhau viśrutakarmāṇāv ubhau yuddhaviśāradau
c ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇāv ubhau yudhi durāsadau
a ity ukto devarājas tu pārthabhīṣmasamāgamam
c pūjayām āsa divyena puṣpavarṣeṇa bhārata
d aśvatthāmā
d aśvatthāmā tato 'bhyetya drutaṃ karṇam abhāṣata
d aham eko haniṣyāmi sametān sarvapāṇḍavān
d iti karṇa samakṣaṃ naḥ sabhāmadhye tvayoditam
d na tu tat kṛtam ekasmād bhīto dhāvasi sūtaja
d vaicitravīryajāḥ sarve tvām āśritya pṛthāsutān
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d jetum icchanti saṃgrāme bhavān yudhyasva phalgunam
d aśvatthāmoditaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā duryodhanas tadā
d pratyuvāca ruṣā drauṇiṃ karṇapriyacikīrṣayā
d mā mānabhaṅgaṃ viprendra kuru viśrutakarmaṇaḥ
d mānabhaṅgena rājñāṃ tu balahānir bhaviṣyati
d śūrā vadanti saṃgrāme vācā karmāṇi kurvate
d parākramanti saṃgrāme svasvavīryānusārataḥ
d tasmāt taṃ nārhasi bhavān garhituṃ śūrasaṃmatam
d rājñaivam uktaḥ sa drauṇir gataroṣo 'bhavat tadā
a tato bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo vāme pārśve samarpayat
c asyataḥ pratisaṃdhāya vivṛtaṃ savyasācinaḥ
a tataḥ prahasya bībhatsuḥ pṛthudhāreṇa kārmukam
c nyakṛntad gārdhrapatreṇa bhīṣmasyāmitatejasaḥ
a athainaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
c yatamānaṃ parākrāntaṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a sa pīḍito mahābāhur gṛhītvā rathakūbaram
c gāṅgeyo yudhi durdharṣas tasthau dīrgham ivāturaḥ
d tataḥ pārtho 'gnisaṃkāśaṃ jvalamānam ivoragam
d nicakhāna lalāṭāgre bhīṣmasya śaram uttamam
d vyāmuhyata tadā bhīṣmas tasthau dīrgham ivāntaram
d dīrghasvareṇa covāca bībhatsuḥ kauravān prati
d vṛddhāryasya prapaśyantu sutārthe śṛṅgam adbhutam
d mānaṃ yathā jñānino 'sya cāpatyaṃ pratiyudhyataḥ
d pārtho 'pi kṣātradharmajño visaṃjñaḥ prāharat tataḥ
a taṃ visaṃjñam apovāha saṃyantā rathavājinām
c upadeśam anusmṛtya rakṣamāṇo mahāratham
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d gās tā vijitya saṃgrāme kurūṇāṃ miṣatāṃ vane
d tato yoddhumanāḥ pārthaḥ prāyāt pañca rathān prati
d ādadānaś ca nārācān vyāmṛśann iṣudhī api
d aśvatthāmā
d saṃspṛśānaś ca gāṇḍīvaṃ bhūyaḥ karṇaṃ samabhyayāt
d karṇa yat tat sabhāmadhye bahv abaddhaṃ prabhāṣase
d na me yudhi samo 'stīti tad idaṃ pratyupasthitam
d eṣo 'ntaka iva kruddhaḥ sarvabhūtāvamardanaḥ
d karṇaḥ
d adūrāt pratyupasthāya jṛmbhate kesarī yathā
d nāhaṃ bibhemi bībhatsoḥ kṛṣṇād vā devakīsutāt
d pāṇḍavebhyo 'pi sarvebhyaḥ kṣatradharmam anuvrataḥ
d sattvādhikānāṃ puṃsāṃ tu dhanurvedopajīvinām
d darśanāj jāyate darpaḥ svaraś ca na viṣīdati
d paśyatv ācāryaputro mām arjunena raṇe saha
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yudhyamānaṃ susaṃyattaṃ daivaṃ tu duratikramam
d taṃ samantād rathāḥ pañca parivārya dhanaṃjayam
d ta iṣūn samyag asyanto mumukṣanto 'pi jīvitam
d te lābham iva manvānāḥ kṣipram ārchan dhanaṃjayam
d śaraughān samyag asyanto jīmūtā iva vārṣikāḥ
d bahubhir vividhair bāṇair niśitair lomavāpibhiḥ
d ādravan pratyavasthāya pratyavidhyan dhanaṃjayam
d tataḥ prahasya bībhatsuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d divyam astraṃ vikurvāṇaḥ pratyayād rathasattamān
d yathā raśmibhir ādityaḥ pracchādayati medinīm
d evaṃ gāṇḍīvanirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ prācchādayad diśaḥ
d na rathānāṃ na nāgānāṃ na dhvajānāṃ na vājinām
d aviddhaṃ niśitair bāṇair āsīd dvyaṅgulam antaram
d sarve śāntiparā yodhāḥ svacittaṃ nābhijajñire
d hastino 'śvāś ca vitrastā vyavalīyanta sarvaśaḥ
d yathā nalavanaṃ nāgaḥ prabhinnaḥ ṣāṣṭihāyanaḥ
d evaṃ sarvān apāmṛdnād arjunaḥ śastratejasā
d gāṇḍīvasya tu ghoṣeṇa pṛthivī samakampata
d manāṃsi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām abhyakṛntad dhanaṃjayaḥ
d tato vigāhya sainyānāṃ madhyaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
d sārathiṃ samare śūram abhyabhāṣata vīryavān
d saṃniyamya hayān etān mandaṃ vāhaya sārathe
d ācāryaputraṃ samare yodhayiṣye 'parājitam
d purā hy eṣa mayā muktaḥ sa me bhavati pṛṣṭhataḥ
d evam ukto 'rjunenājāv aśvatthāmarathaṃ prati
d karṇaḥ
d virāṭaputro javanān bhṛśam aśvān acodayat
d eṣopayāti bībhatsur vyathito gāḍhavedanaḥ
d taṃ tu tatraiva yāsyāmi nāyaṃ mucyeta jīvitāt
d droṇaḥ
d naiṣo bhayena niryāto mahātmā pākaśāsaniḥ
d evaṃ bhītā nivartante na punar gāḍhavedanāḥ
d yady enam abhisaṃrabdhaṃ punar evābhiyāsyasi
d bahūny astrāṇi jānīte na punar mokṣyate bhavān
d diṣṭyā duryodhano mukto diṣṭyā gāvaḥ palāyitāḥ
d muktamuṣṭiṣu saṃgrāme kiṃ raṇena kariṣyasi
d krośamātram atikramya balam anvānayāmahe
d anvāgatabalāḥ pārthaṃ punar evābhiyāsyatha
d parākrame ca śaurye ca vīrye sattve mahāraṇe
d śastrāstreṣu ca sarveṣu lāghave dūrapātane
d yasya nāsti samo loke pitṛdattavaraś ca yaḥ
d jitaśramo jitārātir nistandriḥ khedavarjitaḥ
d yaḥ svecchāmaraṇo jātaḥ pitṛśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
d duryodhanahitārthāya yuddhvā pārthena saṃgare
d pṛthāsutahitārthāya parājita ivābhavat
d arjunaḥ
d dakṣiṇām eva tu diśaṃ hayān uttara vāhaya
d purā sārthībhavaty eṣām ayaṃ śabdo 'tra tiṣṭhatām
d aśvatthāmnaḥ pratirathaṃ prācīm udyāhi sārathe
d acirād draṣṭum icchāmi guruputraṃ yaśasvinam
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d mohayitvā tu tān sarvān dhanurghoṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ
d prasavyaṃ caivam āvṛtya krośārdhaṃ prādravat tataḥ
d yathā susaṃskṛto bāṇaḥ suparṇaś cāpi śīghragaḥ
d tathā pārtharathaḥ śīghram ākāśe paryavartata
d muhūrtoparate śabde pratiyāte dhanaṃjaye
d hastyaśvarathapādātaṃ puraskṛtya mahārathāḥ
d droṇabhīṣmamukhāḥ sarve sainyānāṃ jaghane yayuḥ
d sainikāḥ
d yattāḥ pārtham apaśyantaḥ sahitāḥ śaravikṣatāḥ
d diṣṭyā duryodhano muktaḥ sainyaṃ bhūyiṣṭham āgatam
d krośamātram atikramya balam anvānayāmahe
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d yāma yatra vanaṃ gulmaṃ nadīm anvaśmakāṃ prati
d atha duryodhano dṛṣṭvā bhagnaṃ svabalam āhave
d amṛṣyamāṇaḥ kopena parimārgan dhanaṃjayam
d nyavartata kuruśreṣṭhaḥ svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
d vāryamāṇo durādharṣair bhīṣmadroṇakṛpair bhṛśam
d tato 'rjunaś citram udāravegaṃ
d samīkṣya gāṇḍīvam uvāca vākyam
d idaṃ tv idānīm anayaṃ kurūṇāṃ
d śivaṃ dhanuḥ śatrunibarhaṇaṃ ca
d atyāśugaṃ vegavad āśukartṛ
d avāraṇīyaṃ mahate raṇāya
d pradāraṇaṃ śatruvarūthinīnām
d anīkabhit saṃyati vajrakalpam
d prayāhi yatraiṣa suyodhano hi
d taṃ pātayiṣyāmi śaraiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ
d ācāryaputraṃ ca pitāmahaṃ ca
d suyodhanaṃ sūtasutaṃ ca saṃkhye
d droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva nivārya yuddhe
d śiro hariṣyāmi suyodhanasya
d tam uttaraś citram udāravegaṃ
d dhanuś ca dṛṣṭvā niśitāñ śarāṃś ca
d bhīto 'bravīd arjunam ājimadhye
d nāhaṃ tavāśvān viṣahe niyantum
d tam abravīn mātsyasutaṃ prahasya
d gāṇḍīvadhanvā dviṣatāṃ nihantā
d mayā sahāyena kuto 'sti te bhayaṃ
d praihy uttarāśvān upamantrayasva
d āśvāsitas tena dhanaṃjayena
d vairāṭir aśvān pratutoda śīghram
d viṣphārayaṃs tad dhanur ugravegaṃ
d yuyutsamānaḥ punar eva jiṣṇuḥ
d gāṇḍīvaśabdena tu tatra yodhā
d bhūmau nipetur bahavo 'tivelam
d śaṅkhasya śabdena tu vānarasya
d arjunaḥ
d śabdena te yodhavarāḥ samantāt
d eṣo 'timānī dhṛtarāṣṭrasūnuḥ
d senāmukhe sarvasamṛddhatejāḥ
d parājayaṃ nityam amṛṣyamāṇo
d nivartate yuddhamanāḥ purastāt
d tam eva yāhi prasamīkṣya yattaḥ
d suyodhanaṃ tatra sahānujaṃ ca
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tam āpatantaṃ prasamīkṣya sarve
d kurupravīrāḥ sahasābhyagacchan
d prahasya vīraḥ sa tu tān atītya
d duryodhane dvau nicakhāna bāṇau
d tenārdito nāga iva prabhinnaḥ
d pārthena viddho dhṛtarāṣṭrasūnuḥ
d yuyutsamāno 'tirathena saṃkhye
d svayaṃ nigṛhyārjunam āsasāda
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a bhīṣme tu saṃgrāmaśiro vihāya
palāyamāne dhṛtarāṣṭraputraḥ
c ucchritya ketuṃ vinadan mahātmā
svayaṃ vigṛhyārjunam āsasāda
a sa bhīmadhanvānam udagravīryaṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ śatrugaṇe carantam
c ākarṇapūrṇāyatacoditena
bhallena vivyādha lalāṭamadhye
a sa tena bāṇena samarpitena
jāmbūnadābhena susaṃśitena
c rarāja rājan mahanīyakarmā
yathaikaparvā ruciraikaśṛṅgaḥ
a athāsya bāṇena vidāritasya
prādurbabhūvāsṛg ajasram uṣṇam
c sā tasya jāmbūnadapuṣpacitrā
māleva citrābhivirājate sma
a sa tena bāṇābhihatas tarasvī
duryodhanenoddhatamanyuvegaḥ
c śarān upādāya viṣāgnikalpān
vivyādha rājānam adīnasattvaḥ
a duryodhanaś cāpi tam ugratejāḥ
pārthaś ca duryodhanam ekavīraḥ
c anyonyam ājau puruṣapravīrau
samaṃ samājaghnatur ājamīḍhau
a tataḥ prabhinnena mahāgajena
mahīdharābhena punar vikarṇaḥ
c rathaiś caturbhir gajapādarakṣaiḥ
kuntīsutaṃ jiṣṇum athābhyadhāvat
a tam āpatantaṃ tvaritaṃ gajendraṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ kumbhavibhāgamadhye
c ākarṇapūrṇena dṛḍhāyasena
bāṇena vivyādha mahājavena
a pārthena sṛṣṭaḥ sa tu gārdhrapatra
ā puṅkhadeśāt praviveśa nāgam
c vidārya śailapravaraprakāśaṃ
yathāśaniḥ parvatam indrasṛṣṭaḥ
a śaraprataptaḥ sa tu nāgarājaḥ
pravepitāṅgo vyathitāntarātmā
c saṃsīdamāno nipapāta mahyāṃ
vajrāhataṃ śṛṅgam ivācalasya
a nipātite dantivare pṛthivyāṃ
trāsād vikarṇaḥ sahasāvatīrya
c tūrṇaṃ padāny aṣṭaśatāni gatvā
viviṃśateḥ syandanam āruroha
a nihatya nāgaṃ tu śareṇa tena
vajropamenādrivarāmbudābham
c tathāvidhenaiva śareṇa pārtho
duryodhanaṃ vakṣasi nirbibheda
a tato gaje rājani caiva bhinne
bhagne vikarṇe ca sapādarakṣe
c gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhaiḥ praṇunnās
te yodhamukhyāḥ sahasāpajagmuḥ
a dṛṣṭvaiva bāṇena hataṃ tu nāgaṃ
yodhāṃś ca sarvān dravato niśamya
c rathaṃ samāvṛtya kurupravīro
raṇāt pradudrāva yato na pārthaḥ
a taṃ bhīmarūpaṃ tvaritaṃ dravantaṃ
duryodhanaṃ śatrusaho niṣaṅgī
c prākṣveḍayad yoddhumanāḥ kirīṭī
bāṇena viddhaṃ rudhiraṃ vamantam
d tasmin maheṣvāsavare 'tividdhe
d dhanaṃjayenāpratimena yuddhe
d sarvāṇi sainyāni bhayārditāni
d trāsaṃ yayuḥ pārtham udīkṣya tāni
d tatas tu te śāntiparāś ca sarve
d dṛṣṭvārjunaṃ nāgam iva prabhinnam
d uccair nadantaṃ balavantam ājau
d madhye sthitaṃ siṃham ivarṣabhāṇām
d gāṇḍīvaśabdena tu pāṇḍavasya
d yodhā nipetuḥ sahasā rathebhyaḥ
d bhayārditāḥ pārthaśarābhitaptāḥ
d siṃhābhipannā iva vāraṇendrāḥ
d saṃraktanetraḥ punar indrakarmā
d vaikartanaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
d vidrāvya teṣāṃ dravatāṃ samīkṣya
d duḥśāsanaṃ caikarathena pārthaḥ
d karṇo 'bravīt pārthaśarābhitapto
d duryodhanaṃ duṣprasahaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā
d dṛṣṭo 'rjuno 'yaṃ pratiyāma śīghraṃ
d śreyo vidhāsyāma ito gatena
d manye tvayā tāta kṛtaṃ ca kāryaṃ
d yad arjuno 'smābhir ihādya dṛṣṭaḥ
d bhūyo vanaṃ gacchatu savyasācī
d paśyāmi pūrṇaṃ samayaṃ na teṣām
d śarārditās te yudhi pāṇḍavena
d prasasrur anyonyam athāhvayantaḥ
d karṇo 'bravīd āpataty eṣa jiṣṇur
d duryodhanaṃ saṃparivārya yāmaḥ
d sarvāstravid vāraṇayūthapābhaḥ
d kāle prahartā yudhi śātravāṇām
d ayaṃ ca pārthaḥ punarāgato no
d mūlaṃ ca rakṣyaṃ bharatarṣabhāṇām
d samīkṣya pārthaṃ tarasāpatantaṃ
d duryodhanaḥ kālam ivāttaśastram
d bhayārtarūpaḥ śaraṇaṃ prapede
d droṇaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca kṛpaṃ ca bhīṣmam
d taṃ bhītarūpaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajantaṃ
d duryodhanaṃ śatrusaho niṣaṅgī
d ity abravīt prītamanāḥ kirīṭī
d bāṇena viddhaṃ rudhiraṃ vamantam
 arjuna uvāca
a vihāya kīrtiṃ vipulaṃ yaśaś ca
yuddhāt parāvṛtya palāyase kim
c na te 'dya tūryāṇi samāhatāni
yathāvad udyānti gatasya yuddhe
d na bhokṣyase so 'dya mahīṃ samagrāṃ
d yānāni vastrāṇy atha bhojanāni
d kalyāṇagandhīni ca candanāni
d yuddhāt parājitya tu bhokṣyase kim
d suvarṇamālyāni ca kuṇḍalāni
d hārāṃś ca vaiḍūryakṛtopadhānān
d cyutasya yuddhān na tu śaṅkhaśabdās
d tathā bhaviṣyanti tavādya pāpa
d na bhogahetor varacandanaṃ ca
d striyaś ca mukhyā madhurapralāpāḥ
d yuddhāt prayātasya narendrasūnoḥ
d pare ca loke phalatā na ceha
a yudhiṣṭhirasyāsmi nideśakārī
pārthas tṛtīyo yudhi ca sthiro 'smi
c tadartham āvṛtya mukhaṃ prayaccha
narendravṛttaṃ smara dhārtarāṣṭra
a moghaṃ tavedaṃ bhuvi nāmadheyaṃ
duryodhanetīha kṛtaṃ purastāt
b duryodhanas tvaṃ prathito 'si nāmnā
b suyodhanas tvaṃ nikṛtipradhānaḥ
c na hīha duryodhanatā tavāsti
palāyamānasya raṇaṃ vihāya
a na te purastād atha pṛṣṭhato vā
paśyāmi duryodhana rakṣitāram
c paraihi yuddhena kurupravīra
prāṇān priyān pāṇḍavato 'dya rakṣa
d bhītaṃ vivastraṃ virathaṃ yato 'haṃ
d visaṃjñam ājau vikalaṃ vivastram
d vimuktakeśaṃ ca palāyamānaṃ
d prāptaṃ tavāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vadantam
d tavāsmi ceti pralapantam evaṃ
d rakṣeti māṃ vādinam eva vādīn
d parāṅmukhān nāham aho nihanmi
d yatas tato jīva suyodhana tvam
d vacāṃsi cet tvaṃ smarasi svakīyāny
d uktāny aho dyūtajaye sabhāyām
d ūruṃ svakaṃ darśayatā samakṣam
d asmān samākṣipya jagāda kṛṣṇām
d mṛtā yathaite kila pāṇḍuputrā
d vyāghrā yathā carmamayāś ca sarpāḥ
d prabhagnadaṃṣṭrāś ca sakūrcaṣaṇḍhās
d tilā yathāraṇyabhavās tathaite
d jano yathā kākayavāñ jagāda
d pāṇḍūṃs tathā nāmadharāṃs tu viddhi
d samāviśas tv aṅkam imaṃ mameti
d rājyasya me 'laṃkaraṇaṃ bhava tvam
d droṇasya bhīṣmasya kṛpasya caiva
d yac chṛṇvatas tvaṃ bahudhālapad bhoḥ
d tad ehi bho na tv akajasva sainyaiḥ
d sahāpi mām ekarathaṃ rathaiḥ svaiḥ
d sarvaiḥ svayodhair bahubhiḥ samaṃ tvaṃ
d yudhyasva mām ekam apīha vīram
d jīvan vimokṣe na palāyamāno
d manda svayuktaṃ smara tatsabhāyām
d parīpsa yuddhena kurūn samakṣaṃ
d prāṇān mayā bāhubalābhisṛṣṭān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a āhūyamānas tu sa tena saṃkhye
mahāmanā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraḥ
c nivartitas tasya girāṅkuśena
gajo yathā matta ivāṅkuśena
a so 'mṛṣyamāṇo vacasābhimṛṣṭo
mahārathenātirathas tarasvī
b tato duryodhanaḥ kruddho vikṣipan dhanur uttamam
b duryodhanaḥ
b dhṛtiṃ kṛtvā suvipulāṃ pratyuvāca dhanaṃjayam
b nāham indrād api kruddhād bibhemi bharatarṣabha
b bhuktvā suvipulaṃ rājyaṃ vittāni ca sukhāni ca
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b kimarthaṃ yuddhasamaye palāyiṣye narottama
b evam uktvā mahārājaḥ pratyayudhyata phalgunam
b saṃnipatya tu śīghrāśvas totrārdita iva dvipaḥ
b ākrāntabhogas tejasvī dhanur vakra ivoragaḥ
b rathaṃ rathena saṃgamya yodhayām āsa pāṇḍavam
c paryāvavartātha rathena vīro
bhogī yathā pādatalābhimṛṣṭaḥ
a taṃ prekṣya karṇaḥ parivartamānaṃ
nivartya saṃstabhya ca viddhagātraḥ
c duryodhanaṃ dakṣiṇato 'bhyagacchat
pārthaṃ nṛvīro yudhi hemamālī
a bhīṣmas tataḥ śāṃtanavo nivṛtya
hiraṇyakakṣyāṃs tvarayaṃs turaṃgān
c duryodhanaṃ paścimato 'bhyarakṣat
pārthān mahābāhur adhijyadhanvā
a droṇaḥ kṛpaś caiva viviṃśatiś ca
duḥśāsanaś caiva nivṛtya śīghram
c sarve purastād vitateṣucāpā
duryodhanārthaṃ tvaritābhyupeyuḥ
a sa tāny anīkāni nivartamānāny
ālokya pūrṇaughanibhāni pārthaḥ
c haṃso yathā megham ivāpatantaṃ
dhanaṃjayaḥ pratyapatat tarasvī
a te sarvataḥ saṃparivārya pārtham
astrāṇi divyāni samādadānāḥ
c vavarṣur abhyetya śaraiḥ samantān
meghā yathā bhūdharam ambuvegaiḥ
a tato 'stram astreṇa nivārya teṣāṃ
gāṇḍīvadhanvā kurupuṃgavānām
c saṃmohanaṃ śatrusaho 'nyad astraṃ
prāduścakāraindrir apāraṇīyam
a tato diśaś cānudiśo vivṛtya
śaraiḥ sudhārair niśitaiḥ supuṅkhaiḥ
c gāṇḍīvaghoṣeṇa manāṃsi teṣāṃ
mahābalaḥ pravyathayāṃ cakāra
a tataḥ punar bhīmaravaṃ pragṛhya
dorbhyāṃ mahāśaṅkham udāraghoṣam
c vyanādayat sa pradiśo diśaḥ khaṃ
bhuvaṃ ca pārtho dviṣatāṃ nihantā
a te śaṅkhanādena kurupravīrāḥ
saṃmohitāḥ pārthasamīritena
c utsṛjya cāpāni durāsadāni
sarve tadā śāntiparā babhūvuḥ
a tathā visaṃjñeṣu pareṣu pārthaḥ
smṛtvā tu vākyāni tathottarāyāḥ
c niryāhi madhyād iti matsyaputram
uvāca yāvat kuravo visaṃjñāḥ
a ācārya śāradvatayoḥ suśukle
karṇasya pītaṃ ruciraṃ ca vastram
c drauṇeś ca rājñaś ca tathaiva nīle
vastre samādatsva narapravīra
a bhīṣmasya saṃjñāṃ tu tathaiva manye
jānāti me 'strapratighātam eṣaḥ
c etasya vāhān kuru savyatas tvam
evaṃ hi yātavyam amūḍhasaṃjñaiḥ
a raśmīn samutsṛjya tato mahātmā
rathād avaplutya virāṭaputraḥ
b nānāvidhāny adbhutavarṇakāni
b mahānti cīnāṃśudukūlakāni
b paṭṭāṃśukāni vividhāni manojñakāni
b hārāṃś ca rājñāṃ maṇibhūṣaṇāni
b suvarṇaniṣkābharaṇāni māriṣa
b māṇikyabāhvaṅgadakaṅkaṇāni
b anyāni rājñāṃ maṇibhūṣaṇāni
c vastrāṇy upādāya mahārathānāṃ
tūrṇaṃ punaḥ svaṃ ratham āruroha
d rājñaś ca sarvān mṛtasaṃnikāśān
d saṃmohanāstreṇa visaṃjñakalpān
d nāsāgravinyastakarāṅgulīkaḥ
d pārtho jahāsa smayamānacetāḥ
d tato 'rjuno svāpanam astram ugraṃ
d kodaṇḍam āropya kurūn pratīha
d bhīṣmaṃ guruṃ putrayutaṃ kṛpaṃ ca
d muktvā mumocānyaśirasy amarṣī
d śirāṃsi teṣām atha tat prapadya
d prasvāpanāstraṃ kurupuṃgavānām
d ekaikaśaḥ kūrcaśiro 'rdham ardhaṃ
d pṛthak pṛthag vā lunad anyam anyam
d bhāgaṃ śiraḥ kūrcabhavaṃ vimuṇḍya
d pratyāyayau pārthakaraṃ tad astram
d tataḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ puruṣapravīro
d gurūn namaskṛtya jagāda coccaiḥ
d prayāntu bho 'ntaḥpuram āśu vīrāḥ
d svaṃ svaṃ priyāṇāṃ pratidarśayantu
d prāṇān upādāya mayādya muktā
d mokṣyāmi roṣaṃ punar apy aho svam
a tato 'nvaśāsac caturaḥ sadaśvān
putro virāṭasya hiraṇyakakṣyān
c te tad vyatīyur dhvajinām anīkaṃ
śvetā vahanto 'rjunam ājimadhyāt
a tathā tu yāntaṃ puruṣapravīraṃ
bhīṣmaḥ śarair abhyahanat tarasvī
c sa cāpi bhīṣmasya hayān nihatya
vivyādha pārśve daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ
a tato 'rjuno bhīṣmam apāsya yuddhe
viddhvāsya yantāram ariṣṭadhanvā
c tasthau vimukto rathavṛndamadhyād
rāhuṃ vidāryeva sahasraraśmiḥ
a labdhvā tu saṃjñāṃ ca kurupravīraḥ
pārthaṃ samīkṣyātha mahendrakalpam
c raṇād vimuktaṃ sthitam ekam ājau
sa dhārtarāṣṭras tvarito babhāṣe
c sarvāñ jitān muṇḍitaśīrṣakūrcān
c pṛthakpṛthagbhāgavirūparaudrān
a ayaṃ kathaṃ svid bhavatāṃ vimuktas
taṃ vai prabadhnīta yathā na mucyet
c tam abravīc chāṃtanavaḥ prahasya
kva te gatā buddhir abhūt kva vīryam
a śāntiṃ parāśvasya yathā sthito 'bhūr
utsṛjya bāṇāṃś ca dhanuś ca citram
c na tv eva bībhatsur alaṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ
kartuṃ na pāpe 'sya mano niviṣṭam
a trailokyahetor na jahet svadharmaṃ
tasmān na sarve nihatā raṇe 'smin
b adyāpi caitanyam aho tavātra
b nāsty eva rājan gatacīrakasya
b saṃbhālayātmānam amitrasāha
b kva te gataṃ cīram adīnasattva
b yodhāṃś ca sarvān abhivīkṣya nagnāṃs
b tasmān na vācyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraputra
c kṣipraṃ kurūn yāhi kurupravīra
vijitya gāś ca pratiyātu pārthaḥ
d yuṣmān sametān kupito na hanyāt
d tasmāt puraṃ ja
yāma sa no 'stu lābhaḥ
d mā te svako 'rtho nipateta mohāt
d tat saṃvidhātavyam ariṣṭadhanvan
d saṃmohanāstrapratimohitāḥ stha
d yūyaṃ na jānīta dhanāpahāram
d paśyātmavastrābharaṇāni rājan
d virāṭaputreṇa samāhṛtāni
d nṛpeṣu sarveṣu ca mohiteṣu
d hantuṃ yad icchet sa haniṣyatīti
d tadā tu dharmātmatayā nṛvīro
d na cāhanad vo balabhit tanūjaḥ
d bhāgyena yuṣmān avadhīn na pārthaḥ
d saṃdhiṃ kurūṇām anumanyamānaḥ
d tad yāta yūyaṃ saha sainikaiś ca
d hatāvaśiṣṭair gajasāhvayaṃ puram
a duryodhanas tasya tu tan niśamya
pitāmahasyātmahitaṃ vaco 'tha
b nītāni vastrāṇi ca phālgunena
b samīkṣya rājā hṛdi lajjitaś ca
c atītakāmo yudhi so 'tyamarṣī
rājā viniḥśvasya babhūva tūṣṇīm
a tad bhīṣmavākyaṃ hitam īkṣya sarve
dhanaṃjayāgniṃ ca vivardhamānam
c nivartanāyaiva mano nidadhyur
duryodhanaṃ te parirakṣamāṇāḥ
a tān prasthitān prītamanāḥ sa pārtho
dhanaṃjayaḥ prekṣya kurupravīrān
c ābhāṣamāṇo 'nuyayau muhūrtaṃ
saṃpūjayaṃs tatra gurūn mahātmā
c teṣām anīkāni nirīkṣya pārtho
c viśīrṇatūryadhvajakārmukāni
c gāṇḍīvadhanvā pravaraḥ kurūṇāṃ
c śaṅkhaṃ pradadhmau balavān balena
c te śaṅkhaśabdaṃ tumulaṃ niśamya
c dhvajasya śrutvā nadato 'ntarikṣe
c gāṇḍīvaśabdena muhur muhus te
c bhītā yayuḥ sarvadhanaṃ vihāya
c tān arjuno dūrataraṃ vibhajya
c dhanaṃ ca sarvaṃ nikhilaṃ nivartya
c āpṛcchya tān dūrataraṃ prayātvā
d gurūṃś ca sarvān abhivādya bāṇair
d nyavartatodagramanāḥ śanaiḥ saḥ
a pitāmahaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ sa vṛddhaṃ
droṇaṃ guruṃ ca pratipūjya mūrdhnā
c drauṇiṃ kṛpaṃ caiva gurūṃś ca sarvāñ
śarair vicitrair abhivādya caiva
a duryodhanasyottamaratnacitraṃ
ciccheda pārtho mukuṭaṃ śareṇa
b tan nāma viśrāvya tato nivṛttaḥ
b dhanaṃjayaṃ siṃham ivāttavaktraṃ
b gā vai vijityābhimukhaṃ prayāntam
b udīkṣituṃ pārthivās te na śekur
b yathaiva madhyāhnagataṃ tu sūryam
b ratnāni vāsāṃsi ca tāni gṛhya
b raṇotkaṭo nāga iva prabhinnaḥ
b jitvā ca vairāṭim uvāca pārthaḥ
b prahṛṣṭarūpo rathināṃ variṣṭhaḥ
c āmantrya vīrāṃś ca tathaiva mānyān
gāṇḍīvaghoṣeṇa vinādya lokān
a sa devadattaṃ sahasā vinādya
vidārya vīro dviṣatāṃ manāṃsi
c dhvajena sarvān abhibhūya śatrūn
sa hemajālena virājamānaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā prayātāṃs tu kurūn kirīṭī
hṛṣṭo 'bravīt tatra sa matsyaputram
c āvartayāśvān paśavo jitās te
yātāḥ pare yāhi puraṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ
d devās tu dṛṣṭvā mahad adbhutaṃ tad
d yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ saha phālgunena
d jagmur yathāsvaṃ bhavanaṃ pratītāḥ
d pārthasya karmāṇi vicintayantaḥ
d sa hemamālena virājamāno
d rathena vīro rudhirokṣitena
d uddhuṣyatāṃ te vijayo 'dya śīghraṃ
d gātraṃ tu te sevatu mālyagandhān
d mātā tu te nandatu bāndhavāś ca
d tvām adya dṛṣṭvaivam udīrṇaharṣam
d devāś ca gandharvagaṇāś ca pārthaṃ
d rājarṣayaś cāpi mudaṃ pratītāḥ
d saṃpūjayanto javam eva sarve
d yayuḥ puraskṛtya tadā mahendram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 tato hṛṣṭamanāḥ pārtham uttaraḥ pratyabhāṣata
 kurūn parājitān dṛṣṭvā bhrājamānaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
 diṣṭyā jayasi durdharṣa mahābāho dhanaṃjaya
 prādurbhāvaṃ jayaṃ caiva dṛṣṭvā prīto 'smi pāṇḍava
 niśamya vacanaṃ tasya uttarasya mahātmanaḥ
 arjunaḥ paravīraghnaḥ pratyuvācottaraṃ tadā
 diṣṭyā tvam akṣatas tāta diṣṭyā gāvas tavānagha
 pratyāgatā yathānyāyaṃ śatravaś ca jitā raṇe
 āvartaya rathaṃ śīghraṃ sadaśvān saṃpraṇodaya
 apavartaya gāḥ sarvā yāhi caiva śamīṃ prati
a tato vijitya saṃgrāme kurūn govṛṣabhekṣaṇaḥ
c samānayām āsa tadā virāṭasya dhanaṃ mahat
a gateṣu ca prabhagneṣu dhārtarāṣṭreṣu sarvaśaḥ
c vanān niṣkramya gahanād bahavaḥ kurusainikāḥ
a bhayāt saṃtrastamanasaḥ samājagmus tatas tataḥ
c muktakeśā vyadṛśyanta sthitāḥ prāñjalayas tadā
a kṣutpipāsāpariśrāntā videśasthā vicetasaḥ
c ūcuḥ praṇamya saṃbhrāntāḥ pārtha kiṃ karavāma te
d prāṇān antarmanoyātān prayāciṣyāmahe vayam
d arjunaḥ
d vayaṃ cārjuna te dāsā hy anurakṣyā hy anāthakāḥ
d anāthān duḥkhitān dīnān kṛśān vṛddhān parājitān
d nyastaśastrān nirāśāṃś ca nāhaṃ hanmi kṛtāñjalīn
d bhavanto yāntu visrabdhā nirbhayā amṛtās tathā
d mama pādarajorakṣyā jīvantu suciraṃ bhuvi
 arjuna uvāca
a svasti vrajata bhadraṃ vo na bhetavyaṃ kathaṃ cana
c nāham ārtāñ jighāṃsāmi bhṛśam āśvāsayāmi vaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tām abhayāṃ vācaṃ śrutvā yodhāḥ samāgatāḥ
c āyuḥkīrtiyaśodābhis tam āśirbhir anandayan
d sa karma kṛtvā paramāryakarmā
d nihatya śatrūn dviṣatāṃ nihantā
d prayātāḥ sarvatas tatra namaskṛtya dhanaṃjayam
d tato 'rjunaṃ nāgam iva prabhinnam
d utsṛjya śatrūn vinivartamānam
d virāṭarāṣṭrābhimukhaṃ prayāntaṃ
d nāśaknuvaṃs taṃ kuravo 'bhiyātum
d tataḥ sa taṃ megham ivāpatantaṃ
d vidrāvya pārthaḥ kurumeghasainyam
d taṃ matsyaputraṃ dviṣatāṃ nihantā
d vaco 'bravīt saṃparigṛhya bhūyaḥ
d pituḥ sakāśe tava tāta sarve
d vasanti pārthā viditaṃ tavaiva
d tān mā praśaṃser nagaraṃ praviśya
d bhītaḥ praṇaśyeta sa matsyarājaḥ
d mayā jitā sā dhvajinī kurūṇāṃ
d mayā ca gāvo vijitā dviṣadbhyaḥ
d evaṃ tu kāmaṃ nagaraṃ praviśya
d uttara uvāca
d tvam ātmanā karma kṛtaṃ bravīhi
d yat te kṛtaṃ karma na pāraṇīyaṃ
d tat karma kartuṃ mama nāsti śaktiḥ
d na tvāṃ pravakṣyāmi pituḥ sakāśe
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d yāvan na māṃ vakṣyasi savyasācin
d sa śatrusenām avajitya jiṣṇur
d ācchidya sarvaṃ ca dhanaṃ kurubhyaḥ
d śmaśānam āgamya punaḥ śamīṃ tām
d abhyetya tasthau śaravikṣatāṅgaḥ
d tataḥ sa vahnipratimo mahākapiḥ
d sahaiva bhūtair divam utpapāta
d tathaiva māyā vihitā babhūva
d dhvajaṃ ca siṃhaṃ yuyuje rathe punaḥ
d nidhāya tac cāyudham ājivardhanaṃ
d kurūttamānām iṣudhīr dhvajāṃs tathā
d prāyāt sa matsyo nagaraṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ
d kirīṭinā sārathinā mahātmā
d pārthaś ca kṛtvā param āryakarma
d nihatya śatrūn dviṣatāṃ nihantā
d vidhāya veṇīṃ ca tathaiva bhūyo
d jagrāha raśmīn punar uttarasya
d viveśa hṛṣṭo nagaraṃ mahātmā
d bṛhannalārūpam upetya sārathiḥ
a tato nivṛttāḥ kuravaḥ prabhagnā vaśam āsthitāḥ
b hastināpuram uddiśya sarve dīnā yayus tadā
c panthānam upasaṃgamya phalguno vākyam abravīt
a rājaputra pratyavekṣa samānītāni sarvaśaḥ
c gokulāni mahābāho vīra gopālakaiḥ saha
d arjunaḥ
d agre prayāntu nagaraṃ ghoṣayantu ca te jayam
a tato 'parāhṇe yāsyāmo virāṭanagaraṃ prati
c āśvāsya pāyayitvā ca pariplāvya ca vājinaḥ
a gacchantu tvaritāś caiva gopālāḥ preṣitās tvayā
c nagare priyam ākhyātuṃ ghoṣayantu ca te jayam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uttaras tvaramāṇo 'tha dūtān ājñāpayat tataḥ
c vacanād arjunasyaiva ācakṣadhvaṃ jayaṃ mama
d athottaras tvaramāṇaḥ sa dūtān
d ājñāpayad vacanāt phālgunasya
d ācakṣadhvaṃ vijayaṃ pārthivasya
d bhagnāḥ pare vijitāś cāpi gāvaḥ
d prahṛṣṭās te 'tha gopālāḥ praviśya nagaraṃ tataḥ
d ūcur jayaṃ virāṭasya diṣṭyā godhanam āhṛtam
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d ity evaṃ tau bhāratamatsyavīrau
d saṃmantrya saṃgamya tataḥ śamīṃ tām
d abhyetya bhūyo vijayena tṛptāv
d utsṛṣṭam āropayatāṃ svabhāṇḍam
d sa śatrusenām abhibhūya sarvām
d ācchidya sarvaṃ ca dhanaṃ kurubhyaḥ
d vairāṭir āyān nagaraṃ pratīto
d bṛhannalāsārathir ekavīraḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a avajitya dhanaṃ cāpi virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
c prāviśan nagaraṃ hṛṣṭaś caturbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
a jitvā trigartān saṃgrāme gāś caivādāya kevalāḥ
c aśobhata mahārājaḥ saha pārthaiḥ śriyā vṛtaḥ
a tam āsanagataṃ vīraṃ suhṛdāṃ prītivardhanam
b upāsāṃ cakrire sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha sainikaiḥ
c upatasthuḥ prakṛtayaḥ samastā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
a sabhājitaḥ sasainyas tu pratinandyātha matsyarāṭ
c visarjayām āsa tadā dvijāṃś ca prakṛtīs tathā
a tataḥ sa rājā matsyānāṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
b praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ ramyaṃ strīśatair upaśobhitam
c uttaraṃ paripapraccha kva yāta iti cābravīt
a ācakhyus tasya saṃhṛṣṭāḥ striyaḥ kanyāś ca veśmani
c antaḥpuracarāś caiva kurubhir godhanaṃ hṛtam
a vijetum abhisaṃrabdha eka evātisāhasāt
c bṛhannaḍāsahāyaś ca niryātaḥ pṛthivīṃjayaḥ
a upayātān atirathān droṇaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ kṛpam
c karṇaṃ duryodhanaṃ caiva droṇaputraṃ ca ṣaḍrathān
a rājā virāṭo 'tha bhṛśaṃ prataptaḥ
śrutvā sutaṃ hy ekarathena yātam
c bṛhannaḍāsārathim ājivardhanaṃ
provāca sarvān atha mantrimukhyān
d rājā
d gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi abhibhūya mamātmajam
d kuravaḥ kālayanti sma sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
a sarvathā kuravas te hi ye cānye vasudhādhipāḥ
c trigartān nirjitāñ śrutvā na sthāsyanti kadā cana
a tasmād gacchantu me yodhā balena mahatā vṛtāḥ
c uttarasya parīpsārthaṃ ye trigartair avikṣatāḥ
a hayāṃś ca nāgāṃś ca rathāṃś ca śīghraṃ
padātisaṃghāṃś ca tataḥ pravīrān
c prasthāpayām āsa sutasya hetor
vicitraśastrābharaṇopapannān
a evaṃ sa rājā matsyānāṃ virāṭo 'kṣauhiṇīpatiḥ
c vyādideśātha tāṃ kṣipraṃ vāhinīṃ caturaṅgiṇīm
a kumāram āśu jānīta yadi jīvati vā na vā
c yasya yantā gataḥ ṣaṇḍho manye 'haṃ na sa jīvati
d matsainyaṃ tvaritaṃ gatvā kurūn prāpya ca cottaram
d dṛṣṭvā yadi jitā gāvo vijayenābhyanandata
a tam abravīd dharmarājaḥ prahasya
virāṭam ārtaṃ kurubhiḥ prataptam
c bṛhannaḍā sārathiś cen narendra
pare na neṣyanti tavādya gās tāḥ
a sarvān mahīpān sahitān kurūṃś ca
tathaiva devāsurayakṣanāgān
c alaṃ vijetuṃ samare sutas te
svanuṣṭhitaḥ sārathinā hi tena
a athottareṇa prahitā dūtās te śīghragāminaḥ
c virāṭanagaraṃ prāpya jayam āvedayaṃs tadā
a rājñas tataḥ samācakhyau mantrī vijayam uttamam
c parājayaṃ kurūṇāṃ cāpy upāyāntaṃ tathottaram
a sarvā vinirjitā gāvaḥ kuravaś ca parājitāḥ
c uttaraḥ saha sūtena kuśalī ca paraṃtapa
 kaṅka uvāca
a diṣṭyā te nirjitā gāvaḥ kuravaś ca parājitāḥ
c diṣṭyā te jīvitaḥ putraḥ śrūyate pārthivarṣabha
a nādbhutaṃ tv eva manye 'haṃ yat te putro 'jayat kurūn
c dhruva eva jayas tasya yasya yantā bṛhannaḍā
d devendrasārathiś caiva mātaliḥ khyātavikramaḥ
d kṛṣṇasya sārathiś caiva na bṛhannalayā samau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato virāṭo nṛpatiḥ saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ
c śrutvā tu vijayaṃ tasya kumārasyāmitaujasaḥ
e ācchādayitvā dūtāṃs tān mantriṇaḥ so 'bhyacodayat
f gate tv anubale tasmin dūtavākyaṃ niśamya tu
f uttarasya jayāt prīto virāṭaḥ pratyabhāṣata
a rājamārgāḥ kriyantāṃ me patākābhir alaṃkṛtāḥ
c puṣpopahārair arcyantāṃ devatāś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
a kumārā yodhamukhyāś ca gaṇikāś ca svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi pratyudyāntu sutaṃ mama
d bhavantu te labdhajaye sute me
d paurāś ca nāryaś ca pure ca martyāḥ
d te śuklavastrāḥ prabhavantu mārge
d sugandhamālyābharaṇāś ca nāryaḥ
d bhajantu sarvā gaṇikā sutaṃ me
d nāryaś ca sarvāḥ sahasainikāś ca
d svalaṃkṛtās tāḥ subhagāś ca veśyāḥ
d putrasya panthānam anuvrajantu
a ghaṇṭāpaṇavakaḥ śīghraṃ mattam āruhya vāraṇam
c śṛṅgāṭakeṣu sarveṣu ākhyātu vijayaṃ mama
a uttarā ca kumārībhir bahvībhir abhisaṃvṛtā
c śṛṅgāraveṣābharaṇā pratyudyātu bṛhannaḍām
a śrutvā tu tad vacanaṃ pārthivasya
sarve punaḥ svastikapāṇayaś ca
c bheryaś ca tūryāṇi ca vārijāś ca
veṣaiḥ parārdhyaiḥ pramadāḥ śubhāś ca
a tathaiva sūtāḥ saha māgadhaiś ca
nandīvādyāḥ paṇavās tūryavādyāḥ
c purād virāṭasya mahābalasya
pratyudyayuḥ putram anantavīryam
d śrutvā tu vacanaṃ rājñaḥ paurāḥ svastikapāṇayaḥ
d sūtāś ca sarve saha māgadhāś ca
d hṛṣṭā virāṭasya pure janaughāḥ
d bheryaś ca tūryāṇi ca vārijāś ca
d veṣaiḥ parārdhyaiḥ pramadājanāś ca
d vandipravādaiḥ paṇavānakaiś ca
d tathaiva vādyāni ca śaṅkhaśabdāḥ
d sakāṃsyatālaṃ madhuraṃ ca gītaṃ
d ādāya nāryo nagarāt tadīyāt
d pratyudyayuḥ putram anantavīryaṃ
d te brāhmaṇāḥ śāntiparāḥ pradhānāḥ
d svādhyāyavedādhyayanakramajñāḥ
d svastikriyāgītajayapradhānāḥ
d sarve suprītamanasaḥ pratijagmur yathocitam
a prasthāpya senāṃ kanyāś ca gaṇikāś ca svalaṃkṛtāḥ
b abhyabhāṣata matsyānāṃ rājā kaṅkam amitrahā
b trigartāḥ kuravaḥ sarve saṃgrāme nirjitā mayā
b praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ hṛṣṭau dyūtaṃ devyāmahe vayam
c matsyarājo mahāprājñaḥ prahṛṣṭa idam abravīt
e akṣān āhara sairandhri kaṅka dyūtaṃ pravartatām
e   āsanaṃ copakalpaya
e ādāya vyajanaṃ tvaṃ ca pārśvato 'nantarā bhava
a taṃ tathā vādinaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavaḥ pratyabhāṣata
c na devitavyaṃ hṛṣṭena kitaveneti naḥ śrutam
a na tvām adya mudā yuktam ahaṃ devitum utsahe
c priyaṃ tu te cikīrṣāmi vartatāṃ yadi manyase
d dyūtaṃ kartuṃ na vāñchāmi narendra tava saṃsadi
 virāṭa uvāca
a striyo gāvo hiraṇyaṃ ca yac cānyad vasu kiṃ cana
a   dhānyaṃ yugyam ajāvikam
a vividhāni ca ratnāni
c na me kiṃ cit tvayā rakṣyam antareṇāpi devitum
 kaṅka uvāca
a kiṃ te dyūtena rājendra bahudoṣeṇa mānada
c devane bahavo doṣās tasmāt tat parivarjayet
a śrutas te yadi vā dṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavo vai yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c sa rājyaṃ sumahat sphītaṃ bhrātṝṃś ca tridaśopamān
c   paṇam ekam amanyata
c kṛṣṇāṃ ca bhāryāṃ dayitāṃ
c niḥsaṃśayaṃ ca kitavaḥ paścāt tapyati pāṇḍavaḥ
c vividhānāṃ ca ratnānāṃ dhanānāṃ ca parājaye
c abhakṣitavināśaś ca vākpāruṣyam anantaram
c aviśvāsyaṃ budhair nityam ekāhnā dravyanāśanam
a dyūte hāritavān sarvaṃ tasmād dyūtaṃ na rocaye
c atha vā manyase rājan dīvyāva yadi rocate
d evam ābhāṣya vākyais tu krīḍatus tau narottamau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pravartamāne dyūte tu matsyaḥ pāṇḍavam abravīt
c paśya putreṇa me yuddhe tādṛśāḥ kuravo jitāḥ
d kuravo 'tirathāḥ sarve devair api sudurjayāḥ
a tato 'bravīn matsyarājaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b kaṅkaḥ
b diṣṭyā te vijitā gāvaḥ kuravaś ca parājitāḥ
b atyadbhutam ahaṃ manye uttaraś cet kurūñ jayet
c bṛhannaḍā yasya yantā kathaṃ sa na vijeṣyati
d tato virāṭaḥ kṣubhito manyunābhipariplutaḥ
d uvāca vacanaṃ kruddhaḥ parivrājam anantaram
d tādṛśena tu yodhena maheṣvāsena dhīmatā
d kaṅkaḥ
d kuravo nirjitā yuddhe tatra kiṃ brāhmaṇādbhutam
d yantā tathāvidho yasya rathe tiṣṭhati vīryavān
d yad etad duṣkaraṃ kuryāt tatra kiṃ nādbhutaṃ bhavet
d virāṭaḥ
d pumāṃso bahavo dṛṣṭāḥ sūtāś ca balino mayā
d vikramya yantā yoddhā ca na me dṛṣṭaḥ kadā cana
d vipriyaṃ nācared rājñām ānukūlyaṃ priyaṃ vadet
d ācaran vipriyaṃ rājñāṃ na jātu sukham edhate
a ity uktaḥ kupito rājā matsyaḥ pāṇḍavam abravīt
c samaṃ putreṇa me ṣaṇḍhaṃ brahmabandho praśaṃsasi
a vācyāvācyaṃ na jānīṣe nūnaṃ mām avamanyase
c bhīṣmadroṇamukhān sarvān kasmān na sa vijeṣyati
a vayasyatvāt tu te brahmann aparādham imaṃ kṣame
c nedṛśaṃ te punar vācyaṃ yadi jīvitum icchasi
d tato 'bravīt punaḥ kaṅkaḥ prahasya kuruvardhana
d bṛhannalāyā rājendra ghuṣyatāṃ nagare jayaḥ
d uttareṇa tu sārathyaṃ kṛtaṃ nūnaṃ bhaviṣyati
d nimittaṃ kiṃ cid utpannaṃ tarkaś cāpi dṛḍho mama
d yato jānāmi rājendra nānyathā tad bhaviṣyati
d kuravo 'pi mahāvīryā devair api sudurjayāḥ
d sasomavaruṇādityaiḥ sakuberahutāśanaiḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a yatra droṇas tathā bhīṣmo drauṇir vaikartanaḥ kṛpaḥ
b aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadatto jayadrathaḥ
b bhūriśravāḥ śalo bhūrir jalasaṃdhiś ca vīryavān
b duryodhano duṣprasaho duḥśāsanaviviṃśatī
b vṛṣaseno 'śvasenaś ca vātavegasuvarcasau
b bāhlīko bhūrisenaś ca yuyutsuś ca paraṃtapaḥ
b saubalaḥ śakuniś caiva dyumatsenaś ca sālvarāṭ
b anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā nānājanapadeśvarāḥ
b kṛpeṇācāryamukhyena sahitāḥ kuravo nṛpa
b sajjakārmukanistriṃśā rathino rathayūthapāḥ
c duryodhanaś ca rājendra tathānye ca mahārathāḥ
a marudgaṇaiḥ parivṛtaḥ sākṣād api śatakratuḥ
b tad balaṃ na jayet kruddho bhīṣmadroṇādibhir vṛtam
c ko 'nyo bṛhannaḍāyās tān pratiyudhyeta saṃgatān
d yasya bāhubale tulyo na bhūto na bhaviṣyati
d atīva samaraṃ dṛṣṭvā harṣo yasyopajāyate
d yo 'jayat sahitān sarvān surāsuramahoragān
d tādṛśena sahāyena kasmāt sa na vijeṣyate
d kim evaṃ puruṣo loke divi vā bhuvi vidyate
d kiṃ punar mānuṣeṇeha vijitā tv iha vidyate
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d tena saṃkṣubhito rājā dīryamāṇena cetasā
d abravīd vacanaṃ tāta ajānan vai yudhiṣṭhiram
d kaṅka mā mā bravīr vākyaṃ pratikūlaṃ dvijottama
 virāṭa uvāca
a bahuśaḥ pratiṣiddho 'si na ca vācaṃ niyacchasi
c niyantā cen na vidyeta na kaś cid dharmam ācaret
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ prakupito rājā tam akṣeṇāhanad bhṛśam
b tasya takṣakabhogābhaṃ bāhum udyamya dakṣiṇam
b virāṭaḥ prāharat kruddhaḥ karṇam āśritya dakṣiṇam
c mukhe yudhiṣṭhiraṃ kopān naivam ity eva bhartsayan
a balavat pratividdhasya nastaḥ śoṇitam āgamat
b akṣeṇābhihato rājā virāṭena mahīpatiḥ
b tūṣṇīm āsīn mahābāhuḥ kṛṣṇāṃ saṃprekṣya duḥkhitaḥ
b tasya raktotpalanibhaṃ śirasaḥ śoṇitaṃ tadā
b prāvartata mahābāhor abhighātān mahātmanaḥ
c tad aprāptaṃ mahīṃ pārthaḥ pāṇibhyāṃ pratyagṛhṇata
a avaikṣata ca dharmātmā draupadīṃ pārśvataḥ sthitām
c sā veda tam abhiprāyaṃ bhartuś cittavaśānugā
d sā viṣaṇṇā ca bhītā ca kruddhā ca drupadātmajā
d bāṣpaṃ niyamya duḥkhaṃ ca bhartur niḥśreyakāriṇī
d uttarīyeṇa sūkṣmeṇa tūrṇaṃ jagrāha śoṇitas
d nigṛhya raktaṃ vastreṇa sairandhrī duḥkhamohitā
a pūrayitvā ca sauvarṇaṃ pātraṃ kāṃsyam aninditā
b pūrayitvā ca sauvarṇaṃ pānīyasya ca bhājanam
c tac choṇitaṃ pratyagṛhṇād yat prasusrāva pāṇḍavāt
d virāṭo 'syābravīt tatra kim etat kriyatām iti
d sairandhri uvāca
d sairandhri brūhi tattvena mama praśnam aśeṣataḥ
d yad idaṃ śoṇitaṃ rājan kaṅkasya patati kṣitau
d idaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ te kṣipraṃ vinaśyeta na saṃśayaḥ
d na ca dvādaśa varṣāṇi varṣayeta puraṃdaraḥ
d ītayaś ca pravartante na sasyaṃ jāyate kva cit
d aśubhaṃ syāc ca rājendra nṛpasya ca purasya ca
d virāṭaḥ
d sairandhri kim idaṃ raktam uttarīyeṇa gṛhyate
d ko 'tra hetur viśālākṣi tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ
d sairandhrī
d raktabindūni kaṅkasya yāvanti dharaṇīm iyuḥ
d tāvad varṣāṇi rāṣṭre te anāvṛṣṭir bhaviṣyati
d etan nimittaṃ rājendra kaṅkasya rudhiraṃ mayā
d gṛhītam uttarīyeṇa vināśo mā bhavet tava
d janamejayaḥ
d yuddhaṃ tv amānuṣaṃ draṣṭum āgatās tridaśāḥ punaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d kim akurvanta te paścāt kathayasva mamānagha
d vāsavapramukhāḥ sarve devāḥ sarṣipurogamāḥ
d yakṣagandharvasaṃghāś ca gaṇā hy apsarasāṃ tathā
d yuddhaṃ tv amānuṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā kurūṇāṃ phalgunasya ca
d ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca raudram atyugradarśanam
d astrāṇām atha divyānāṃ prayogān atha saṃgrahān
d laghu suṣṭhu ca citraṃ ca kṛtīnāṃ ca prayatnataḥ
d bhīṣmaṃ śāradvataṃ droṇaṃ karṇaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
d jitān anyāṃś ca bhūpālān dṛṣṭvā jagmur divaukasaḥ
d sarve te parituṣṭāś ca praśasya ca muhur muhuḥ
d asaṅgagatinā tena vimānenāśugāminā
d pratijagmur asaṅgena tridivaṃ ca divaukasaḥ
d kuravo 'rjunabāṇaiś ca tāḍitāḥ śaravikṣatāḥ
d kurūn abhimukhā yātāḥ samagrabalavāhanāḥ
d virāṭanagarāc caiva gajāśvarathasaṃkulāḥ
d yodhaiḥ kṣatriyadāyādair balavadbhir adhiṣṭhitāḥ
d virāṭaprahitā senā nagarāc chīghrayāyinī
d uttaraṃ saha sūtena pratyayāt tam ariṃdamam
d tasmiṃs tūryaśatākīrṇe hastyaśvarathasaṃkule
d arjunaḥ
d praharṣaḥ strīkumārāṇāṃ tumulaḥ samapadyata
d nagare tumulaḥ śabdo reṇuś cākramate nabhaḥ
d kiṃ nu khalv apayātās te kuravo nagaraṃ gatāḥ
d te caiva nirjitāsmābhir maheṣvāsāḥ sacetasaḥ
d āmuñca kavacaṃ vīra codayasva ca vājinaḥ
d javenābhiprapadyasva virāṭanagaraṃ prati
d na tāvat talanirghoṣaṃ gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanam
d uttaraḥ
d dhvajaṃ vā darśayiṣyāmi kadā cit svajano bhavet
d senāgram etan mātsyānāṃ gaṇikāś ca svalaṃkṛtāḥ
d kanyā ratheṣu dṛśyante yodhā vividhavāsasaḥ
d uttarām atra paśyāmi sakhībhiḥ parivāritām
d anīkāni prakāśante hastino 'śvāś ca varmitāḥ
d rathinaś ca padātāś ca bahavo na ca śastriṇaḥ
d virāgavasanāḥ sarve saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pratibhāti me
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d na ca me 'tra pratīghātaś cittasya svajane yathā
d tataḥ śīghraṃ samāgamya uttaraḥ svajanaṃ bahu
d parasparam amitraghnaḥ sasvaje taṃ samāgatam
d prītimān puruṣavyāghro harṣayuktaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
d diṣṭyā jayasi bhadraṃ te diṣṭyā sūto bṛhannalā
d uttaraḥ
d diṣṭyā saṃgrāmam āgamya bhayaṃ tava na kiṃ cana
d ajaiṣīd eṣa tāñ jiṣṇuḥ kurūn ekaratho raṇe
d etasya bāhuvīryeṇa yad gāvo vijitā mayā
d kuravo nirjitā yasmāt saṃgrāme 'mitatejasaḥ
d akārṣīd eṣa tat karma devaputropamo yuvā
d eṣa tat puruṣavyāghro vikṣobhya kurumaṇḍalam
d gāvaḥ prasahya vijitā raṇe māṃ cābhyapālayat
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d uttarasya vacaḥ śrutvā śaṃsamānasya cārjunam
d coditā rājaputreṇa jayamaṅgalavādinaḥ
d tato gandhaiś ca mālyaiś ca dhūpaiś caiva susaṃbhṛtaiḥ
d kanyāḥ pārtham amitraghnaṃ kirantyaḥ samapūjayan
a athottaraḥ śubhair gandhair mālyaiś ca vividhais tathā
c avakīryamāṇaḥ saṃhṛṣṭo nagaraṃ svairam āgamat
d bheryaś ca tūryāṇi ca veṇavaś ca
d vicitraveṣaḥ pramadājanaś ca
d purād virāṭasya mahābalasya
d niṣkramya bhūmiṃjayam abhyanandan
d praśasyamānas tu jayena tatra
d putro virāṭasya na hṛṣyati sma
d saṃbhāṣyamāṇas tu janena tena
d so 'ntarmanāḥ pāṇḍavam īkṣamāṇaḥ
d putro virāṭasya tato varāṇi
d vastrāṇy ādāt pāṇḍusutaḥ sakhībhyaḥ
d sabhājayaṃś cāpi samāgatās tā
d diṣṭyājayantac ca balaṃ kumāryaḥ
d bṛhannalāsārathinaṃ praśasya
a sabhājyamānaḥ pauraiś ca strībhir jānapadais tathā
c āsādya bhavanadvāraṃ pitre sa pratyahārayat
a tato dvāḥsthaḥ praviśyaiva virāṭam idam abravīt
a   praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
a vardhayitvā jayāśīrbhir
b dvāḥsthaḥ
b rājan pṛthuyaśās tubhyaṃ jitvā śatrūn samāgataḥ
c bṛhannaḍāsahāyas te putro dvāry uttaraḥ sthitaḥ
d kumāro yodhamukhyaiś ca gaṇikābhiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ
d paurajānapadair yuktaḥ pūjyamāno jayāśiṣā
a tato hṛṣṭo matsyarājaḥ kṣattāram idam abravīt
c praveśyatām ubhau tūrṇaṃ darśanepsur ahaṃ tayoḥ
a kṣattāraṃ kururājas tu śanaiḥ karṇa upājapat
c uttaraḥ praviśatv eko na praveśyā bṛhannaḍā
a etasya hi mahābāho vratam etat samāhitam
c yo mamāṅge vraṇaṃ kuryāc choṇitaṃ vāpi darśayet
e anyatra saṃgrāmagatān na sa jīved asaṃśayam
a na mṛṣyād bhṛśasaṃkruddho māṃ dṛṣṭvaiva saśoṇitam
c virāṭam iha sāmātyaṃ hanyāt sabalavāhanam
d uttaras tv eka evāsmāt praveśyo na bṛhannaḍā
d indraṃ vāpi kuberaṃ vā yamaṃ vā varuṇaṃ tathā
d mama śoṇitakartāraṃ mṛdnīyāt kiṃ punar naram
d kṣaṇamātraṃ tu tatraiva dvāri tiṣṭhatu vīryavān
d iti provāca dharmātmā yudhiṣṭhira udāradhīḥ
d ity uktvā kṣamayā yukto dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d sabhāyāṃ saha mātsyena tūṣṇīm upaviveśa ha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato rājñaḥ suto jyeṣṭhaḥ prāviśat pṛthivīṃjayaḥ
c so 'bhivādya pituḥ pādau dharmarājam apaśyata
d paśyan yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dṛṣṭyā vakrayā caraṇau pituḥ
a sa taṃ rudhirasaṃsiktam anekāgram anāgasam
b hṛdaye 'dahyata tadā mṛtyugrasta ivottaraḥ
b ko vā jigamiṣan mṛtyuṃ kena spṛṣṭaḥ padoragaḥ
b śrotriyo brāhmaṇaśreṣṭha indrāsanaratikṣamaḥ
b vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
b pūjanīyo 'bhivādyaś ca na prabādhyo 'yam īdṛśaḥ
b sa putravacanaṃ śrutvā virāṭo rāṣṭravardhanaḥ
b pratyuvācottaraṃ vākyaṃ sādhvasāddhvastamānasaḥ
b virāṭaḥ
b putra te vijayaṃ śrutvā prahṛṣṭo 'haṃ mahābhuja
b akṣakrīḍanayānena kālakṣepam akāriṣam
b tato 'jayat kurūn sarvān uttaro rāṣṭravardhanaḥ
b ity uktaṃ hi mayā putra neti kaṅko bṛhannalā
b ajayat sā kurūn sarvān iti mām abravīn muhuḥ
b praśaṃsite mayā putra vijaye tava viśrute
b bṛhannalāyā vijayaṃ kaṅkas tu vadate ruṣā
c bhūmāv āsīnam ekānte sairandhryā samupasthitam
a tataḥ papraccha pitaraṃ tvaramāṇa ivottaraḥ
c kenāyaṃ tāḍito rājan kena pāpam idaṃ kṛtam
 virāṭa uvāca
a mayāyaṃ tāḍito jihmo na cāpy etāvad arhati
c praśasyamāne yaḥ śūre tvayi ṣaṇḍhaṃ praśaṃsati
d tāḍito 'yaṃ mayā putra durātmā śatrupakṣakṛt
d bṛhannalāpraśaṃsābhir abhyasūyāmy ahaṃ tadā
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d śrutvā pitur bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ pitaraṃ vākyam abravīt
 uttara uvāca
a akāryaṃ te kṛtaṃ rājan kṣipram eva prasādyatām
c mā tvā brahmaviṣaṃ ghoraṃ samūlam api nirdahet
d yāvan na kṣayam āyāti kulaṃ sarvam aśeṣataḥ
d sphītaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca mātsyānām ayaṃ tāvat pradhakṣyati
d praṇamya pādayor asya daṇḍavat kṣitimaṇḍale
d pragṛhya pādau pāṇibhyām ayaṃ tāvat prasādyatām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa putrasya vacaḥ śrutvā virāṭo rāṣṭravardhanaḥ
c kṣamayām āsa kaunteyaṃ bhasmacchannam ivānalam
a kṣamayantaṃ tu rājānaṃ pāṇḍavaḥ pratyabhāṣata
c ciraṃ kṣāntam idaṃ rājan na manyur vidyate mama
a yadi hy etat pated bhūmau rudhiraṃ mama nastataḥ
c sarāṣṭras tvaṃ mahārāja vinaśyethā na saṃśayaḥ
a na dūṣayāmi te rājan yac ca hanyād adūṣakam
c balavantaṃ mahārāja kṣipraṃ dāruṇam āpnuyāt
d ity uktvā mārjayām āsa śoṇitaṃ sa narādhipaḥ
a śoṇite tu vyatikrānte praviveśa bṛhannaḍā
a   putro rājānam abravīt
a na yuktam iva tasyātra dvāri sthātuṃ mahātmanaḥ
a anuttamabhujasyāsya ślāghyasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ
c abhivādya virāṭaṃ ca kaṅkaṃ cāpy upatiṣṭhata
a kṣamayitvā tu kauravyaṃ raṇād uttaram āgatam
b pariṣvajya dṛḍhaṃ rājā praveśya bhavanottamam
c praśaśaṃsa tato matsyaḥ śṛṇvataḥ savyasācinaḥ
a tvayā dāyādavān asmi kaikeyīnandivardhana
c tvayā me sadṛśaḥ putro na bhūto na bhaviṣyati
a padaṃ padasahasreṇa yaś caran nāparādhnuyāt
b śūraś ca laghuhastaś ca karṇo laghuparākramaḥ
c tena karṇena te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
a manuṣyaloke sakale yasya tulyo na vidyate
c yaḥ samudra ivākṣobhyaḥ kālāgnir iva duḥsahaḥ
e tena bhīṣmeṇa te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
f yasya tad viśrutaṃ loke mahad vratam anuttamam
f pituḥ kṛte kṛtaṃ ghoraṃ brahmacaryaṃ suduṣkaram
f yena yuddhaṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ jāmadagnyena vai saha
f bhīṣmeṇa puruṣavyāghra na ca yuddhe parājitaḥ
f parākramī vai durdharṣo vidvāñ śūro jitendriyaḥ
f kṣiprakārī dṛḍhaṃ vedhī viśrutaḥ sarvakarmasu
f tena te saha bhīṣmeṇa kuruvṛddhena saṃyuge
f yuddham āsīt kathaṃ tāta sarvam etad bravīhi me
f rāmaṃ yo jitavān saṃkhye bhārgavaṃ sumahābalam
f kṣatriyāntakaraṃ vīraṃ tejorāśiṃ durāsadam
f akṣaśiṣyaṃ mahābāhum ajeyaṃ daivatair api
f kālāgnirudrasaṃkāśaṃ katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
a ācāryo vṛṣṇivīrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yo dvijaḥ
c sarvakṣatrasya cācāryaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
e tena droṇena te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
a ācāryaputro yaḥ śūraḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtām api
c aśvatthāmeti vikhyātaḥ kathaṃ tena samāgamaḥ
d sarve caiva mahāvīryā dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥ
d taiś ca vīraiś ca te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
a raṇe yaṃ prekṣya sīdanti hṛtasvā vaṇijo yathā
c kṛpeṇa tena te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
a parvataṃ yo 'bhividhyeta rājaputro maheṣubhiḥ
c duryodhanena te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
d avagāḍhā dviṣanto me sukho vāto 'bhivāti mām
d yas tvaṃ dhanam athājaiṣīḥ kurubhir grastam āhave
d teṣāṃ bhayābhibhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bāhuśālinām
d nūnaṃ prakālya tān sarvāṃs tvayā yuddhe nararṣabhān
d ācchinnaṃ godhanaṃ sarvaṃ śārdūlānām ivāmiṣam
d parigṛhya vinirmuktā labdhavān balavān punaḥ
d uttara kṣatriyaśreṣṭha kenopāyena śātravān
d vinirjayasi saṃgrāme        
d sarve caiva mahāvīryā dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥ
d taiś ca vīraiś ca te tāta katham āsīt samāgamaḥ
 uttara uvāca
a na mayā nirjitā gāvo na mayā nirjitāḥ pare
c kṛtaṃ tu karma tat sarvaṃ devaputreṇa kena cit
a sa hi bhītaṃ dravantaṃ māṃ devaputro nyavārayat
a   bhīṣmadroṇamukhān kurūn
a dṛṣṭvā viṣaṇṇaṃ saṃgrāme
c sa cātiṣṭhad rathopasthe vajrahastanibho yuvā
a tena tā nirjitā gāvas tena te kuravo jitāḥ
c tasya tat karma vīrasya na mayā tāta tat kṛtam
a sa hi śāradvataṃ droṇaṃ droṇaputraṃ ca vīryavān
c sūtaputraṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca cakāra vimukhāñ śaraiḥ
a duryodhanaṃ ca samare sanāgam iva yūthapam
c prabhagnam abravīd bhītaṃ rājaputraṃ mahābalam
a na hāstinapure trāṇaṃ tava paśyāmi kiṃ cana
b na hāstinapure bhogā bhoktuṃ śakyāḥ palāyatā
c vyāyāmena parīpsasva jīvitaṃ kauravātmaja
a na mokṣyase palāyaṃs tvaṃ rājan yuddhe manaḥ kuru
c pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyase jitvā hato vā svargam āpsyasi
a sa nivṛtto naravyāghro muñcan vajranibhāñ śarān
c sacivaiḥ saṃvṛto rājā rathe nāga iva śvasan
a tatra me romaharṣo 'bhūd ūrustambhaś ca māriṣa
c yad abhraghanasaṃkāśam anīkaṃ vyadhamac charaiḥ
a tat praṇudya rathānīkaṃ siṃhasaṃhanano yuvā
c kurūṃs tān prahasan rājan vāsāṃsy apaharad balī
a ekena tena vīreṇa ṣaḍrathāḥ parivāritāḥ
c śārdūleneva mattena mṛgās tṛṇacarā vane
d hayānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ ca dhanuṣmatām
d nihatāni sahasrāṇi bhagnā ca kuruvāhinī
d sūtaputraṃ śarair viddhvā hayān hatvā mahārathaḥ
d devaputrasamaḥ saṃkhye raktaṃ vastraṃ samādade
d caturbhiḥ punar ānarcchad bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtavanaṃ raṇe
d taṃ viddhvātha hayāṃś cāsya śuklaṃ vastraṃ samādade
d duryodhanaṃ ca balavān bāṇair vivyādha saptabhiḥ
d taṃ sa viddhvā hayāṃś cāsya pītaṃ vastraṃ samādade
d droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ ca balavān somadattaṃ jayadratham
d bhūriśravasam indrābhaṃ śakuniṃ ca mahāratham
d tribhis tribhiḥ sa viddhvā tu duḥśāsanamukhān api
d vividhāni ca vastrāṇi mahārhāṇy ājahāra saḥ
d dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ viddhvā tu tathācāryasutaṃ raṇe
d cāpaṃ chitvā vikarṇasya nīle cādatta vāsasī
 virāṭa uvāca
a kva sa vīro mahābāhur devaputro mahāyaśāḥ
c yo me dhanam avājaiṣīt kurubhir grastam āhave
a icchāmi tam ahaṃ draṣṭum arcituṃ ca mahābalam
c yena me tvaṃ ca gāvaś ca rakṣitā devasūnunā
d tasmai dāsyāmi tāṃ putrīṃ grāmāṃś caiva tu hāṭakān
d sphuritaṃ kaṭisūtraṃ ca strīsahasraśatāni ca
 uttara uvāca
a antardhānaṃ gatas tāta devaputraḥ pratāpavān
c sa tu śvo vā paraśvo vā manye prādurbhaviṣyati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam ākhyāyamānaṃ tu channaṃ satreṇa pāṇḍavam
c vasantaṃ tatra nājñāsīd virāṭaḥ pārtham arjunam
a tataḥ pārtho 'bhyanujñāto virāṭena mahātmanā
b saha putreṇa mātsyasya mantrayitvā dhanaṃjayaḥ
b ity evaṃ brūhi rājānaṃ virāṭasya yudhiṣṭhiram
b ity uktvā sahasā pārthaḥ praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ śubham
b āmantrayitvā kaunteyam uttaro vākyam abravīt
b iti rājñaḥ pravakṣyāmi dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c pradadau tāni vāsāṃsi virāṭaduhituḥ svayam
a uttarā tu mahārhāṇi vividhāni tanūni ca
c pratigṛhyābhavat prītā tāni vāsāṃsi bhāminī
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d pradāya vastrāṇi kirīṭamālī
d virāṭagehe muditaḥ sakhibhyaḥ
d kṛtvā mahat karma tad ājimadhye
d didṛkṣayā so 'bhijagāma pārtham
d taṃ prekṣamāṇas tv atha dharmarājaṃ
d papraccha pārtho 'tha sa bhīmasenam
d kiṃ dharmarājo hi yathāpuraṃ māṃ
d mukhaṃ praticchādya na cāha kiṃ cit
d tam evam uktvā pariśaṅkamānaṃ
d dṛṣṭvārjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca rājā
d tatrābravīt tāv abhivīkṣya vīrau
d yudhiṣṭhiras tat parimṛjya raktam
d durātmanā tvayy abhipūjyamāne
d virāṭarājñābhihato 'smi pārtha
d tasmāt prahārād rudhirasya bindūn
d paśyan na ceme pṛthivīṃ spṛśeyuḥ
d iti praticchādya mukhaṃ tato 'haṃ
d manyuṃ niyacchann upaviṣṭa āsam
d kruddhe tu vīre tvayi cāpratīte
d rājā virāṭo na labheta śarma
d ajānatā tena tavaiva vīryaṃ
d channasya satreṇa balaṃ ca pārtha
d idaṃ virāṭena mayi prayuktaṃ
d tvāṃ vīkṣamāṇo na gato 'smi harṣam
d tenāprameyena mahābalena
d tasmiṃs tathokte śamam āśritena
d taṃ bhīmaseno balavān amarṣī
d dhanaṃjayaṃ kruddha uvāca vākyam
d na pārtha nityaṃ kṣamakālam āha
d bṛhaspatir jñānavatāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
d kṣamī hi sarvaiḥ paribhūyate hi
d yathā bhujaṃgo viṣavīryahīnaḥ
d virāṭam adyaiva nihatya śīghraṃ
d saputrapautraṃ sakulaṃ sasainyam
d yokṣyāmahe dharmasutaṃ tu rājye
d adyaiva śīghraṃ tv arir eṣa mātsyaḥ
d anena pāñcālasutātha kṛṣṇā
d upekṣitā kīcakenānuyātā
d tasmād ayaṃ nārhati rājaśabdaṃ

d yad idaṃ māmakaṃ rāṣṭraṃ puraṃ rājyaṃ ca pārthiva
d sadaṇḍakośaṃ visṛje tava bhṛtyo 'smi pārthiva
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d vayaṃ ca sarve sāmātyā bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
d taṃ dharmarājaḥ patitaṃ mahītale
d sabandhuvargaṃ prasamīkṣya pārthivam
d uvāca vākyaṃ paralokadarśanaḥ
d pranaṣṭamanyur gataśokamatsaraḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d na te bhayaṃ pārthiva vidyate mayi
d pratītarūpo 'smy anucintya mānasam
d etat tvayā samyag ihopapāditaṃ
d dvijair amātyaiḥ sadṛśaiś ca paṇḍitaiḥ
d imāṃ ca kanyāṃ samalaṃkṛtāṃ bhṛśaṃ

d kṣāntam etan mahābāho yan māṃ vadasi pārthiva
d na caiva kiṃ cit paśyāmi vikṛtaṃ te narādhipa
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d a tato virāṭaḥ paramābhituṣṭaḥ
d b sametya rājñā samayaṃ cakāra
d c rājyaṃ ca sarvaṃ visasarja tasmai
d d sadaṇḍakośaṃ sapuraṃ mahātmā
d virāṭaḥ
d yac ca vakṣyāmi te sarvaṃ mā śaṅkethā yudhiṣṭhira
d idaṃ sanagaraṃ rāṣṭraṃ savanaṃ savadhūjanam

d rājyaṃ dattvā tu yuṣmabhyaṃ pravrajiṣyāmi kānanam
a uttarāṃ pratigṛhṇātu savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ
c ayaṃ hy aupayiko bhartā tasyāḥ puruṣasattamaḥ

c īkṣitaś cārjuno bhrātrā matsyaṃ vacanam abravīt
d vayaṃ vanāntarāt prāptā na te rājyaṃ gṛhāmahe
d kiṃ tu duryodhanādīnāṃ rājñāṃ rājyaṃ gṛhāmahe
a pratigṛhṇāmy ahaṃ rājan snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ tava
c yuktaś cāvāṃ hi saṃbandho matsyabhāratasattamau
 virāṭa uvāca
a kimarthaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha bhāryāṃ duhitaraṃ mama
c pratigrahītuṃ nemāṃ tvaṃ mayā dattām ihecchasi
 arjuna uvāca
a antaḥpure 'ham uṣitaḥ sadā paśyan sutāṃ tava
c rahasyaṃ ca prakāśaṃ ca viśvastā pitṛvan mayi
a priyo bahumataś cāhaṃ nartako gītakovidaḥ
c ācāryavac ca māṃ nityaṃ manyate duhitā tava
a vayaḥsthayā tayā rājan saha saṃvatsaroṣitaḥ
c atiśaṅkā bhavet sthāne tava lokasya cābhibho
a tasmān nimantraye tvāhaṃ duhituḥ pṛthivīpate
c śuddho jitendriyo dāntas tasyāḥ śuddhiḥ kṛtā mayā
a snuṣāyā duhitur vāpi putre cātmani vā punaḥ
c atra śaṅkāṃ na paśyāmi tena śuddhir bhaviṣyati
a abhiṣaṅgād ahaṃ bhīto mithyācārāt paraṃtapa
c snuṣārtham uttarāṃ rājan pratigṛhṇāmi te sutām
a svasrīyo vāsudevasya sākṣād devaśiśur yathā
c dayitaś cakrahastasya bāla evāstrakovidaḥ
a abhimanyur mahābāhuḥ putro mama viśāṃ pate
c jāmātā tava yukto vai bhartā ca duhitus tava
 virāṭa uvāca
a upapannaṃ kuruśreṣṭhe kuntīputre dhanaṃjaye
c ya evaṃ dharmanityaś ca jātajñānaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
a yatkṛtyaṃ manyase pārtha kriyatāṃ tadanantaram
c sarve kāmāḥ samṛddhā me saṃbandhī yasya me 'rjunaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ bruvati rājendre kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c anvajānāt sa saṃyogaṃ samaye matsyapārthayoḥ
a tato mitreṣu sarveṣu vāsudeve ca bhārata
c preṣayām āsa kaunteyo virāṭaś ca mahīpatiḥ
d pratigṛhya snuṣārthaṃ vai darśayan vṛttam ātmanaḥ
d śīlaśaucasamācāraṃ lokasyāvedya phalgunaḥ
d loke vikhyāpya māhātmyaṃ yaśaś ca sa paraṃtapaḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d kṛtārthaḥ śucir avyagras tuṣṭimān abhavat tadā
d rājan prīto 'smi bhadraṃ te sakhā me 'si paraṃtapa
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d sukham adhyuṣitāḥ sarve ajñātās tvayi pārthiva
d virāṭanagare rājā dharmātmā saṃśitavrataḥ
d pūjitaś cābhiṣiktaś ca ratnaiś ca śataśaś citaḥ
d tathā bruvantaṃ prasamīkṣya rājā
d paraṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ svajanena tena
d snehāt pariṣvajya nṛpo bhujābhyāṃ
d dadau tam arthaṃ kurupuṃgavānām
d yuddhāt prayātāḥ kuravo hi mārge
d sametya sarve hitam eva tatra
d ācāryaputraḥ śakuniś ca rājā
d duryodhanaḥ sūtaputraś ca karṇaḥ
d saṃmantrya rājan sahitāḥ samarthāḥ
d samādiśan dūtam atho samagrāḥ
d yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpi susaṃprahṛṣṭo
d duryodhanād dūtam apaśyad āgatam
d sa cābravīd dharmarājaṃ sametya
d yudhiṣṭhiraṃ pāṇḍavam ugravīryam
d dhanaṃjayenāsi punar vanāya
d pravrājitaḥ samaye tiṣṭha pārtha
d trayodaśe hy eṣa kirīṭamālī
d saṃvatsare pāṇḍaveyo 'dya dṛṣṭaḥ
d tato 'bravīd dharmasutaḥ prahasya
d kṣipraṃ gatvā brūhi suyodhanaṃ tam
d pitāmahaḥ śāṃtanavo bravītu
d yady atra pūrṇo 'dya trayodaśo naḥ
d saṃvatsarānte tu dhanaṃjayena
d viṣphāritaṃ gāṇḍivam ājimadhye
d pūrṇo na pūrṇo na iti bravītu
d yad asya satyaṃ mama tat pramāṇam
d tenaivam uktaḥ sa nivṛtya dūto
d duryodhanaṃ prāpya śaśaṃsa tattvam
d sametya dūtena sa rājaputro
d duryodhano mantrayām āsa tatra
d bhīṣmeṇa karṇena kṛpeṇa caiva
d droṇena bhūriśravasā ca sārdham
d saṃmantrya rātrau bahubhiḥ suhṛdbhir
d bhīṣmo 'bravīd dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahātmā
d tīrṇapratijñena dhanaṃjayena
d viṣphāritaṃ gāṇḍivam ājimadhye
d te dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samayaṃ niśamya
d tīrṇapratijñasya dhanaṃjayasya
d saṃcintya sarve sahitāḥ suhṛdbhiḥ
d sapārthivāḥ svāni gṛhāṇi jagmuḥ
a tatas trayodaśe varṣe nivṛtte pañca pāṇḍavāḥ
c upaplavye virāṭasya samapadyanta sarvaśaḥ
d virāṭena saputreṇa pūjyamānāḥ samāvasan
d dūtān mitreṣu sarveṣu jñātisaṃbandhikeṣv api
d preṣayām āsa kaunteyo virāṭaś ca mahīpatiḥ
a tasmin vasaṃś ca bībhatsur ānināya janārdanam
c ānartebhyo 'pi dāśārhān abhimanyuṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
d abhimanyuṃ samādāya rāmeṇa sahitas tadā
d sarvayādavamukhyaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ paravīrahā
d śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair virāṭanagaraṃ yayau
a kāśirājaś ca śaibyaś ca prīyamāṇau yudhiṣṭhire
c akṣauhiṇībhyāṃ sahitāv āgatau pṛthivīpate
a akṣauhiṇyā ca tejasvī yajñaseno mahābalaḥ
b saha putrair mahāvīryair dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍibhiḥ
b upaplāvyaṃ yayuḥ śīghraṃ pāṇḍavārthe mahābalāḥ
b tataḥ śatasahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
b samīpam abhivartante yodhā yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ balam
b samudram iva gharmānte srotaḥśreṣṭhāḥ pṛthak pṛthak
c draupadyāś ca sutā vīrāḥ śikhaṇḍī cāparājitaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca durdharṣaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c samastākṣauhiṇīpālā yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ
e sarve śastrāstrasaṃpannāḥ sarve śūrās tanutyajaḥ
a tān āgatān abhiprekṣya matsyo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
b pūjayām āsa vidhivat sabhṛtyabalavāhanān
c prīto 'bhavad duhitaraṃ dattvā tām abhimanyave
a tataḥ pratyupayāteṣu pārthiveṣu tatas tataḥ
c tatrāgamad vāsudevo vanamālī halāyudhaḥ
d te dūtā dvārakām etya dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇīn mahārathān
d ūcuḥ prāñjalayas tatra pāṇḍavānāṃ mataṃ tadā
d tasmin kāle niśamyātha dūtavākyaṃ janārdanaḥ
d dayitaṃ svastriyaṃ putraṃ subhadrāyāḥ sumānitam
e kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyo yuyudhānaś ca sātyakiḥ
a anādhṛṣṭis tathākrūraḥ sāmbo niśaṭha eva ca
b anye 'pi bahavaḥ śūrā nṛpāḥ prītiparāyaṇāḥ
b bibhyan ke 'pi samājagmuḥ pāṇḍavebhyo hitaiṣiṇaḥ
b pradyumnaś ca mahābāhur ulmukaś ca mahābalaḥ
c abhimanyum upādāya saha mātrā paraṃtapāḥ
d kṛṣṇena sahitāḥ sarve pāṇḍavān draṣṭum āgatāḥ
a indrasenādayaś caiva rathais taiḥ susamāhitaiḥ

d vāsudevaṃ tathāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍusutās tadā
d mātsyena sahitāḥ sarve pratyudyātā janārdanam
d śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair maṅgalyaiś ca janārdanam
d vavandur muditāḥ sarve pādayos tasya pāṇḍavāḥ
d pāṇḍavāḥ
d mātsyena sahitāḥ sarve ānandāśrupariplutāḥ
d evaṃ tava prasādād vai varṣāṇy etāni sarvaśaḥ

d uṣitāḥ smo jagannātha tvaṃ nātho no janārdana

d rakṣasva devadeveśa tvām adya śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ

d virāṭasya sahāyāṃs tān sarvayādavasavṛtaḥ

d mā śokaṃ kuru kalyāṇi dhārtarāṣṭrān samāhitān

d ity uktvā tāṃ visṛjyātha prīyamāṇo yudhiṣṭhiram
d anvāsta vṛṣṇiśārdūlaḥ saha vṛṣṇyandhakais tadā
a pāribarhaṃ dadau kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c striyo ratnāni vāsāṃsi pṛthak pṛthag anekaśaḥ
d rājāno rājaputrāś ca nivṛtte samaye tadā
d yathārhaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhe hy avartantābhipūjitāḥ
d āsan prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ pāribarhaṃ dadus tadā
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d teṣu tatra sameteṣu rājāno vṛṣṇibhiḥ saha

d vastrāṇi ca mahārhāṇi maṇīnāṃ nicayāni ca

a tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca gomukhāḍambarās tathā

d draupady antaḥpure caiva virāṭasya gṛhe striyaḥ

d bhṛṅgāraṃ tu samādāya sauvarṇaṃ jalapūritam
d pārthasya haste sahasā satām indīvarekṣaṇām
d snuṣārthaṃ prākṣipad dvāri virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
a tāṃ pratyagṛhṇāt kaunteyaḥ sutasyārthe dhanaṃjayaḥ
c saubhadrasyānavadyāṅgīṃ virāṭatanayāṃ tadā

d drupadaś ca virāṭaś ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahāyaśāḥ
d kāśirājaś ca śaibyaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca sātyakiḥ
d saptaite 'kṣauhiṇīpālā yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ

a pratigṛhya ca tāṃ pārthaḥ puraskṛtya janārdanam
c vivāhaṃ kārayām āsa saubhadrasya mahātmanaḥ
d dhaumyaḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto bhānumān iva raśmibhiḥ
d tato vivāho vavṛdhe sphītaḥ sarvaguṇānvitaḥ
d saubhadrasyādbhutaś caiva pitus tava pitus tadā
d dhaumyaḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto juhāvāgnau vidhānataḥ
d agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kurvan saubhadraḥ pāṇim agrahīt
d tataḥ pārthāya saṃhṛṣṭo mātsyarājo dhanaṃ mahat
a tasmai sapta sahasrāṇi hayānāṃ vātaraṃhasām
c dve ca nāgaśate mukhye prādād bahu dhanaṃ tadā
d prādān matsyapatir hṛṣṭaḥ kanyādhanam anuttamam
d pāribarhaṃ ca pārthasya pradadau matsyapuṃgavaḥ
d kṛṣṇena saha kaunteyaḥ pratyagṛhṇāt prabhūtavat
d hutvā samyak samiddhāgnim arcayitvā dvijanmanaḥ
d rājyaṃ balaṃ ca kośaṃ ca sarvam ātmānam eva ca
d nyavedayan pāṇḍavebhyo virāṭaḥ prītimāṃs tadā
a kṛte vivāhe tu tadā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c brāhmaṇebhyo dadau vittaṃ yad upāharad acyutaḥ
a gosahasrāṇi ratnāni vastrāṇi vividhāni ca
c bhūṣaṇāni ca mukhyāni yānāni śayanāni ca
d paṭṭavāsāṃsi citrāṇi dāsīdāsān bahūn dadau
d nāgarān prītibhir divyais tarpayām āsa bhūpatiḥ
d bhojanāni ca hṛdyāni pānāni vividhāni ca
a tan mahotsavasaṃkāśaṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanāvṛtam
c nagaraṃ matsyarājasya śuśubhe bharatarṣabha
d purohitair amātyaiś ca paurair jānapadair api
d virāṭanṛpatiḥ śrīmān saubhadrāyābhimanyave
d tāṃ sutām uttarāṃ dattvā mumude paramaṃ tadā

d purād bahir upaplāvya ūṣuḥ pāṇḍusutās tadā
d janamejayaḥ
d vṛtte vivāhe hṛṣṭātmā yad uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tat sarvaṃ kathayasveha kṛtavanto yad uttaram
d caturtham etad vipulaṃ vairāṭaṃ parvavarṇanam
d atrāpi parisaṃkhyātā adhyāyānāṃ mahātmanā
d saptaṣaṣṭir atho pūrṇā ślokānām api me śṛṇu
d ślokānāṃ dve sahasre tu trīṇi ślokaśatāni ca
d parvaṇy asmin samākhyātaṃ saṃkhyānaṃ paramarṣiṇā
d virāṭaparve deyāni vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca
d kṛtvā vivāhaṃ tu kurupravīrās
d tadābhimanyor muditasya pakṣāḥ
d viśramya catvāry uṣasaḥ pratītāḥ
d sabhāṃ virāṭasya tato 'bhijagmuḥ
